śṛṅgāra-vīra-sauhārdaṃ maugdhya-vaiyātya-saurabham । lāsya-tāṇḍava-saujanyaṃ dāmpatyaṃ tad bhajāmahe ।। vīṇāṅkita-karāṃ vande vānīm eṇīdṛśaṃ sadā । sadānanda-mayīṃ devīṃ sarojāsana-vallabhām ।।
asti kiñcit paraṃ vastu paramānanda-kandalam । kamalākuca-kāṭhinya-kutūhali-bhujāntaram ।। tasya pādāmbujāj jāto varṇo vigata-kalmaṣaḥ । yasya sodaratāṃ prāptaṃ bhagīratha-tapaḥ-phalam ।।
tatra recarlavaṃśābdhi-śarad-rākā-sudhākaraḥ । kalā-nidhir udāra-śrīr āsīd dācaya-nāyakaḥ ।। yasyāsi-dhārā-mārgeṇa durgeṇāpi raṇāṅgaṇe । pāṇḍya-rāja-gajānīkāj jaya-lakṣmīr upāgatā ।।
aṅga-nārāyaṇe yasmin bhavati śrīr atisthirā । bhūr abhūt kariṇī vaśyā duṣṭa-rāja-gajāṅkuśe ।। tasya bhāryā mahābhāgyā viṣṇoḥ śrīr iva viśrutā । pocamāmbā guṇodārā jātā tāmarasānvayāt ।।
putrās trayas trāsita-vairi-vīrāḥ । vīrāgraṇī reca-mahī-patiś ca ।। kalāv eka-pado dharmo yair ebhiś caraṇair iva । sampūrṇa-padatāṃ prāpya nākāṅkṣati kṛtaṃ yugam ।।
tatra siṃha-mahīpāle pālayaty akhilāṃ mahīm । namatām unnatiś citraṃ rājñām anamatāṃ natiḥ ।। vītāpāyam anekaśo vidadhatā brahma-pratiṣṭhāpanam । nirmāṇātiśaya-prayāsa-garima-vyāsaṅgini brahmaṇi ।।
dṛṣṭvā yadīyāṃ trasatām arīṇām । mānoṣmaṇām ātanute praśāntim ।। prāpto vīra-guru-prathāṃ pṛthutarāṃ vīrasya mudrākarīm । putraṃ nāgayanāyakaṃ vasumatī-vīraika-cūḍāmaṇim ।।
so' yaṃ siṃha-mahīpālo vasudeva iti sphuṭam । ananta-mādhavau yasya tanūjau loka-rakṣakau ।। dig-antarāla-prathita-pratāpaḥ । tanūbhavā veda-girīndra-mukhyāḥ ।।
aprota-bhāvād anapota-saṃjñām । ananta-sajñāṃ ca mahīdharatvam ।। pradyumnas tanayo' p pautra-nivaho yasyāniruddhādayaḥ । dhatte cāru-sudarśana-śriyam asau satvātma-hastāmbuje ।।
bahu-soma-sutaṃ kṛtvā bhūlokaṃ yatra rakṣati । eka-soma-sutaṃ rakṣan svarlokaṃ lajjate hariḥ ।। bhuja-bala-bhīme' rigāya-gobāle । jagatāṃ jāgarti nitya-kalyāṇam ।।
hemācalaṃ hasta-gataṃ vidhāya । śrī-parvataṃ sarva-janāṅghri-gamyam ।। saṅkhyo' py abhagnātma-gati-kramo' pi । dadhāti somānvaya-bhārgavāṅkam ।।
khaḍge khaḍge phalita-vapuṣaṃ yaṃ purastād vilokya । saṃmanyante sphuṭam avitathaṃ khaḍga-nārāyaṇāṅkam ।। annamāmbeti vikhyātā tasyāsīd dharaṇī-pateḥ । devī śivā śivasyeva rājamauler mahojjvalā ।।
śatrughnaṃ śrutakīrtir yā subhadrā yaśasārjunam । ānandayati bhartāraṃ śyāmā rājānam ujjvalam ।। tayor abhūtāṃ putrau dvāv ādyo veda-girīśvaraḥ । dvitīyas tv advitīyo' sau yaśasā siṃha-bhūpatiḥ ।।
atha śrī-siṃha-bhūpālo dīrghāyur vasudhām imām । nijāṃsa-pīṭhe nirvyājaṃ kurute supratiṣṭhitām ।। bali-dhvaṃsī bāṇaḥ para-puram anekaṃ ca viṣayaḥ । maheśo' yaṃ siṃha-kṣitipa iti yaṃ jalpati janaḥ ।।
tṛṇa-caraṇaṃ nija-purāc ca niḥsaraṇam । paricaraṇaṃ vā virodhināṃ śaraṇam ।। kalāḥ kāntāḥ puṣṇan dadhad api ca jaivātṛka-kathām । tathā cakrānandān api ca kamalollāsa-suṣamām ।।
svātyām eva hi śuktikāsu dadhate muktāni muktātmatām । māṇikyāni mahāmbarāṇi bahuśo dhāmāni hemāni ca ।। padam apadaṃ nijam avetya ripu-bhūpāḥ । vinamanti padāravinda-pīṭhāntam ।।
tvat-sāmanta-mahī-bhujaḥ karuṇayā te rakṣaṇīyā iti । manye yasya dṛg-antayoḥ parisaraṃ sā kāma-dhenuḥ śritā ।। ity antaḥ-pura-pṛcchayā yad ariṣu prāpteṣu lajjā-vaśam । gaṇḍāndolita-karṇa-kuṇḍala-harin-māṇikya-varṇāṅkurāḥ ।।
candana-santāna-kalpa-maṇi-sadṛśaiḥ । veda-giri-svāmi-māda-dāmaya-saṃjñaiḥ ।। anitara-jana-sulabha-dāna-muditair bhuvi yaḥ । rājakarāra-cita-sukamalollāsaḥ ।।
ekasyāgrajam ātma-rūpa-vibhave cāpe dvayor agrajam । satyoktau caturagrajaṃ vitaraṇe kiṃ cāpi pañcāgrajam ।। majjanti pratipakṣa-bhūmi-patayaḥ śauryoṣma-santāpitāḥ । prabhraśyat-kuca-kuṅkumāḥ parigalan-netrānta-kālāñjanāḥ ।।
dayite vallabha-rāya-pūrṇa-candre । kamalānām abhivardhanaṃ tu citram ।। etair anyaiś ca tanayaiḥ so' yaṃ siṃha-mahīpatiḥ । ṣaḍbhiḥ pratiṣṭhām ayate svāmīvāṅgaiḥ susaṅgataiḥ ।।
adhyāsta vaṃśa-krama-rājadhānīm । nyāyānurodhād anusandadhānajñāḥ ।। vindhya-śrī-śaila-madhya-kṣmā-maṇḍalaṃ pālayan sutaiḥ । vaṃśa-pravartakair arthān bhuṅkte bhoga-purandaraḥ ।।
kāṭhinyaṃ kuca-maṇḍale taralatā netrāñcale subhruvām । kauṭilyaṃ cikureṣu kiṃ ca kṛśatā madhye paraṃ badhyate ।। so' haṃ kalyāṇa-rūpasya varṇotkarṣaika-kāraṇam । vidvat-prasādanā-hetor vakṣye nāṭyasya lakṣaṇam ।।
purā purandarādyās te praṇamya caturānanam । kṛtāñjali-puṭā bhūtvā papracchuḥ sarva-vedinam ।। bhagavan śrotum icchāmaḥ śrāvyaṃ dṛśyaṃ manoharam । dharmyaṃ yaśasyam arthyaṃ ca sarva-śilpa-pradarśanam ।।
paraṃ pañcamam āmnāyaṃ sarva-varṇādhikārikam । iti pṛṣṭaḥ sa tair brahmā sarva-vedān anusmaran ।। tebhyaś ca sāram ādāya nāṭya-vedam athāsṛjat । adhyāpya bharatācāryaṃ prajāpatir abhāṣata ।।
saha putrair imaṃ vedaṃ prayogeṇa prakāśaya । iti tena niyuktas tu bharataḥ saha sūnubhiḥ ।। prāyojayat sudharmāyām indrasyāgre' psaro-gaṇaiḥ । sarva-lokopakārāya nāṭya-śāstraṃ ca nirmame ।।
tathā tad-anusāreṇa śāṇḍilyaḥ kohalo' pi ca । dattilaś ca mataṅgaś ca ye cānye tat-tanūdbhavāḥ ।। granthān nānā-vidhāṃś cakruḥ prakhyātās te mahītale । teṣām atigabhīratvād viprakīrṇa-kramatvataḥ ।।
sampradāyasya vicchedāt tad-vidāṃ viralatvataḥ । prāyo virala-sañcārā nāṭya-paddhatir asphuṭā ।। tasmād asmat-prayatno' yaṃ tat-prakāśana-lakṣaṇaḥ । sāraika-grāhiṇāṃ cittam ānandayati dhīmatām ।।
jyotsnā kiṃ na cakora-pāraṇa-kṛte tat-kāla-saṃśobhinī । tat sampraty api mādṛśām api vacaḥ syād eva samprītaye ।। svaccha-svādu-rasādhāro vastu-cchāyā-manoharaḥ । sevyaḥ suvarṇa-nidhivan nāṭya-mārgaḥ sa-nāyakaḥ ।।
sāttvikādyair abhinayaiḥ prekṣakāṇāṃ yato bhavet । naṭe nāyaka-tādātmya-buddhis tan nāṭyam ucyate ।। rasotkarṣo hi nāṭyasya prāṇās tat sa nirūpyate । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca sāttvikair vyabhicāribhiḥ ।।
ānīyamānaḥ svādutvaṃ sthāyī bhāvo rasaḥ smṛtaḥ । tatra jñeyo vibhāvas tu rasa-jñāpana-kāraṇam ।। budhair jñeyo' yam ālamba uddīpana iti dvidhā । ādhāra-viṣayatvābhyāṃ nāyako nāyikāpi ca ।।
ālambanaṃ mataṃ tatra nāyako guṇavān pumān । tad-guṇās tu mahā-bhāgyam audāryaṃ sthairya-dakṣate ।। aujjvalyaṃ dhārmikatvaṃ ca kulīnatvaṃ ca vāgmitā । kṛtajñatvaṃ nayajñatvaṃ śucitā māna-śālitā ।।
tejasvitā kalāvattvaṃ prajā-rañjakatādayaḥ । ete sādhāraṇāḥ proktāḥ nāyakasya guṇā budhaiḥ ।। sarvātiśāyi-rājyatvaṃ mahābhāgyam udāhṛtam ।। athā- sasāgarāṃ sāgara-dhīra-cetāḥ ।
purārgalādīrgha-bhujo bubhoja ।। yad-viśrāṇana-śīlatvaṃ tad audāryaṃ budhā viduḥ ।। dvāv apy abhūtām abhinandya-sattvau । nṛpo' rthi-kāmād adhika-pradaś ca ।।
vyāpāraṃ phala-paryantaṃ sthairym āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।। athā- sthira-karmā virarāma karmaṇaḥ । sthira-dhīrā paramātma-darśanāt ।। duṣkare kṣipra-kāritvaṃ dakṣatāṃ paricakṣate ।।
vāladhiṃ trātum āvṛtya camareṇārpite gale । patantam iṣum anyena sa kṛpālur akhaṇḍayat ।। Some MSS have the following example sa dakṣiṇaṃ tūṇa-mukhena vāmaṃ । vyāpārayan hastam alakṣyatājau । ākarṇa-kṛṣṭā sakṛd asya yoddhum । aurvīva bāṇān suṣuve ripu-ghnān ।। aujjvalyaṃ nayanānanda-kāritvaṃ kathyate budhaiḥ ।। athā-
nāryo na jagmur viṣayāntarāṇi । sarvātmanā cakṣur iva praviṣṭā ।। dharma-pravaṇa-cittatvaṃ dhārmikatvam itīryate ।। sthityai daṇḍayato daṇḍyān pariṇetuḥ prasūtaye ।
apy artha-kāmau tasyāstāṃ dharma eva manīṣiṇaḥ ।। kule mahati sambhūtiḥ kulīnatvam udāhṛtam ।। athā- sūryācandramasau yasya mātāmaha-pitāmahau । svayaṃ vṛtaḥ patir dvābhyāṃ urvaśyā ca bhuvā ca yaḥ ।।
vāgmitā tu budhair uktā samayocita-bhāṣitā ।। vijayante dviṣato yad asya pakṣyāḥ । pratiśabdo' pi harer bhinatti nāgān ।। kṛtānām upakārāṇām abhjñatvaṃ kṛtajñatā ।। athā-
ekasyaivopakārasya prāṇān dāsyāmi te kape । pratyahaṃ kriyamāṇasya śeṣasya ṛṇino vayam ।। sāmādy-upāya-cāturyaṃ nayajñatvam udāhṛtam ।। vibhajya samyag viniyoga-sat-kriyāḥ ।
upetya saṅgharṣam ivārtha-sampadaḥ ।। antaḥ-karaṇa-śuddhir yā śucitā sā prakīrtitā ।। athā- kiṃ vā mad-abhyāgama-kāraṇaṃ te । manaḥ para-strī-vimukha-pravṛtti ।।
akārpaṇya-sahiṣṇutvaṃ kathitā māna-śālitā ।। krīḍā-kṛtta-punaḥ-prarūḍha-śiraso vīrasya lipsor varam । tvaṃ vṛṇv ity abhito mukhāni sa daśagrīvaḥ kathaṃ varṇyatām ।। tejasvitvam avajñāder asahiṣṇutvam ucyate ।। athā-
vīraḥ krauñcasya bhedī kṛta-dharaṇi-talāpūrva-haṃsāvatāraḥ । tvāṃ pṛcchan jāmadagnyaḥ sva-guru-hara-dhanur bhaṅga-roṣād upaiti ।। kalāvattvaṃ nigaditaṃ sarva-vidyāsu kauśalam ।। kalā-kalāpasya sa tāratamyam ।
viveda hemno nikaṣāśmanīva ।। rañjakatvaṃ tu sakala-cittāhlādana-kāritā ।। athā- aham eva mato mahīpater iti sarvaḥ prakṛtiṣv acintayat । udadher iva nimnagāśateṣv abhavan nāsya vimānanā kvacit ।।
uktair guṇaiś ca sakalair yuktaḥ syād uttamo netā । madhyaḥ katipaya-hīno bahu-guṇa-hīno' dhamo nāma ।। netā caturvidho' sau dhīrodāttaś ca dhīra-lalitaś ca । dhīra-praśānta-nāmā tataś ca dhīroddhataḥ khyātaḥ ।।
dayāvān atigambhīro vinītaḥ sattva-sāravān । dṛḍha-vratas titikṣāvān ātmaślāghāparāṅmukhaḥ । nigūḍhāhaṅkṛtir dhīrair dhīrodātta udāhṛtaḥ ।। dayātiśaya-śālitvaṃ dayāvattvam udāhṛtam ।। athā-
nikṣepitāḥ ketuṣu pārthivānām । na jīvitaṃ vaḥ kṛpayeti varṇāḥ ।। gāmbhīryam avikāraḥ syāt saty api kṣobha-kāraṇe ।। dadhato maṅgala-kṣaume vasānasya ca balkale ।
dadṛśur vismitās tasya mukha-rāgaṃ samaṃ janāḥ ।। rabhasād rathād avatarītum icchataḥ । vinayaṃ viśeṣayati sambhrameṇa saḥ ।। utsmāyitvā mahābāhuḥ prekṣya cāsthi mahābalaḥ ।
pādāṅguṣṭhena cikṣepa sampūrṇaṃ daśa-yojanam ।। tam aśakyam apākraṣṭuṃ nideśāt svargiṇaḥ pituḥ । yayāce pāduke paścāt kartuṃ rājyādhidevate ।। śapamānāya na cedi-bhūbhuje ।
na hi gomāyu-rutāni kesarī ।। tasya saṃstūyamānasya caritārthais tapasvibhiḥ । śuśubhe vikramodagraṃ vrīḍayāvanataṃ śiraḥ ।। yad vīreṇa bhavādṛśena vadatā triḥ sapta-kṛtvo jayam ।
tat krodhād virama prasīda bhagavan jātyaiva pūjyo' si naḥ ।। niścinto dhīra-lalitas taruṇo vanitā-vaśaḥ ।। athā- kāścana svayam avartayat samāḥ । strī-vidheya-nava-yauvano' bhavat ।।
śama-prakṛtikaḥ kleśa-sahiṣṇuś ca vivecakaḥ । lalitādi-guṇopeto vipro vā sacivo vaṇik । dhīra-śāntaś cārudatta-mādhavādir udāhṛtaḥ ।। lalita-vikaṭa-nyāsaḥ śrīmān mṛgāṅka-nibhānanaḥ ।
pravigalad-asṛk-paṅkaḥ pāṇir lalan nara-jāṅgalaḥ ।। mātsaryavān ahaṅkārī māyāvī roṣaṇaś calaḥ । vikatthano bhārgavādir dhīroddhata udāhṛtaḥ ।। tena vyārujatā dhanur bhagavato devād bhavānī-pateḥ । tat-putras tu madāndha-tāraka-vadhād viśvasya dattotsavaḥ
skandaḥ skanda iva priyo' ham athavā śiṣyaḥ kathaṃ vismṛtaḥ ।। ete ca nāyakāḥ sarva-rasa-sādhāraṇāḥ smṛtāḥ । śṛṅgārāpekṣayā teṣāṃ traividhyaṃ kathyate budhaiḥ ।। patiś copapatiś caiva vaiśikaś ceti bhedataḥ ।
patis tu vidhinā pāṇigrāhakaḥ kathyate budhaiḥ ।। kanyāṃ kulasya sthitaye sthitijñaḥ । ātmānurūpāṃ vidhinopayeme ।। caturdhā so' pi kathito vṛttyā kāvya-vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।
anukūlaḥ śaṭho dhṛṣṭo dakṣiṇaś ceti bhedataḥ ।। anukūlas tv eka-jāniḥ ।। tasyā eva pratikṛti-sakho yat kratūnājahāra । sā durvāraṃ katham api parityāga-duḥkhaṃ viṣehe ।।
saha devyā vijahāra suprajāḥ । marutāṃ pālayiteva nandane ।। nanu so' ham eva yam anandayat purā । tava mūrtimān iva mahotsavaḥ karaḥ ।।
nidrāccheda-vivartaneṣv abhimukhaṃ nādyāsi sambhāvitā । doṣaṃ paśyasi kaṃ priye parijanopālambha-yogye mayi ।। śaṭho gūḍhāparādha-kṛt ।। pratyabhaitsur avadanty eva tam ।
krodha-bhinna-valayir vivartanaiḥ ।। dhṛṣṭo vyaktānya-yuvatī-bhoga-lakṣmāpi nirbhayaḥ ।। dhatte bhūṣaṇam ardha-candram amalaṃ candre na kiṃ kālimā । bhāgyaṃ draṣṭum anīśayaiva bhavataḥ kāntāparāddhaṃ mayā ।।
nāyikāsv apy anekāsu tulyo dakṣiṇa ucyate ।। athā- dyūte rātrir iyaṃ jitā kamalayā devī prasādyādya ca । devenāpratipatti-mūḍha-manasā dvitrāḥ sthitaṃ nāḍikāḥ ।। laṅghitācārayā yas tu vināpi vidhinā striyā ।
saṅketaṃ nīyate prokto budhair upapatis tu saḥ ।। athā- śvaśrūr iṅgita-daivataṃ nayanayor ūhāliho yātaraḥ । vaidagdhī-racanā-prapañca-rasika vyartho' yam atra śramaḥ ।। dākṣiṇyam ānukūlyaṃ ca dhārṣṭyaṃ cāniyatatvataḥ ।
nocitānyasya śāṭhyaṃ syād anya-cittatva-sambhavāt ।। śaṭhopapatir, yathā- majjhaṇṇe jaṇa-suṇṇe kariṇīe bhakkhidesu kamalesu । avisesaṇṇa kahaṃ bia gado si saṇa-bāḍḍiaṃ daṭṭhuṃ ।। [madhyāhne jana-śūnye kariṇyā bhakṣiteṣu kamaleṣu ।
aviśeṣajña katham iva gato' si śaṇa-vāṭikāṃ draṣṭum ।।] atra kayācit svairiṇyāṃ mayi saṅketaṃ gatāyāṃ tvaṃ tu śāṇa-vāṭikāyāṃ kathāpi rantuṃ gato' sīti vyaṅgyārthenānyāsaṅga-sūcanād ayaṃ śaṭhopapatiḥ । rūpavān śīla-sampannaḥ śāstrajñaḥ priya-darśanaḥ । kulīno matimān śūro ramya-veṣa-yuto yuvā ।।
adīnaḥ surabhis tyāgī sahanaḥ priya-bhāṣaṇaḥ । śaṅka-vihīno mānī ca deśa-kāla-vibhāga-vit ।। dākṣya-cāturya-mādhurya-saubhāgyādibhir anvitaḥ । veśyopabhoga-rasiko yo bhavet sa tu vaiśikaḥ ।।
kalakaṇṭhādiko lakṣyo bhāṇādāv eva vaiśikaḥ । sa tridhā kathyate jyeṣṭha-madhya-nīca-vibhedataḥ ।। eṣāṃ lakṣaṇāni bhāva-prakāśikāyām uktāni । yathā- asaṅgo' pi svabhāvena saktavac ceṣṭate muhuḥ । tyāgī svabhāva-madhuraḥ sama-duḥkha-sukhaḥ śuciḥ ।।
kāma-tantreṣu nipuṇaḥ kruddhānunaya-kovidaḥ । sphurite cādhare kiṃcid dayitāyā virajyati ।। upacāra-paro hy eṣa uttamaḥ kathyate budhaiḥ । vyalīka-mātre dṛṣṭe' syā na kupyati na rajyati ।।
dadāti kāle kāle ca bhāvaṃ gṛhṇāti bhāvataḥ । sarvārthair api madhya-sthas tām evopacaret punaḥ ।। dṛṣṭe doṣe virajyeta sa bhaven madhyamaḥ pumān । kāma-tantreṣu nirlajjaḥ karkaśo rati-keliṣu ।।
avijñāta-bhayāmarṣaḥ kṛtyākṛtya-vimūḍha-dhīḥ । mūrkhaḥ prasakta-bhāvaś ca viraktāyām api striyām ।। mitrair nivāryamāṇo' pi pāruṣyaṃ prāpito' pi ca । anya-sneha-parāvṛttāṃ saṃkrānta-ramaṇām api ।
striyaṃ kāmayate yas tu so' dhamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। iti । atha śṛṅgāra-netṝṇāṃ sāhāyya-karaṇocitāḥ । nirūpyante pīṭhamarda-viṭa-ceṭa-vidūṣakāḥ ।। nāyakānucaro bhaktaḥ kiñcid ūnaś ca tad-guṇaiḥ ।
pīṭhamarda iti khyātaḥ kupita-strī-prasādakaḥ ।। kāma-tantra-kalā-vedī viṭa ity abhidhīyate । sandhāna-kuśalaś ceṭaḥ kalahaṃsādiko mataḥ । vikṛtāṅga-vaco-veṣair hāsya-kārī vidūṣakaḥ ।।
deśa-kālajñatā bhāṣā-mādhuryaṃ ca vidagdhatā । protsāhane kuśalatā yathokta-kathanaṃ tathā । nigūḍha-mantratety ādyāḥ sahāyānāṃ guṇā matāḥ ।। netṛ-sādhāraṇa-guṇair upetā nāyikā matā ।
svakīyā parakīyā ca sāmānyā ceti sā tridhā ।। sampat-kāle vipat-kāle yā na muñcati vallabham । śīlārjava-guṇopetā sā svakīyā kathitā budhaiḥ ।। kiṃ vā me sasureṇa vāsava-mahā-siṃhāsaṇaddhāsiṇā ।
kosallātaṇaassa jattha calaṇe vandāmi ṇandāmi a ।। kiṃ vā me śvaśureṇa vāsava-mahā-siṃhāsanādhyāsinā । kausalyā-tanayasya yatra caraṇau vande ca nandāmi ca ।।] sā ca svīyā tridhā mugdhā madhyā prauḍheti kathyate ।।
mugdhā nava-vayaḥ-kāmā ratau vāmā mṛduḥ krudhi । yatate rata-ceṣṭāyāṃ gūḍhaṃ lajjā-manoharam ।। kṛtāparādhe dayite vīkṣate rudatī satī । apriyaṃ vā priyaṃ vāpi na kiñcid api bhāṣate ।।
uttejitaṃ viṣama-sādhaka-bāṇa-yugmam । asyām ullāsitā ca gagane tanu-vīci-rekhā ।। dattādarā pariṇaye maṇi-putrikāṇām । ālakṣyate tad iha bhāva-navāvatāraḥ ।।
āliṅgatīti sahasā parivartamānā । sā sambhramāt sahacarīm avalambate sma ।। bhrūbhedo' pi tad īkṣaṇa-vyasaninā vyasmāri me cakṣuṣā । sakhyaḥ kiṃ karavāṇi māna-samaye saṅghāta-bhedo mama ।।
tais tair bandhu-vadhū-janasya vacanair nītābhimukhyaṃ punaḥ । saṃrohat-pulakā hareṇa hasatā śliṣṭā śivāyāstu vaḥ ।। sakhyaṃ saroja-śaśinoḥ sahasā babhūva । indīvara-dvayam avāpa tuṣāra-dhārām ।।
samāna-lajjā-madanā prodyat-tāruṇya-śālinī । madhyā kāmayate kāntaṃ mohānta-surata-kṣamā ।। tasmin kāma-kalāpa-kuśale vyāvṛtta-vaktre kila । lajjā-manmatha-madhyagāpi nitarāṃ tasyābhavat prītaye ।।
sakhyaṃ karoti jaghanaṃ pulinena sākam । vibhāti nitarāṃ madanasya lakṣmīḥ ।। āmīlitākṣi-yugam ādṛta-pāravaśyam । āśāsmahe kim api ceṣṭitam āyatākṣyāḥ ।।
madhyā tridhā māna-vṛtter dhīrādhīrobhayātmikā ।। dhīrā tu vakti vakroktyā sotprāsaṃ sāgasaṃ priyam ।। dhatte bhūṣaṇam ardha-candram amalaṃ candre na kiṃ kālimā । bhāgyaṃ draṣṭum anīśayaiva bhavataḥ kāntāparāddhaṃ mayā ।।
adhīrā paruṣair vākyaiḥ khedayed vallabhaṃ ruṣā ।। athā mamaiva- kācin nitānta-paruṣaṃ vinivṛtta-vaktrā । yāhīti khinnam akarod asakṛd bruvāṇā ।। dhīrādhīra tu vakroktyā sa-bāṣpaṃ vadati priyam ।।
citrokti-śravaṇotsukena kalitā tasyāṃ niśānāthatā । rājann ity uditāśru-gadgada-padaṃ kācid bravīti priyam ।। sampūrṇa-yauvanonmattā pragalbhā rūḍha-manmathā । dayitāṅge vilīneva yatate rati-keliṣu ।
rata-prārambha-mātre' pi gacchaty ānanda-mūrcchatām ।। ampūrṇa-yauvanatvam, yāthā- uttuṅgau kuca-kumbhau rambhā-stambhopamānam ūru-yugam । tarale dṛśau ca tasyāḥ sṛjatā dhātrā kim āhitaṃ sukṛtam ।। nirmṛṣṭāṅga-vilepanaiś ca karaṇaiś citre pravṛtte rate । kāñcī-dāma vibhinnam aṅgada-yugaṃ bhagnaṃ tathāpi priyaṃ
samprotsāhayati sma sā vidadhatī hastaṃ kvaṇat-kaṅkaṇam ।। māna-vṛtteḥ pragalbhāpi tridhā dhīrādi-bhedataḥ ।। udāste surate dhīrā sāvahitthā ca sādarā ।। athā- nādatte nava-mañjarīm ali-bhaya-vyājena dattām api ।
cāturyād vidadhāti mānam athavā vyaktīkaroti priyā ।। santarjya niṣṭhuraṃ roṣād adhīrā tāḍayet priyam ।। bhrūbhaṅgī-kuṭilair apāṅga-valanair ālokamānā muhuḥ । līlānīlasaroruheṇa niṭilaṃ hanti sma roṣākulā ।।
dhīrādhīra-guṇopetā dhīrādhīreti kathyate ।। athā, mamaiva- vaiyātyāt purataḥ sthite sati punar mānāvadhūtāśayā । uktvā mekhalayā hatena sahasāśliṣṭā sa-bāṣpaṃ sthitā ।। dvedhā jyeṣṭhā kaniṣṭheti madhyā prauḍhāpi tādṛśī ।।
ekasyā nayane nimīlya vihita-krīḍānubandha-cchalaḥ । antar-hāsa-lasat-kapola-phalakāṃ dhūrto' parāṃ cumbati ।। atretarasyāṃ paśyantyām api sambhāvanārhatayā pihita-locanāyā jyeṣṭhatvam । tatra samakṣaṃ sambhāvanānarhatvāt cumbitāyāḥ kanīyastvam । evam itarad-udāhāryam । dhīrādhīrādi-bhedena madhyā-prauḍhe tridhā tridhā ।
jyeṣṭhā-kaniṣṭḥā-bhedena tāḥ pratyekaṃ dvidhā dvidhā । mugdhā tv eka-vidhā caivaṃ sā trayodaśadhoditā ।। tha parakīyā- anyāpi dvividhā kanyā paroḍhā ceti bhedataḥ ।। tatra kanyā tv anūḍhā syāt sa-lajjā pitṛ-pālitā ।
sakhī-keliṣu visrabdhā prāyo mugdhā-guṇānvitā ।। kanyāṃ kila prekṣya pituḥ samīpe । premṇā śarīrārdha-harāṃ harasya ।। pradhānam apradhānaṃ vā nāṭakādāv iyaṃ bhavet ।
mālatī-mādhave lakṣye mālatī-madayantike ।। paroḍhā tu pareṇoḍhāpy anya-sambhoga-lālasā । lakṣyā kṣudra-prabandhe sā sapta-śatyādike budhaiḥ ।। śvaśrūr iṅgita-daivataṃ nayanayor īhāliho yātaraḥ ।
vaidagdhī-racanā-prapañca-rasika vyartho' yam atra śramaḥ ।। sādhāraṇa-strī gaṇikā kalā-prāgalbhya-dhārṣṭya-yuk ।। athā- sandaṣṭādhara-mukta-sītkṛtam atibhrāmyad-bhru-nṛtyat-karam । veśyānāṃ dhṛti-dhāma puṣpa-dhanuṣaḥ prāpnoti dhanyo ratam ।।
eṣā syād dvividhā raktā viraktā ceti bhedataḥ ।। tatra raktā tu varṇyā syād aprādhānyena nāṭake । agnimitrasya vijñeyā yathā rājña irāvatī ।। pradhānam apradhānaṃ vā nāṭaketara-rūpake ।
sā ced divyā nāṭake tu prādhānyenaiva varṇyate ।। ā darśanāt praviṣṭā sā me sura-loka-sundarī hṛdayam । bāṇena makara-ketoḥ kṛta-mārgam abandhya-pātena ।। viraktā tu prahasana-prabhṛtiṣv eva varṇyate ।
tasyā dhaurya-prabhṛtayo guāṣ tad-upayoginaḥ ।। channa-kāmān ratārthājñān bāla-pāṣaṇḍa-ṣaṇḍakān । rakteva rañjayed ibhyān niḥsvān mātrā vivāsayet ।। channa-kāmāḥ śrotriyādayaḥ । ratārthā rati-sukha-prayojanāḥ । ajñā mūḍhāḥ ।
gaṇikāyā nānurāgo guṇavaty api nāyake । rasābhāsa-prasaṅgaḥ syād araktāyāś ca varṇane ।। ataś ca nāṭakādau tu varṇyā sā na bhaved iti ।। athā cāhuḥ [śṛti }- sāmānyā vanitā veśyā sā dravyaṃ param icchatā ।।
guṇa-hīne ca na dveṣo nānurāgo guṇiny api । śṛṅgārābhāsa etāsu na śṛṅgāraḥ kadācana ।। iti । tan-mataṃ nānumanute dhīmān śrī-siṃha-bhūpatiḥ । bhāvānubandhābhāve ca nāyikātva-parāhateḥ ।।
tasyāḥ prakaraṇādau ca nāyikātva-vidhānataḥ । anāyikā-varṇane tu rasābhāsa-prasaṅgataḥ ।। tathā prakaraṇādīnām arasāśrayatāgateḥ । rasāśrayaṃ tu daśadhety ādi-śāstra-virodhataḥ ।।
tasmāt sādhāraṇa-strīṇāṃ guṇa-śālini nāyake । bhāvānubandhaḥ syād eva rudraṭasyāpi bhāṣaṇāt ।। atrāha rudraṭaḥ- niḥśaṅka-kelir na parāṅganāsu । sarvasvam etās tad aho smarasya ।। iti ।
udāttādi-bhidāṃ kecit sarvāsām api manvate । tās tu prāyeṇa dṛśyante sarvatra vyavahārataḥ ।। prathamaṃ proṣita-patikā vāska-sajjā tataś ca virahotkā । atha khaṇḍitā matā syāt kalahāntaritābhisārikā caiva ।।
kathitā ca vipralabdhā svādhīna-patis tathā cānyā । śṛṅgāra-kṛtāvasthābhedāt tāś cāṣṭadhā bhinnāḥ ।। dūra-deśaṃ gate kānte bhavet proṣita-bhartṛkā । asyās tu jāgaraḥ kārśyaṃ nimittādi-vilokanam ।।
mālinyam anavasthānaṃ prāyaḥ śayyā-niveṣaṇam । jāḍya-cintā-prabhṛtayo vikriyāḥ kathitā budhaiḥ ।। athā mama- kaṣṭaṃ kokila-kūjitāni sahasā jātāni dambholayaḥ । hā kaṣṭaṃ mama duṣkṛtasya mahimā candro' pi caṇḍāyate ।।
bharatādayair abhidadhe strīṇām vāras tu vāsakaḥ । svavāsaka-vaśāt kānte sameṣyati gṛhāntaram ।। sajjī-karoti cātmānaṃ yā sā vāsaka-sajjikā । asyās tu ceṣṭāḥ samparka-manoratha-vicintanam ।।
sakhī-vinodo hṛl-lekho muhur dūti-nirīkṣaṇam । priyābhigamana-mārgābhivīkṣaṇa-pramukhā matāḥ ।। atha mamaiva- darśaṃ darśaṃ dayita-padavīṃ sādaraṃ vīkṣamāṇā । sāraṅgākṣī raṇa-raṇikayā niḥśvasantī samāste ।।
anāgasi priyatame cirayaty utsukā tu yā । virahotkaṇṭhitā bhāva-vedibhiḥ sā samīritā ।। asyās tu ceṣṭā hṛt-tāpo vepathuś cāṅga-sādanam । aratir bāṣpa-mokṣaś ca svāvasthā-kathanādayaḥ ।। athā mamaiva-
madhu malayajaṃ mākandaṃ vā nirīkṣitum akṣamā । parabhṛta-rutaṃ śrutvā bāṣpaṃ vimuñcati vepate ।। ullaṅghya samayaṃ yasyāḥ preyān anyopabhogavān । bhoga-lakṣmāñcitaḥ prātar āgacchet sā hi khaṇḍitā ।।
asyās tu cintā niḥśvāsas tūṣṇīṃ-bhāvo' śru-mocanam । kheda-bhrānty-asphuṭālāpā ity ādyā vikriyā matāḥ ।। vadhūr dṛṣṭvā roṣāt kim api kuṭilaṃ jalpati muhuḥ । vidhatte niḥśvāsaṃ muhur api ca bāṣpaṃ visṛjati ।।
yā sakhīnāṃ puraḥ pāda-patitaṃ vallabhaṃ ruṣā । nirasya paścāt tapati kalahāntaritā hi sā ।। asyās tu bhrānti-saṃlāpau moho niḥśvasitaṃ jvaraḥ । muhuḥ pralāpa ity ādyā iṣṭāś ceṣṭā manīṣibhiḥ ।।
kopenādya kṛtaṃ mayā kim idam ity ārtā sakhīṃ jalpati । ramyaṃ dveṣṭi muhur muhuḥ pralapati śvāsādhikaṃ mūrcchati ।। madanānala-santaptā yābhisārayati priyam । jyotsnā-tāmasvinī yāna-yogyāmbara-vibhūṣaṇā ।।
svayaṃ vābhisared yā tu sā bhaved abhisārikā । asyāḥ santāpa-cintādyā vikriyās tu yathocitam ।। kāntābhisaraṇae svīyā lajjānāśādi-śaṅkayā । vyāghra-huṅkāra-santrasta-mṛga-śāva-vilocanā ।।
nīlyādi-rakta-vasana-racitāṅgāvaguṇṭhanā । svāṅge vilīnāvayavā niḥśabdaṃ pāda-cāriṇī ।। susnigdhaika-sakhī-mātra-yuktā yāti samutsukā । mṛṣā priye tu nidrāṇe pārśve tiṣṭhati niścalā ।।
garvātireka-nibhṛtā śītaiḥ srag-dāma-candanaiḥ । bhāvajñā bodhayaty enaṃ tad-bhāvāvekṣaṇotsukā ।। nināda-doṣeṇa nunoda nūpuram । iyeṣa dūtīm abhisārikā-janaḥ ।।
sarvāṅgīṇārdra-candanāḥ । jyotsnāyām abhisārikā ।। svīyāvat kanyakā jñeyā kāntābhisaraṇa-krame ।। veśyābhisārikā tv eti hṛṣṭā vaiśika-nāyakam ।
āvirbhūta-smita-mukhī mada-ghūrṇita-locanā ।। anuliptākhilāṅgī ca vicitrābharaṇānvitā । snehāṅkurita-romāñca-sphuṭībhūta-manobhavā ।। saṃveṣṭitā parijanair bhogopakaraṇānvitaiḥ ।
raśanārāva-mādhurya-dīpitānaṅga-vaibhavā ।। caraṇāmbuja-saṃlagna-maṇi-mañjīra-mañjulā । eṣā ca mṛdu-saṃsparśaiḥ keśa-kaṇḍūyanādibhiḥ । prabodhayati tad-bodhe praṇayāt kupitekṣaṇā ।।
māsi madhau candrātapa-dhavalāyāṃ niśi sakhī-janālāpaiḥ । madanāturābhisarati praṇayavatī yaṃ sa eva khalu dhanyaḥ ।। bāhu-vikṣepa-lulita-srasta-dhammilla-mallikā । calita-bhrū-vikārādi-vilāsa-lalitekṣaṇā ।।
maireyāviratāsvāda-mada-skhalita-jalpitā । preṣyābhiyāti dayitaṃ ceṭībhiḥ saha garvitā ।। priyaṃ kaṅkaṇa-nikvāṇa-mañju-vyajana-vījanaiḥ । vibodhya nirbhartsayati nāsābhaṅga-puraḥsaram ।।
vyaktālāpam itas tataḥ pratipadaṃ vikṣipta-bāhālatā । kvāṇena pratibodhya bhartsayati yaṃ dhanyaḥ sa ekaḥ pumān ।। kṛtvā saṅketam aprāpte daivād vyathitā tu yā । vipralabdheti sā proktā budhair asyās tu vikriyā ।
nirveda-cintā-khedāśru-mūrcchā-niḥśvasanādayaḥ ।। paśya tena sakhi vañcitā vayam । tatra vā kim iti vivyathe vadhūḥ ।। svāyattāsanna-patikā hṛṣṭā svādhīna-vallabhā ।
asyās tu ceṣṭāḥ kathitāḥ smara-pūjā-mahotsavaḥ । vana-keli-jala-krīḍā-kusumāpacayādayaḥ ।। kapole sotkampaṃ mṛga-mada-mayaṃ patra-tilakam । yuvā dhanyaḥ so' yaṃ madayati ca nityaṃ priyatamām ।।
uttamā madhyamā nīcety evaṃ sarvāḥ striyas tridhā ।। abhijātair bhoga-tṛptair guṇibhir yā ca kāmyate । gṛhṇāti kāraṇe kopam anunītā prasīdati ।। vidadhaty apriyaṃ patyau svayam ācarati priyam ।
vallabhe sāparādhe' pi tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭhati sottamā ।। puṃsaḥ svayaṃ kāmayate kāmyate yā ca tair vadhūḥ । sakrodhe krudhyati muhuḥ sānṛte' nṛta-vādinī ।। sāpakāre' pakartrī syāt snigdhe snihyati vallabhe ।
evam ādi-guṇopetā madhyamā sā prakīrtitā ।। akasmāt kupyati ruṣaṃ prārthitāpi na muñcati । surūpaṃ vā kurūpaṃ vā guṇavantam athāguṇam ।। sthaviraṃ taruṇaṃ vāpi yā vā kāmayate muhuḥ ।
īrṣyā-kopa-vivādeṣu niyatā sādhamā smṛtā ।। āsām udāharaṇāni lokata evāvagantavyāni । svīyā trayodaśa-vidhā vividhā ca varāṅganā । vaiśikaivaṃ ṣoḍaśadhā tāś cāvasthābhir aṣṭabhiḥ ।।
ekaikam aṣṭadhā tāsām uttamādi-prabhedataḥ । traividhyam evaṃ sa-caturaśītis triśatī bhavet ।। avasthā-trayam eveti kecid āhuḥ para-striyāḥ ।। try-avasthaiva para-strī syāt prathamaṃ virahonmanāḥ ।
tato æbhisārikā bhūtvābhisarantī vrajet svayaṃ ।। saṅketāc cet paribhraṣṭā vipralabdhā bhavet punaḥ । parādhīna-patitvena nānyāvasthātra saṅgatā ।। iti । āsāṃ dūtyaḥ sakhī ceṭī liṅginī prativeśinī ।
dhātreyī śilpakārī ca kumārī kathinī tathā । kārur vipraśnikā ceti netṛ-mitra-guṇānvitāḥ ।। liṅginī paṇḍita-kauśikyādiḥ । prativeśinī samīpa-gṛha-vartinī । śilpa-kārī vīṇā-vādanādi-nipuṇā । vipraśnikā daivajñā । itara-rasālambanānām anati-nirūpaṇīyatayā pṛthak-prakaraṇārambhasyānupayogāt tat-tad-rasa-prasaṅga eva nirūpaṇaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ ।। iti nāyikā-prakaraṇam ।।
uddīpanaṃ caturdhā syād ālambana-samāśrayam । guṇa-ceṣṭālaṅkṛtayas taṭasthāś ceti bhedataḥ ।। yauvanaṃ rūpa-lāvaṇye saundaryam abhirūpatā । mārdavaṃ saukumāryaṃ cety ālambana-gatā guṇāḥ ।।
sarvāsām api nārīṇāṃ yauvanaṃ tu caturvidham । pratiyauvanam etāsāṃ ceṣṭitāni pṛthak pṛthak ।। īṣac-capala-netrāntaṃ smara-smera-mukhāmbujam । sa-garva-jarajogaṇḍam asamagrāruṇādharam ।।
lāvaṇyodbheda-ramyāṅgaṃ vilasad-bhāva-saurabham । unmīlitāṅkura-kucam asphuṭāṅgaka-sandhikam ।। prathamaṃ yauvanaṃ tatra vartamānā mṛgekṣaṇā । apekṣate mṛdu-sparśaṃ sahate noddhatāṃ ratim ।।
sakhī-keli-ratā svāṅga-saṃskāra-kalitādarā । na kopa-harṣau bhajate sapatnī-darśanādiṣu । nātirajyati kāntasya saṅgame kiṃ tu lajjate ।। rekhodbhāsi tathā vali-trayam idaṃ na spaṣṭa-nimnottam ।
ramyaṃ yauvana-śaiśava-vyatikaronmiśraṃ vayo vartate ।। sāvajñam ādṛta-sakhī-jana-jalpitāni । vaḥ pāntu nūtana-samāgama-ceṣṭitāni ।। stanau pīnau tanur madhyaḥ pāṇipādasya raktimā ।
ūrū karikarākārāv aṅgaṃ vyaktāṅga-sandhikam । nitambo vipulo nābhir gabhīrā jaghanaṃ ghanam ।। vyaktā romāvalī snaigdhyam aṅga-keśaradākṣiṣu । dvitīya-yauvane tena kalitā vāma-locanā ।।
sakhīṣu svāśayajñāsu snigdhā prāyeṇa māninī । na prasīdaty anunaye sapatnīṣv abhyasūyinī ।। nāparādhān viṣahate praṇayerṣyākaṣāyitā । rati-keliṣv anibhṛtā ceṣṭate garvitā rahaḥ ।।
madhye kṣāmā cakita-hariṇī-prekṣaṇā nimna-nābhiḥ । yā tatra syād yuvatī-viṣaye sṛṣṭir ādyaiva dhātuḥ ।। asnigdhatā nayanayor gaṇḍayor mlāna-kāntitā । vicchāyatā khara-sparśo' py aṅgānāṃ ślathatā manāk ।।
adhare masṛṇo rāgas tṛtīye yauvane bhavet । tatra strīṇām iyaṃ ceṣṭā rati-tantra-vidagdhatā ।। vallabhasyāparityāgas tadākarṣaṇa-kauśalam । anādaro' parādheṣu sapatnīṣv apy amatsaraḥ ।।
madhyaiś ca māṃsalataraiḥ śithilair urojaiḥ । vṛntaślathāni kusumāni viḍambayanti ।। jarjaratvaṃ stana-śroṇi-gaṇḍoru-jaghanādiṣu । nirmāṃsatā ca bhavati caturthe yauvane striyāḥ ।।
tatra ceṣṭā rati-vidhāv anutsāho' samarthatā । sapatnīṣv ānukūlyaṃ ca kāntenāviraha-sthitiḥ ।। lambaiḥ kucair gata-kathā-pracuraiḥ prasaṅgaiḥ । bhartuḥ paṇān abhilaṣanty ahahālasāṅgyaḥ ।।
tatra śṛṅgāra-yogyatvaṃ sarasāhlāda-kāraṇam । ādya-dvitīyayor eva na tṛtīya-caturthayoḥ ।। aṅgāny abhūṣitāny eva prakṣepādyair vibhūṣaṇaiḥ । yena bhūṣitavad bhāti tad rūpam iti kathyate ।।
bhūyo' sahā bhūṣayituṃ śarīram । yāṃ vīkṣya lajjāṃ dadhire sabhūṣāḥ ।। muktāphaleṣu chāyāyās taralatvam ivāntarā । pratibhāti yad aṅgeṣu lāvaṇyaṃ tad ihocyate ।।
aṅgeṣu sphaṭikādarśa-darśanīyeṣu jṛmbhate । amalā komalā kāntir jyotsneva pratibimbitā ।। aṅga-pratyāngakānāṃ yaḥ sanniveśo yathocitam । susliṣṭa-sandhi-bandhaḥ syāt tat saundaryam itīryate ।।
saṅkṣiptaṃ niviḍonnata-stanam uraḥ pārśve pramṛṣṭe iva । chando nartayitur yathaiva manasi śliṣṭaṃ tathāsyā vapuḥ ।। yadātmīya-guṇotkarṣair vastv anyan nikaṭa-sthitam । sārūpyaṃ nayati prājñair ābhirūpyaṃ tad ucyate ।।
kāntāyāḥ karatala-rāga-rakta-raktaḥ । khasthaḥ san nayana-marīci-nīla-nīlaḥ ।। spṛṣṭaṃ yatrāṅgam aspṛṣṭam iva syān mārdavaṃ hi tat ।। athā- visraṃsate snaigdhya-guṇena dṛṣṭiḥ ।
saṃsparśa-śaṅkā na vidheḥ karābhyām ।। atra amūrtāpi dṛṣṭir visraṃsate । mūrtau karau kim uteti ślakṣṇatvātiśaya-kathanān mārdavam । yā sparśāsahatāṅgeṣu komalasyāpi vastunaḥ । tat saukumāryaṃ tredhā syān mukhya-madhyādhama-kramāt ।।
aṅgaṃ puṣpādi-saṃsparśāsahaṃ yena tad uttamam ।। svakeśa-puṣpair api yā sma dūyate । niṣeduṣī sthaṇḍila eva kevale ।। atra yadyapy uttarārdhe sthaṇḍila-sparśa-sahatvam uktam । tathāpi sthirāgrahasyaiva manasaḥ kleśa-sahiṣṇutvaṃ pratīyate na punaḥ śarīrasyety atrottama-saukumāryam upapadyate ।
na saheta kara-sparśaṃ yenāṅgaṃ madhyamaṃ hi tat ।। athā- sakhyāḥ kareṇa taruṇāmbuja-komalena । lākṣā-rasaḥ punar abhūn na tu bhūṣaṇāya ।। yenāṅgamātapādīnām asahaṃ tad ihādhamam ।।
nilīna-nīlālaka-cañcarīkam । tviṣā raveḥ komalayāpi tāmram ।। tac-ceṣṭā līlā-vilāsādayaḥ । te' py anubhāva-prakaraṇe vakṣyante । caturdhālaṅkṛtir vāso-bhūṣā-mālyānulepanaiḥ ।। atra vastrālaṅkāro, yathā-
paryāpta-candreva śarat-triyāmā । bhūyo babhau darpaṇam ādadhānā ।। jyotirbhir udyadbhir iva triyāmā । sarid vihaṅgair iva līyamānair āmucyamānābharaṇā cakāśe ।।
kāntiḥ kāpi kapolayoḥ prathayate tāmbūlam antargatam । veṣaḥ ko' pi vidagdha eṣa sudṛśaḥ sūte sukhaṃ cakṣuṣoḥ ।। taṭasthāś candrikā dhārā-gṛha-candrodayāv api । kokilālāpam ākanda-manda-māruta-ṣaṭ-padāḥ ।
latā-maṇḍapa-bhūgeha-dīrghikā-jala-dāravāḥ ।। prāsāda-garbha-saṅgīta-krīḍādri-sarid-ādayaḥ । evam ūhyā yathā kālam upabhogopayoginaḥ ।। rlatāli-kuñje lalitā nigūhitā ।
kuto' pi dṛṣṭvā bhajati sma mūrcchanām ।। vedīm adhiṣṭhātum apārayantī । ghorāsidhārā-gṛham anvamaṃsta ।। paśya tena sakhi vañcitā vayam ।
tatra vā kim iti vivyathe vadhūḥ ।। puṃskokilo yan madhuraṃ cukūja । tad eva jātaṃ vacanaṃ smarasya ।। svakarāvarjita-kumbha-vāri-sekaiḥ ।
payasā pannaga-vardhanṃ tad etat ।। mākanda ity aśokādīnām upalakṣaṇam । vinirgatas tad-garalena sākam । adakṣiṇo dakṣiṇa-mātariśvā ।।
mantrair apūrvair iva mañjunādaiḥ । māna-grahoccāṭanam ācaranti ।। tan-madhye' pi sarovaraṃ nidhuvanāntānanda-mandānilam । vallī-maṇḍapam atra sā sunayanā tvan-mārgam avekṣate ।।
dhūpādhivāsāśraya-bhū-gṛheṣu । śyāmākucoṣmāśrayiṇaḥ pumāṃsaḥ ।। vyādhūta-sphurad-uru-daṇḍa-puṇḍarīkāḥ । dṛśantām avirahita-śriyo vibhāgāḥ ।।
tathāpanīto ghana-garjitena । kṣaṇaṃ vidagdhāḥ kupitā ivāsan ।। atra jaladārava-grahaṇaṃ vidyud-ādīnām apy upalakṣaṇam । vidyuto, yathā- dgopāṅganā mādhavam āliliṅga ।
hrīṇeva tūrṇaṃ jaladaṃ jagāhe ।। kapota-pālī-stha-kapotakeṣu । reme payodānila-durgameṣu ।। maṇḍape paṭu-raṭan-madhuvrate ।
māna-mīna-vaḍiśena veṇunā ।। tvat-samparkāt pulakitam iva prauḍha-puṣpaiḥ kadambaiḥ । uddāmāni prathayati śilā-veśmabhir yauvanāni ।। rodho-latā-puṣpa-vahe sarayvāḥ ।
tasyāmbhasi grīṣma-sukhe babhūva ।। ity ādy anyad apy udāhāryam । ālambana-gatāś ceṣṭā anubhāvā vivakṣitāḥ । bhāvaṃ manogataṃ sākṣāt sva-hetuṃ vyañjayanti ye ।
te' nubhāvā iti khyātā bhrū-kṣepa-smitādayaḥ ।। te caturdhā citta-gātra-vāg-buddhyārambha-sambhavāḥ । tatra ca bhāvo hāvo helā śobhā kānti-dīptī ca ।। prāgalbhyaṃ mādhuryaṃ dhairyaudāryaṃ ca cittajā bhāvāḥ ।
nirvikārasya cittasya bhāvaḥ syād ādi-vikriyā ।। cittasyāvikṛtiḥ sattvaṃ vikṛteḥ kāraṇe sati । tatrādyā vikriyā bhāvo bījasyādi-vikāravat ।। iti । dattādarā pariṇaye maṇi-putrikāṇām ।
ālakṣyate tad iha bhāvanavāvatāraḥ ।। atra pūrvaṃ śaiśavena rasānabhijñasya cittasya prasādhana-vidhitsā-pāñcālikā-pariṇayādara-sakhī-jana-hāsa-śaṅkādīnāṃ tat-prathamam eva sambhūtatvād bhāvaḥ । grīvā-recaka-saṃyukto bhrū-netrādi-vilāsa-kṛt । bhāva īṣat-prakāśo yaḥ sa hāva iti kathyate ।।
kṣaṇaṃ saroṣa-smita-mātta-lajjā । sambandhinī svasya sakhī-janasya ।। atra citta-vikārāṇāṃ roṣa-harṣa-lajjādīnāṃ kuṭilekṣaṇa-smita-natānanatvādibhir īṣat-prakāśanād ayaṃ hāvaḥ । nānā-vikāraiḥ suvyaktaḥ śṛṅgārākṛti-sūcakaiḥ ।
hāva eva bhaved dhelā lalitābhinayātmikā ।। sphurad bāla-kadamba-kalpaiḥ । mukhena paryasta-vilocanena ।। atra romāñca-mukha-sācīkaraṇa-paryasta-vilocanatvādi-vikāraiś citta-vyāpārasyātiprakāśatvena helā ।
sā śobhā rūpa-bhogādyair yat syād aṅga-vibhūṣaṇam ।। athā- avirata-rata-vegād aṃsa-lamboru-cūlīm । kara-tala-dhṛta-nīvīṃ kātarākṣīṃ bhajāmaḥ ।। śobhaiva kāntir ākhyātā manmathāpyāyanojjvalā ।।
dhṛtvā cānyena vāsaḥ śithilita-kavarī-bhāram aṃse vahantyāḥ । śayyām āliṅgya nītaṃ vapur alasa-lasad-bāhu lakṣmyāḥ punātu ।। atra pūrva-ratānta-janitāyā vapuḥ-kānter uttara-ratārambha-hetutvān manmathāpyāyakatvam । kāntir eva vayo-bhoga-deśa-kāla-guṇādibhiḥ ।
uddīpitātivistāraṃ yātā ced dīptir ucyate ।। aṅga-glāniṃ surata-janitāṃ tantu-jālāvalambāḥ । vyālumpanti sphuṭa-jala-lava-syandinaś candra-kāntāḥ ।। atra priyatamāliṅgana-saudha-jyotsnādi-guṇaiḥ surata-glāni-vyālopanād uttara-suratotsāha-rūpā dīptiḥ pratīyate ।
niḥśaṅkatvaṃ prayogeṣu prāgalbhyaṃ parikīrtyate ।। śiṣyatāṃ nidhuvanopadeśinaḥ śaṅkarasya rahasi prapannayā । yat tad eva guru-dakṣiṇī-kṛtam ।। atra guru-dakṣiṇī-kṛtam ity anena pratikaraṇa-rūpaṃ prāgalbhyaṃ pratīyate ।
mādhuryaṃ nāma ceṣṭānāṃ sarvāvasthāsu mārdavam ।। kṛtvā śyāmāviṭapa-sadṛśaṃ srasta-muktaṃ dvitīyam । nṛttād asyāḥ sthitam atitarāṃ kāntam ṛjvāyatārdham ।। atra pādāṅguṣṭhena kusuma-lolanādi-kriyāṇāṃ nṛttānta-pariśrāntāv api cārutvān mādhuryam ।
sthirā cittonnatir yā tu tad dhairyam iti saṃjñitam ।। athā- atha viśvātmane gaurī sandideśa mithaḥ sakhīm । dātā me bhūtbhṛtāṃ nāthaḥ pramāṇīkriyatām iti ।। audāryaṃ vinayaṃ prāhuḥ sarvāvasthānugaṃ budhāḥ ।।
na kāma-cāro mayi śaṅkanīyaḥ । vipāka-visphūrjathur aprasahyaḥ ।। atrānaparādhe' pi niṣkāsayato rāmasyānupālambhāt sītāyā audāryaṃ pratīyate । sarvāvasthā-samatvāviditeṅgitākāratva-rūpayor lakṣaṇayoś citta-dhairya evāntarbhūtatvāt bhoja-rāja-lakṣitau sthairya-gāmbhīrya-rūpāv anyau dvau cittārambhau cāsmad-ukte dhairya evāntarbhūtāv iti daśaiva cittārambhāḥ । līlā vilāso vicchittir vibhramaḥ kilakiñcitam ।
moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭamitaṃ bibboko lalitaṃ tathā । vihṛtaṃ ceti vijñeyā yoṣitāṃ daśa gātrajāḥ ।। priyānukaraṇaṃ yat tu madhurālāpa-pūrvakaiḥ । ceṣṭitair gatibhir vā syāt sā līleti nigadyate ।।
duṣṭa-kāliya tiṣṭhādya kṛṣṇo' ham iti cāparā । bāhum āsphoṭya kṛṣṇasya līlā-sarvasvam ādade ।। priya-samprāpti-samaye bhrū-netrānana-karmaṇām । tātkāliko viśeṣo yaḥ sa vilāsa itīritaḥ ।।
ālokya mugdha-madhurair alasair apāṅgaiḥ । lakṣmīr abhitti-likhiteva ciraṃ samāste ।। ākalpa-kalpanālpāpi vicchittir atikānti-kṛt ।। kāntiḥ kāpi kapolayoḥ prathayate tāmbūlam antargatam ।
veṣaḥ ko' pi vidagdha eṣa sudṛśaḥ sūte sukhaṃ cakṣuṣoḥ ।। priyā-gamana-velāyāṃ madanāveśa-sambhramāt । vibhramo' ṅgada-hārādi-bhūṣā-sthāna-viparyayaḥ ।। kāñcī-kalāpaṃ stana-bhāra-yugme ।
nitamba-bimbe ca babandha hāram ।। śoka-roṣāśru-harṣādeḥ saṅkaraḥ kila-kiñcitam ।। athā- vivakṣati preyasi kuñcita-bhrūḥ । mukhaṃ pidhatte sma kapolakena ।।
mayā labdhe tasyāḥ kvaṇita-kala-kaṇṭhārdham adhare । smita-krodhodbhrāntaṃ punar api vidadhyān mayi mukham ।। svābhilāṣa-prakaṭam moṭṭāyitam itīritam ।। tanvyā priyasya gaditāni sakhī-kathāsu ।
āvellite bhuja-late lalitāṅga-bhaṅgam ।। keśādharādi-grahaṇe modamāne' pi mānase । duḥkhiteva bahiḥ kupyed yatra kuṭṭamitaṃ hi tat ।। śītkṛtāni nayanārdha-nimeṣāḥ ।
astratām upayayur madanasya ।। atra rahasīti sāmānya-sūcitānāṃ keśādhara-grahaṇādīnāṃ kārya-bhūtaiḥ pāṇi-pallava-vidhūnana-sītkṛtādibhir bahir eva kopasya pratīyamānatvāt kuṭṭamitam । iṣṭe' py anādaro garvān mānād bibboka īritaḥ ।। arvād, yathā- garvān nirīheva cucumba kācit ।
striyaḥ parārthān iva kalpayanti ।। vāci bhartur avadhīraṇā-parā । ālalāpi vijayām ahetukam ।। atra sandhyā-nimittaṃ mānād anādareṇa bibbokaḥ ।
vinyāsa-bhaṅgi-raṅgānāṃ bhrū-vilāsa-manoharāḥ । sukumārā bhaved yatra lalitaṃ tad-udīritam ।। kanaka-maya-kavāṭaṃ pāṇinā kampayantī । varatanur iyam āste mandirasyeva lakṣmīḥ ।।
īrṣyayā māna-lajjābhyāṃ na dattaṃ yogyam uttaram । kriyayā vyajyate yatra vihṛtaṃ tad udīritam ।। sakhyāṃ sakhī vetra-bhṛd ābabhāṣe । vadhūr asūyākuṭilaṃ dadarśa ।।
atra na vrajāva ity uttaram adattvā kuṭila-darśanenaiva vyañjanād vihṛtam । rātrau mayi kṣutavati kṣiti-pāla-putryā । karṇe' rpitaṃ kanaka-patram anālapantyā ।। praśna-tatparam anaṅga-śāsanam ।
mūrdha-kampamayam uttaraṃ dadau ।। itthaṃ śrī-siṃha-bhūpena sattvālaṅkāra-śālinā । kathitāḥ sattvajāḥ strīṇām alaṅkārās tu viṃśatiḥ ।। sattvād daśaiva bhāvādyā jātā līlādayas tu na ।
ato hi viṃśatir bhāvāḥ sāttvikā iti nocitam ।। yujyate sāttvikatvaṃ ca bhāvādi-sahacāriṇaḥ । līlādi-daśakasyāpi chatri-nyāya-balāt sphuṭam ।। bhojena krīḍitaṃ kelir ity anyau gātrajau smṛtau ।
ato viṃśatir ity atra saṅkhyeyaṃ nopapadyate ।। krīḍitaṃ kelir ity anyau gātrārambhāv udāhṛtau । bālya-yauvana-kaumāra-sādhāraṇa-vihāra-bhāk । viśeṣaḥ krīḍitaṃ kelis tad eva dayitāśrayam ।। iti ।
udāhṛtaṃ ca । krīḍitaṃ, yathā- sā kandukaiḥ kṛtrima-putrakaiś ca । krīḍā-rasaṃ nirviśatīva bālye ।। apārayantaṃ kila puṣpajaṃ rajaḥ ।
priyaṃ jaghānonnata-pīvara-stanī ।। iti । atrocyate bhāva-tattva-vedinā siṃha-bhūbhujā । ādyaḥ prāg eva bhāvādi-samutpatteś ca śaiśave ।। kanyā-vinoda-mātratvād anubhāveṣu neṣyate ।
prema-visrambha-mātratvān nānyasyāpy anubhāvatā । ato viṃśatir ity eṣā saṅkhyā saṅkhyāvatāṃ matā ।। śobhā vilāso mādhuryaṃ dhairyaṃ gāmbhīryam eva ca । lalitaudārya-tejāṃsi sattva-bhedās tu pauruṣāḥ ।।
nīce dayādhike spardhā śauryotsāhau ca dakṣatā । yatra prakaṭatāṃ yānti sā śobheti prakīrtitā ।। yuṣmad-gātreṣu lajjāṃ dadhati paramam amī sāyakāḥ sampatantaḥ । kiñcid bhrū-bhaṅga-līlā-niyamita-jaladhiṃ rāmam anveṣayāmi ।।
atra prathamārdhe kṣudra-kapi-viṣaye dayā, uttarārdhe rāma-viṣayā spardhā cendrajitaḥ pratīyate । śaurye sattva-sāraḥ । utsāhaḥ sthairyam । dakṣatā kṣipra-kāritvam । eṣāṃ nāyaka-guṇa-nirūpaṇāvasara evodāharaṇāni darśitāni । vṛṣabhasyeva gambhīrā gatir dhīraṃ ca darśanam । sasmitaṃ ca vaco yatra sa vilāsa itīritaḥ ।। tān arghyān arghyam ādāya dūraṃ pratyudyayau giriḥ ।
namayan sāra-gurubhiḥ pāda-nyāsair vasundharām ।। prabhāta-paṅkeruha-bandhureṇa । pratyābabhāṣe sa ca daitya-dūtam ।। dyotitāntaḥ-sabhaiḥ kunda-kuḍmalāgra-dataḥ smitaiḥ ।
snapitevābhavat tasya śuddha-varṇā sarasvatī ।। tan mādhuryaṃ yatra ceṣṭā-dṛṣṭy-ādeḥ spṛhaṇīyatā ।। ।। MISSING śaram utsaṅga-niṣaṇṇa-dhanvanaḥ । nayanopānta-vilokitaṃ ca yat ।।
dhairya-gāmbhīrye tu nāyaka-guṇa-varṇanāvasara evokte । śṛṅgāra-pracurā ceṣṭā yatra tal lalitaṃ bhavet ।। smara-smeraṃ gaṇḍoḍḍamara-pulakaṃ vaktra-kamalam । jaṭājūṭa-granthiṃ draḍhayati raghūṇāṃ parivṛḍhaḥ ।।
audārya-tejasor api nāyaka-prasaṅga eva lakṣaṇodāharaṇe prokte । atra gāmbhīrya-dhairye dve cittaje gātrajāḥ pare । eke sādhāraṇān etān menire citta-gātrayoḥ ।। ālāpaś ca vilāpaś ca saṃlāpaś ca pralāpakaḥ ।
anulāpāpalāpau ca sandeśaś cātideśakaḥ ।। nirdeśaś copadeśaś cāpadeśo vyapadeśakaḥ । evaṃ dvādaśadhā proktā kīrtitā vāg-ārambhā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। tatrālāpaḥ priyoktiḥ syāt ।।
kas te vākyāmṛtaṃ tyaktvā śṛṇoty anya-giraṃ budhaḥ । sahakāra-rasaṃ tyaktvā nimbaṃ cumbati kiṃ śukaḥ ।। mugdhākṣīṇāṃ vahasi mṛdhunā kuntalenopamānam । pūjā-puṣpaṃ bhavati bhavato bhukta-śeṣaṃ surāṇām ।।
vilāpo duḥkhajaṃ vacaḥ ।। śrotuṃ ca tasyāḥ paridevitāni । ajīvayan mārutir ātta-vairaḥ ।। ukti-pratyuktimad-vākyaṃ saṃlāpa iti kīrtitam ।।
puṣpiṇy ahaṃ khalu surāsura-vandanīya । vākyair alaṃ phala-bhug īśa paro' sti yāhi ।। vyarthālāpaḥ pralāpaḥ syāt ।। stanau ca pīnau kaṭhinau ṭhinau ṭhinau ।
aho vicitraṃ taruṇī ruṇī ruṇī ।। anulāpo muhur vacaḥ ।। śaśī śaśī nahi nahi dṛk-sukhaṃ mukham । nabho nabho nahi nahi cāru madhyamam ।।
apalāpas tu pūrvoktasyānyathā yojanaṃ bhavet ।। kim atra gotra-skhalanaṃ mameti । prasādayan vyāja-padena rādhāṃ punātu devaḥ puruṣottamo vaḥ ।। atra nāyikā-vācakayoḥ rukmiṇī-satyabhāmā-padayoḥ pūrvoktayoḥ suvarṇavattva-satya-kopatva-lakṣaṇenārthena yojanād apalāpaḥ ।
sandeśas tu proṣitasya sva-vārtā-preṣaṇaṃ bhavet ।। athā- mā kaulīnād asita-nayane mayy aviśvāsinī bhūḥ । iṣṭe vastuny upacita-rasāḥ prema-rāśī-bhavanti ।। so' tideśo mad-uktāni tad-uktānīti yad vacaḥ ।।
jagad-ātmā puruṣottamaḥ svayam । giram asmākam avehi vāridhe ।। nirdeśas tu bhavet so' yam aham ity ādi-bhāṣaṇam ।। athā- ete vayam amī dārāḥ kanyeyaṃ kula-jīvitam ।
brūta yenātra vaḥ kāryam anāsthā bāhya-vastuṣu ।। yatra śikṣārtha-vacanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate ।। mānyaṃ mānayata sajjanaṃ bhajata । dīpa-śikhā-cañcalā lakṣmīḥ ।।
anyārtha-kathanaṃ yatra so' padeśa itīritaḥ ।। athā- dhatte cūta-latā navaṃ kisalayaṃ puṃskokilāsvāditam । celānte tirodadhe stana-taṭaṃ bimbādharaṃ pāṇinā ।। vyājenātmābhilāṣoktir yatrāyaṃ vyapadeśakaḥ ।।
taha paricuṃbia cūda-mañjariṃ । mahara bihmarido' si ṇaṃ kahaṃ ।। tathā paricumbya cūta-mañjarīm । madhukara vismṛto' syenāṃ katham ।।]
buddhy-ārambhās tathā proktā rīti-vṛtti-pravṛttayaḥ ।। tatra rītiḥ । rītiḥ syāt pada-vinyāsa-bhaṅgī sā tu tridhā matā । komalā kaṭhinā miśrā ceti syāt tatra komalā ।।
dvitīya-turya-varṇair yā svalpair vargeṣu nirmitā । alpa-prāṇākṣara-prāyā daśa-prāṇa-samanvitā ।। samāsa-rahitā svalpaiḥ samāsair vā vibhūṣitā । vidarbha-jana-hṛdyatvāt sā vaidarbhīti kathyate ।।
udvela-rāgam urarīkṛta-kāma-tantram । saṃlāpa-rūpam amṛtaṃ sarasīruhākṣyāḥ ।। atha yantāram ādiśya dhuryān viśrāmayeti saḥ । tām avāropayat patnīṃ rathād avatatāra ca ।।
śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatā mādhuryaṃ sukumāratā । artha-vyaktir udāratvam ojaḥ kānti-samādhayaḥ । ete vaidarbha-mārgasya prāṇā daśa guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। kevalālpa-prāṇa-varṇa-pada-sandarbha-lakṣaṇam ।
śaithilyaṃ yatra na spṛṣṭaṃ sa śleṣaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। yathā mamaiva utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity ādau śliṣṭa-varṇa-miśrita-bandhatvāt śleṣaḥ । prasiddhārtha-padatvaṃ yat sa prasādo nigadyate ।। athā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atra padānām akleśenaivārtha-bodhana-sāmarthyāt prasādaḥ । bandha-vaiṣamya-rāhityaṃ samatā pada-gumphane ।
bandho mṛduḥ sphuṭo miśra iti tredhā sa nigadyate ।। atra mṛdu-varṇa-bandhasya samatā, yathā- kanaka-maya-kavāṭaṃ pāṇinā kampayantī । vara-tanur iyam āste mandirasyeva lakṣmīḥ ।। atra mṛdu-varṇa-prāya-bandhasya nirvyūḍhatvān mṛdu-bandha-samatā ।
madhu-samṛddhi-samedhita-medhayā । dhvani-bhṛtānibhṛtākṣaram ujjage ।। atra sphuṭa-varṇa-prāya-bandhasya nirvyūḍhatvāt sphuṭa-bandha-samatā । miśra-bandha-samatā, yathā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity ādau । atra miśrī-bhūta-mṛdu-sphuṭa-varṇa-bandhasya nirvāhād miśra-bandha-samatā ।
tan mādhuryaṃ bhaved yatra śabde' rthe ca sphuṭo rasaḥ ।। yathā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atra śabdārthayoḥ śṛṅgāra-parivāhitvena mādhuryam । yad aniṣṭhura-varṇatvaṃ saukumāryaṃ tad ucyate ।। athā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam udgata-manda-hāsam ity atra saṃyuktākṣara-sadbhāve' py aniṣṭhuratvāt saukumāryam । śrūyamāṇasya vākyasya vinā śabdāntara-spṛhām ।
arthāvagamakatvaṃ yad artha-vyaktir iyaṃ matā ।। athā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atra sarveṣāṃ padānām adhyāhāraya-pada-nirākāṅkṣatayā artha-vyaktiḥ । ukte vākye guṇotkarṣa-pratibhānam udāratā ।। yathā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atrānyonyānurāgotkarṣa-pratibhānād udāratvam । samāsa-bahulatvaṃ yat tad ojaḥ iti gīyate ।। b
yathā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atra yathocita-samāsa-bāhulyād ojaḥ । loka-sthitim anullaṅghya hṛdyārtha-pratipādanam । kāntiḥ syād dvividhā khyātā vārtāyāṃ varṇanāsu ca ।। ārtā nāma kuśala-praśna-pūrvikā saṅkathā । tatra yathā- paridhauta-bhavat-padāmbunā nava-candrātapa-śītalena me ।
api santata-marma-kṛntanaḥ kṛta-nirvāṇa ivaurva-pāvakaḥ ।। atra brāhmaṇa-pādodakasya santāpa-śamana-rūpāṃ laukikīṃ sthitim anullaṅghyaiva samudreṇa munīnāṃ purataḥ saṅkathanāt kāntiḥ । uttuṅgau stana-kalaśau sambhā-stambhopamānam ūru-yugam । tarale dṛśau ca tasyāḥ sṛjatā dhātrā kim āhitaṃ sukṛtam ।।
atra viśiṣṭa-vastu-nirmāṇam apuṇya-kṛtāṃ na bhavatīti loka-sthity-anurodhenaiva varṇanāt kāntiḥ । samādhiḥ so' nya-dharmāṇāṃ yad anyatrādhiropaṇam ।। yathā utphulla-gaṇḍa-yugam ity atrotphullodgatodvelatva-rūpāṇāṃ puṣpa-prāṇi-samudra-dharmāṇaṃ gaṇḍa-sthala-manda-hāsa-rāgeṣu samāropitatvāt samādhiḥ । atidīrgha-samāsa-yutā bahulair varṇair yutā mahā-prāṇaiḥ ।
kaṭhinā sā gauḍīyety uktā tad-deśa-budha-manojñatvāt ।। bādhā-lampaṭa-bāhu-sampad-udayad-durvāra-garvāśayam । bāṇair dāśarathī rathī ratha-gataṃ vivyādha divyāyudhaḥ ।। atra dīrgha-samsatvaṃ mahā-prāṇākṣara-prāyatvaṃ ca spaṣṭam ।
yatrobhaya-guṇa-grāma-saṃniveśas tulādhṛtaḥ । sā miśrā saiva pāñcālīty uktā tad-deśaja-priyā ।। tanor madhyasyāntaḥ parimilanam aprāpya haritam । kṛśāṅgyāḥ santāpaṃ vadati visinī-patra-śayanam ।।
atrālpa-samāsatva-dīrgha-samāsatva-rūpayoḥ prasāda-sphuṭa-bandhatva-rūpayor aniṣṭhurākṣara-prāyatva-rūpayoḥ pṛthak-padatva-granthilatvayoś ca ubhaya-rīti-dharmayos tulādhṛtayor iva saṃniveśān miśreyaṃ rītiḥ । āndhrī lāṭī ca saurāṣṭrīty ādayo miśra-rītayaḥ । santi tat-tad-deśa-vidvat-priya-miśraṇa-bhedataḥ ।। ta eva pada-saṅghātās tā evārtha-vibhūtayaḥ ।
tathāpi navyaṃ bhavati kāvyaṃ grathana-kauśalāt ।। tāsāṃ grantha-gaḍutvena lakṣaṇaṃ nocyate mayā । bhojādi-grantha-bandheṣu tad-ākāṅkṣibhir īkṣyatām ।। bhāratī sātvatī caiva kaiśiky ārabhaṭīti ca ।
catasro vṛttayas tāsām utpattir vakṣyate sphuṭam ।। jagaty ekārṇave jāte bhagavān avyayaḥ pumān । bhogi-bhogam adhiṣṭhāya yoga-nidrā-paro' bhavat ।। tadā vīrya-madonmattau daityendrau madhu-kaiṭabhau ।
tarasā devadeveśam āgatau raṇa-kāṅkṣiṇau ।। vividhaiḥ paruṣair vākyair adhikṣepa-vidhāyinau । muṣṭi-jānu-prahāraiś ca yodhayāmāsatur harim ।। tan-nābhi-kamalotpannaḥ prajāpatir abhāṣata ।
kim etad bhāratī-vṛttir adhunāpi pravartate ।। tad imau naya durdharṣau nidhanaṃ tvarayā vibho । iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā nijagāda janārdanaḥ ।। idaṃ kāvya-kriyā-hetor bhāratī nirmitā dhruvam ।
bhāṣaṇād vākya-bāhulyād bhāratīyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। adhunaiva nihanmy etāv ity ābhāṣya vaco hariḥ । nirmalair nirvikāraiś ca sāṅga-hārair manoharaiḥ ।। aṅgais tau yodhayāmāsa daityendrau yuddha-śālinau ।
bhūmi-sthānaka-saṃyogaiḥ pada-kṣepais tathā hareḥ ।। bhūmes tadābhavad bhāras tad-vaśād api bhāratī । valgitaiḥ śārṅgiṇas tatra dīptaiḥ sambhrama-varjitaiḥ ।। sattvādhikair bāhu-daṇḍaiḥ sātvatvī vṛttir udgatā ।
vicitrair aṅga-hāraiś ca helayā sa tadā hariḥ ।। yat tau babandha keśeṣu jātā sā kaiśikī tataḥ । sa-saṃrambhaiḥ savegaiś ca citra-cārī-samutthitaiḥ ।। niyuddha-karaṇair jātā citrair ārabhaṭī tataḥ ।
yasmāc citrair aṅgahāraiḥ kṛtaṃ dānava-mardanam ।। tasmād abja-bhuvā loke niyuddha-samayaḥ kṛtaḥ । yaḥ śastrāstrādi-mokṣeṣu nyāyaḥ sa pāribhāṣitaḥ ।। nāṭya-kāvya-kriyā-yoge rasa-bhāva-samāśritaḥ ।
sa eva samayo dhātrā vṛttir ity eva saṃjñitaḥ ।। hariṇā tena yad vastu valigitair yādṛśaṃ kṛtam । tadvad eva kṛtā vṛttir dhātrā tasyāṅga-sambhavā ।। ṛgvedāc ca yajurvedāt sāmavedād atharvaṇaḥ ।
bhāraty-ādyā kramāj jātā ity anye tu pracakṣate ।। prayuktatvena bharatair bhāratīti nigadyate । prastāvanopayogitvāt sāṅgaṃ tatraiva lakṣyate ।। sāttvikena guṇenātityāga-śauryādinā yutā ।
harṣa-pradhānā santyakta-śoka-bhāvā ca yā bhavet ।। sātvatī nāma sā vṛttiḥ proktā lakṣaṇa-kovidaiḥ । aṅgāny asyās tu catvāri saṃlāpottāpakāv api । saṅghātyaḥ parivartaś cety eṣāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate ।।
īrṣyā-krodhādibhir bhāvai rasair vīrādbhutādibhiḥ । parasparaṃ gabhīroktiḥ saṃlāpa iti śabdyate ।। athānargha-rāghave, rāmaḥ- rakṣo-rājam api tvayā vidadhatā sandhyā-samādhi-vratam । sarvābhir mahiṣībhir ambu-nidhayo viśve' pi vismāpitāḥ ।।
mārāṅka-vaijñānika payśatas tvām । na śṛṇvatas tṛpyati mānasaṃ me ।। atra dhīrodātta-dhīroddhatayoḥ rāma-bālinoḥ parasparaṃ yuddha-cikīrṣābhiprāya-yogād anyonya-parākramotkarṣa-varṇanāt saṃlāpaḥ । preraṇaṃ yat parasyādau yuddhāyotthāpakas tu saḥ ।।
śiśu-krīḍā-bhagna-tripura-hara-dhanvā tava puraḥ । nisṛṣṭārtho bāhuḥ kathaya kataras te paraharatu ।। atra rāmabhadreṇa prāk prahārāya jāmadagnyaḥ prerita ity utthāpakaḥ । mantra-śaktyārtha-śaktyā vā daiva-śaktyātha pauruṣāt ।
saṅghasya bhedanaṃ yat tu saṅghātyaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ।। mantro naya-prayogaḥ । tasya śaktyā yathā mudrā-rākṣase cāṇakyena śatru-sahāyānāṃ bhedanāt saṅghātyaḥ । artha-śaktyā yathā mahābhārate ādiparvaṇi devais tilottamālakṣaṇenārthena sundopasundayor atisnigdhayor bhedanāt saṅghātyaḥ । hā hā vatsa vibhīṣaṇa tvam api me kāryeṇa heyaḥ sthitaḥ । vatse kekasi hā hatāsmi na cirāt trīn putrakān paśyasi ।।
atra rāghavānukūla-daiva-mohitena mālyavatā khara-dūṣaṇa-triśirasāṃ bhedaḥ saṃvihita iti saṅghātyaḥ । pūrvodyuktasya kāryasya parityāgena yad bhavet । kāryāntara-svīkaraṇaṃ jñeyaḥ sa parivartakaḥ ।। yathottara-rāma-carite pañcamāṅke kumārau -aho priya-darśanaḥ kumāraḥ ।
purāṇo vā janmāntara-niviḍa-baddhaḥ paricayaḥ । mamaitasmin dṛṣṭe hṛdayam avadhānaṃ racayati ।। atra lavasya candraketoś ca parasparākāra-viśeṣa-sandarśanena raṇa-saṃrambhauddhatya-parihāreṇa vinayārjava-svīkāra-kathanāt parivartakaḥ । nṛtya-gīta-vilāsādi-mṛdu-śṛṅgāra-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।
samanvitā bhaved vṛttiḥ kaiśikī ślakṣṇa-bhūṣaṇā ।। aṅgāny asyās tu catvāri narma tat-pūrvakā ime । sphañja-sphoṭau ca garbhaś ca teṣāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate ।। śṛṅgāra-rasa-bhūyiṣṭhaḥ priya-cittānurañjakaḥ ।
agrāmyaḥ parihāsas tu narma syāt tat tridhā matam ।। śṛṅgāra-hāsyajaṃ śuddha-hāsyajaṃ bhaya-hāsyajam । śṛṅgāra-hāsyajaṃ narma trividhaṃ parikīrtitam ।। sambhogecchā-prakaṭanād anurāga-niveśanāt ।
tathā kṛtāparādhasya priyasya pratibhedanāt । sambhogecchā-prakaṭanaṃ tridhā vāg-veṣa-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।। atra vācā sambhogecchā-prakaṭanād, yathā- kiṃ tv evaṃ vijanasthayor hata-janaḥ sambhāvayaty anyathā । āśliṣyan pulakotkarāñcita-tanur gopīṃ hariḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
atra nijāvasthāna-vilambanasya vyarthatvaṃ dhīratvādi-sūcakair acyutādi-padair vadantyā tayāpi gopikayā vācā sambhogecchā prakaṭiteti narma । santāpa-saṃvalitamānasa-locanābhiḥ । vinyāsa-hāsita-sakhījanam aṅganābhiḥ ।। atra viparīta-nyasta-bhūṣaṇa-lakṣaṇena veṣeṇa janitaiḥ sakhī-jana-hāsaiḥ kāminīnāṃ sambhogecchā prakaṭiteti narma ।।
sāloe cia sūre ghariṇī ghara-sāmiassa ghettūṇa । ṇecchaṃ tassa bi pāe dhubai hasaṃtī hasaṃtassa ।। [sāloka eva sūrye gṛhiṇī gṛha-svāmino gṛhītvā । necchato' pi pādau dhāvati hasantī hasataḥ ।।]
atra sūryāstamayāt prāg eva caraṇa-prakṣālana-lakṣaṇayā kriyayā niṣkramaṇa-nivāraṇa-janitena hāsena sambhogecchā-prakaṭanān narma । anurāga-prakāśo' pi bhogecchā-narmavat tridhā ।। ayaṃ tv akasmād vikalaḥ kathāntare । viśuddha-mugdhaḥ kula-kanyakā-janaḥ ।।
atra lavaṅgikayā viśuddha-mugdhaḥ kula-kanyakā-jana iti parihāsena madayantikānurāga-nivedanān narma । tais tair bandhu-vadhū-janasya vacanair nītābhimukhyaṃ punaḥ । saṃrohat-pulakā hareṇa hasatā śliṣṭā śivāyāstu vaḥ ।। atra pulaka-saṃroha-lakṣaṇa-veṣa-janitena śivasya hasanena gaurī-hṛdayānurāgasya prakāśanān narma ।
pārvatī pratimukhaṃ nipātitam । priye vidyud āhatam iva ।। atra pati-mukha-darśana-kriyā-janitena śivasya hāsena gaurī-hṛdayānurāga-nivedanān narma । priyāparādha-nirbhedo' py uktas tredhā tathā budhaiḥ ।। ācā priyāparādha-nirbhedād, yathā mālavikāgnimitre prathamāṅke' nte devī-
jai rāa-kajjesu īrisī ṇiuṇadā ayya-uttassa tadā sohaṇaṃ habe ।। atra īdṛśī nipuṇatā yadīti caturokti-parihāsena tvayaiva mālavikā-darśanena nāṭyācaryayor vivādaḥ saṃvihita iti priyāparādhoghāṭanān narma । tan-mālyaṃ vyapanīyatāṃ ravi-kara-sparśair ivāmarditam । cāṭūktāni bhavanti hanta kṛtināṃ modāya bhogād api ।।
atra svedodgama-mālya-mlānatvayor druta-gamana-ravi-kara-sparśa-rūpa-kāraṇāsatyatva-kathana-rūpeṇa parihasanena sapatnī-sambhoga-rūpa-priyāparādha-nirbhedanān narma । tad-vṛttānta-nirīkṣaṇe kṛta-namaskāro vilakṣaḥ sthitaḥ । utsṛṣṭo guru-sannidhāv api vidhir dvābhyāṃ na kālocitaḥ ।। atha vilakṣa-sthiti-śirodhūnana-ceṣṭayā priyāparādha-nirbhedanān narma ।
śuddha-hāsyajam apy uktaṃ tadvad eva tridhā budhaiḥ ।। tarjanyā viṣa-karburān gaṇayataḥ saṃspṛśya dantāṅkurān । vācaḥ śakti-dharasya śaiśava-kalāḥ kurvantu vo maṅgalam ।। cāmuṇḍā-karatāla-kuṭṭita-layaṃ vṛtte vivāhotsave ।
tenādyāpi mayi prabhuḥ sa jagatām āste prasādonmukhaḥ ।। atra bhṛṅgi-riṭi-veṣeṇa śivayor hasitāvirbhāvāc chuddha-hāsyajam । yaḥ śṛṅgāro rahasi purataḥ patyur āviṣkṛto' bhūt । krīḍā-nṛtyair vikaṭa-gatibhir vyañjayan kuñjarāsyaḥ ।।
hāsyād bhayena janitāj janitaṃ bhaya-hāsyajam । tad dvidhā mukham aṅgaṃ tu tad dvayaṃ pūrvavat tridhā ।। ghorārāvam abhidrutasya vikaṭaiḥ paścāt padair gacchataḥ । dṛṣṭvā bhṛṅgiriṭer daśāṃ paśupatiḥ smerānanaḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
atra bhṛṅgiriṭer vikṛtākāreṇa vikaṭa-paścād-gamanena pāhi pāhi pāhīty atra varṇa-vyatyāsa-bhāṣaṇena janitasya paśupati-hāsasyānya-rasānaṅgatayā mukhyaṃ bhaya-hāsyajam । vidūṣakaḥ-kahaṃṇa kido pasādo devīe ja ajjaṃ biakkhada-sarīrā ciṭṭhahma । rājā -dhiṅ mūrkha ! kim evam upahasasi ? tvat-kṛta evāyam āpatito' smākam anartha-kramaḥ ।। pāṇi-grahe bhujaga-kaṅkaṇa-bhīṣitāyāḥ ।
ardhokti-sasmita-nataṃ mukham ambikāyāḥ ।। atra bhujaga-kaṅkaṇa-lakṣaṇena veṣeṇa janitasya pārvatī-bhaya-hāsyāsya śṛṅgārāṅgatayā kathanāt tad idam aṅgaṃ bhaya-hāsyajam । asmād iti dhvanita-narmasu gopikāsu । līlā-mṛdu stana-taṭeṣu nakhāṅkurāṇi vyāpārayann avatu vaḥ śikhi-piccha-mauliḥ ।।
atra nakhāṅkura-vyāpāreṇa janitasya gopikā-hasitasya prahlāda-vatsaleti caturokti-rūpasya śṛṅgārāṅgatayā tad idam aṅgaṃ bhaya-hāsyajam । agrāmya-narma-nirmāṇa-vedinā siṃha-bhūbhujā । narmāṣṭādaśadhā bhinnam eva sphuṭam udāhṛtam ।। narma-sphañjaḥ sukhodyogo bhayānto nava-saṅgame ।। athā-
kara-sparśārambha-prakalita-dukūlānta-śayanam । ahalyā-sutrāmṇoḥ kṣaṇikam iva tat saṅgatam abhūt ।। narma-sphoṭas tu bhāvāṃśaiḥ sūcito' lpa-raso bhavet । anyais tv akāṇḍe sambhoga-viccheda iti gīyate ।। ādyo yathā-
yātaṃ yac ca nitambayor gurutayā mandaṃ vilāsād iva । sarvaṃ tat kila mat-parāyaṇam aho kāmī svatāṃ paśyatī ।। atra sarvaṃ tat kilety aniścayenānurāgasya svalpa-mātra-sūcanayā narma-sphoṭatvam । prāptā katham api daivāt kaṇṭham anītaiva sā prakaṭa-rāgā ।
ratnāvalīva kāntā mama hastād bhraṃśitā bhavatā ।। atra vidūṣaka-vākya sūcita-devī-śaṅkā-visṛṣṭa-sāgarikā-hastena rājñā akāṇḍe tvayā sambhoga-bhaṅgaḥ kṛta ity uktatvāt narma-sphoṭaḥ । netur vā nāyikāyā vā vyāpāraḥ svārtha-siddhaye । pracchādana-paro yas tu narma-garbhaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ।। athā-
sakhī-varge gūḍhaṃ kṛtavasatir utthāya sahasā । priyāntām āliṅgan harir arati-khedaṃ haratu vaḥ ।। atra kupitāyāḥ śriyaḥ prasādanārthaṃ puruṣottamena pracchanna-sthityādi-rūpo vyāpāraḥ kṛta ity ayaṃ narma-garbhaḥ । pūrva-sthito vipadyeta nāyako yatra cāparas tiṣṭhet ।
tam apīha narma-garbhaṃ pravadati bharato hi nāṭya-veda-guruḥ ।। athā- mayena nirmitāṃ laṅkāṃ labdhvā mandodarīm api । reme mūrtāṃ daśagrīva-lakṣmīm iva vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। atra rāvaṇe vipanne tat-padābhiṣiktena vibhīṣaṇena mandodaryādiṣu tad ucitaṃ karma nirmitam ity ayaṃ narma-garbhaḥ । kecit tv etad ārabhaṭī-bhedaṃ saṅkṣiptim āhuḥ । tatra mūlaṃ na jānīmaḥ ।
māyendra-jāla-pracurāṃ citra-yuddha-kriyā-mayīm । chedyair bhedyaiḥ plutair yuktāṃ vṛttim ārabhaṭīṃ viduḥ ।। aṅgāny asyās tu catvāri saṅkṣiptir avapātanam । vastūtthāpana-sampheṭāv iti pūrve babhāṣire ।।
saṅkṣipta-vastu-viṣayā yā māyāśilpa-yojitā । sā saṅkṣiptir iti proktā bharatena mahātmanā ।। athā anargha-rāghave- paścād enaṃ drutam anusaraty eṣa vatsaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ । dhig dhik kaṣṭaṃ prathayati nnijām ākṛtiṃ rāvaṇo' yam ।।
atra bahu-vidhāno māyānāṃ saṅkṣepeṇa kathanāt saṅkṣiptiḥ । vadanty anye tu tāṃ netur avasthāntara-saṅgatim ।। tad adya dṛṣṭvā tava dhāma vaiṣṇavam । cirasya kañcil laghimānam aśnute ।।
atra rāmabhadra-sahavāsena parihṛta-dhīroddhata-vikārasya jāmadagnyasya dhīra-śāntāvasthā-parigrahāt saṅkṣiptir iti । parivartaka-bhedatvāt tad upekṣāmahe vayam ।। thāvapātanam - vibhrāntir avapātaḥ syāt praveśa-drava-vidravaiḥ ।। chittvā droṇa-sutasya kārmuka-latāṃ kṛtvā visaṃjñaṃ kṛpam ।
tvat-putro bhaya-vidravat-kurupateḥ panthānam anvety ayam ।। tad-vastūtthāpanaṃ yat tu vastu māyopakalpitam ।। b saumitre drutam āryaputra cakitāṃ māṃ pāhi pāhīti ca । kaṇṭhe kaitava-maithilīṃ kupita-dhīś ciccheda tucchāśayaḥ ।।
atra nikumbhilāyām abhicāraṃ cikīrṣuṇā indrajitā rāghavādi-buddhi-pramoṣaṇārthaṃ māyā-kalpita-maithilī-kaṇṭha-khaṇḍanaṃ kṛtam iti vastūtthāpanam । sampheṭas tu samāghātaḥ kruddha-saṃrabdhayor dvayoḥ ।। tāv eva sūtau rathinau ca kaucit । bhagnāyudhau bāhu-vimarda-niṣṭhau ।।
āsāṃ ca madhye vṛttīnāṃ śabda-vṛttis tu bhāratī । tisro' rtha-vṛttayaḥ śeṣās tac-catasro hi vṛttayaḥ ।। anye tu miśraṇād āsāṃ miśrāṃ vṛttiṃ ca pañcamīm । aśeṣa-rasa-sāmānyāṃ manyante lakṣayanti ca ।।
miśratvam āśritya mithaḥ prathante । sādhāraṇīm artha-catuṣṭayasya ।। iti । tan vicāra-saham । kutaḥ ? tat kiṃ vṛtti-dharmāṇāṃ miśraṇam aikya-rūpeṇa nyūnādhika-bhāvena vā । na prathamaḥ avaiṣamyeṇa miśraṇābhāvāt । tathā miśraṇe tu miśra-vṛtti-vyaṅgyo raso' pi miśro nyūnādhikaḥ prasajyeta । vṛttīnāṃca rasa-viśeṣa-niyamasya vakṣyamāṇatvāt । nanu miśrā vṛttiḥ sarva-rasa-sādhāraṇīti cet, na । bhāratyā vṛttyā apahṛta-viṣayatvāt । mūla-pramāṇābhāvena svokti-mātratvāc ca । nāpi dvitīyaḥ । vaiṣamyeṇa vṛtti-guṇānāṃ miśraṇe yatra yad-vṛtti-pratyabhijñā-hetu-bhūtā bahavo guṇā lakṣyante tatra saiva vṛttir iti niścayāt । nanu, tatra prakaraṇādi-vaśena rasa-viśeṣa-vyaktir iti cet tarhi prastuta-rasānurodhenaiva vṛtti-viśeṣa-nirdhāraṇam apy aṅgīkartavyam eva । tathā ca bharataḥ- bhāvo vāpi raso vāpi pravṛttir vṛttir eva vā ।
sarveṣāṃ samavetānāṃ rūpaṃ yasya bhaved bahu । sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇo matāḥ ।। iti । kaiśikī syāt tu śṛṅgāre rase vīre tu sātvatī । radura-bībhatsayor vṛttir niyatārabhaṭī punaḥ ।
śṛṅgārādiṣu sarveṣu raseṣv iṣṭaiva bhāratī ।। tac ca śṛṅgārādi-grahaṇaṃ taj-janyānāṃ hāsyādīnām apy upalakṣaṇam । ataś ca śṛṅgāra-hāsyayoḥ kaiśikī । vīrādbhutayoḥ sāttvatī । raudra-karuṇayor bībhatsa-bhayānakayoś ca ārabhaṭīti niyamaḥ pratīyate । tathā ca bharataḥ- śṛṅgāraṃ caiva hāsyaṃ ca vṛttiḥ syāt kaiśikī śritā । sāttvatī nāma vijñeyā raudra-vīrādbhutāśrayā ।। bhayānake ca bībhatse raudre cārabhaṭī bhavet ।
bhāratī cāpi vijñeyā karuṇābhuta-saṃśrayā ।। Variant found in KLJoshi edition hāsya-śṛṅgāra-bahulā kaiśikī paricakṣitā । sātvatī cāpi vijñeyā vīrādbhuta-śamāśrayā । raudre bhayānake caiva vijñeyārabhaṭī budhaiḥ । bībhatse karuṇe caiva bhāratī samprakīrtitā ।। atra sātvatyā raudrānupraveśa-kathanaṃ raudra-pratibhaṭasya yuddha-vīrasyaiva saṃlāpādibhiḥ sātvatī-bhedaiḥ paripoṣaṇaṃ na tu dāna-vīra-dayā-vīrayor iti jñāpanārtham । tasmān na niyama-virodhaḥ । bhāratyāś ca karuṇādbhuta-viṣayatva-kathanaṃ tayoḥ prāyeṇa vāg-ārambha-mukhena paripoṣa iti jñāpanārtham । tena bhāratyāḥ sarva-rasa-sādhāraṇayam upapannam eva । kecit tu tam imaṃ ślokaṃ bhāratīyaṃ niyāmakam ।
prāyikābhiprāyatayā vyācakṣāṇā vicakṣaṇāḥ । āsāṃ raseṣu vṛttīnāṃ niyamaṃ nānumanvate ।। śṛṅgāra-hāsya-karuṇa-rasātiśaya-siddhaye । eṣā vṛttiḥ prayatnena prayojyā rasa-kovidaiḥ ।।
Śṛṅgāra-tilaka reading śṛṅgāra-hāsya-karuṇa-rasānāṃ parivṛddhaye । eṣā vṛttiḥ paryoktavyā prayatnena budhair yathā ।। vicāra-sundaro naiṣa mārgaḥ syād ity udāsmahe । kaiśikī-vṛtti-bhedānāṃ narmādīnāṃ prakalpanam ।। yatra karuṇam āśritya rasābhāsatva-kāraṇam ।
rasābhāsa-prakaraṇe vakṣyate tad idaṃ sphuṭam ।। tat-tan-nyāya-pravīṇena nyāya-mārgānuvartinā । darśitaṃ siṃha-bhūpena spaṣṭaṃ vṛtti-catuṣṭayam ।। tat-tad-deśocitā bhāṣā kriyā veṣā pravṛttayaḥ ।
tatra bhāṣā dvidhā bhāṣā vibhāṣā ceti bhedataḥ ।। tatra bhāṣā sapta-vidhā prācyāvantyā ca māgadhī । bāhlīkā dākṣiṇātyā ca śaurasenī ca mālavī ।। saptadhā syād vibhāṣādi śabara-dramilāndhrajāḥ ।
śakārābhīra-caṇḍāla-vanecara-bhavā iti ।। bhāṣā-vibhāṣāḥ santy anyās tat-tad-deśa-janocitāḥ । tāsām anupayogitvān nātra lakṣaṇam ucyate । tat-tad-deśocitā veṣāḥ kriyāś cātisphuṭāntarāh ।।
anyeṣāṃ sukha-duḥkhādi-bhāveṣu kṛta-bhāvanam । ānukūlyena yac cittaṃ bhāvakānāṃ pravartate ।। sattvaṃ tad iti vijñeyaṃ prājñaiḥ sattvodbhavān imān । sāttvikā iti jānanti bharatādi-maharṣayaḥ ।।
sarveṣām api bhāvānāṃ yaiḥ sva-sattvaṃ hi bhāvyate । te bhāvā bhāva-tattva-jñaiḥ sāttvikā samudīritāḥ ।। te stambha-sveda-romāñcāḥ svara-bhedaś ca vepathuḥ । vaivarṇyam aśru-pralayāv ity aṣṭau parikīrtitāḥ ।।
stambho harṣa-bhayāmarṣa-viṣādādbhuta-sambhavaḥ । anubhāvā bhavanty ete stambhasya muni-saṃmatāḥ । saṃjñā-virahitatvaṃ ca śūnyatā niṣprakampatā ।। nidāgha-harṣa-vyāyāma-śrama-krodha-bhayādibhiḥ ।
svedaḥ sañjāyate tatra tv anubhāvā bhavanty amī । svedāpanayavātecchā-vyajana-grahaṇādayaḥ ।। nijair vivasvān vikacodarebhyaḥ । svedāpadeśān makaranda-bindūn ।।
dhūnvan śirojān karajaiḥ priyāyāḥ । svinnāntarān eva cakāra kaścit ।। atrobhayor anyonya-sparśa-harṣeṇa svedaḥ । krāmann ūru-druma-bhuja-latāḥ pūrṇa-nābhi-hradāntaḥ ।
svedāpūro yuvati-saritāṃ prāpa gaṇḍa-sthalāni ।। atra kusumāpacaya-paryaṭanena vyāyāmena svedaḥ । vātāya vātāyana-saṃśritānām । sambhogam abhoruha-locanānām ।।
ādi-śabdād gīta-nṛtya-śrānty-ādayaḥ । kiṃcit samucchvāsita-patra-lekham । priyā-mukhaṃ kiṃpuruṣaś cucumbe ।। sveda-bhinna-tilakaṃ pariśramāt ।
atyajīvad amarālakeśvarau ।। dadhat sandhyāruṇa-vyoma-sphurat-tārānukāriṇīḥ । dviṣad-dveṣoparaktāṅga-saṅginīḥ sveda-vipruṣaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā yadīyāṃ trasatām arīṇām ।
mānoṣmaṇām ātanute praśāntim ।। romāñco vismayotsāha-harṣādyais tatra vikriyāḥ । romodgamolluka-sanagātra-saṃsparśanādayaḥ ।। prauḍhim ājagava-bhañjanodbhaṭam ।
romaharṣaṇam abhūt pinākinaḥ ।। svādhīna-vraṇitāṅga-śastra-vivare romodgamaṃ varmayan । dhanyoddāma-jaya-śriyaḥ pṛthu-raṇa-stambhe patākāyate ।। atrotsāhena romāñcaḥ ।
vara-śriyaṃ vīkṣitum utsukāni । udgrīvikādānam ivān bhūvan ।। vaisvaryaṃ sukha-duḥkhādyais tatra syur gadgadādayaḥ ।। sakhīṃ vacobhiḥ kila sā tatarja ।
bhūyo babhūvuḥ svara-vaikṛtāni ।। atra priya-saṃsmaraṇa-janitena harṣeṇa bhūyo vaisvaryam । sahajām apy apahāya dhīratām । bhajate kaiva kathā śarīriṣu ।।
vepathur harṣa-santrāsa-jarā-krodhādibhir bhavet । tatrānubhāvāḥ sphuraṇa-gātra-kampādayo matāḥ ।। pita sa-bāṇa-vraṇam āmamarśa । prasūḥ karābhyāṃ bhaya-kampitābhyām ।।
vadhveva gāḍham anayā jarayopagūḍhaḥ । gantuṃ padād api padaṃ gadituṃ ca nālam ।। na kevalaṃ tasya vapuś cakampe । nipātitolkā ca sa-tārakā dyauḥ ।।
viṣādātaparoṣādyair vaivarṇyam upajāyate । mukha-varṇa-parāvṛtti-kārśyādyās tatra vikriyāḥ ।। śara-kāṇḍa-pāṇḍu-gaṇḍa-sthalīyam ābhāti parimitābharaṇā । mādhava-pariṇata-patrā katipaya-kusumeva kundalatā ।।
atra viraha-janitena viṣādena pāṇḍutvam । āyāsād aviśad alocanotpalānām । uṣṇāṃśu-dyuti-janitaḥ kapola-rāgaḥ ।। kadā mukhaṃ vara-tanu kāraṇād ṛte tavāgataṃ kṣaṇam ayi kopa-pātratām ।
aparvaṇi graha-kaluṣendu-maṇḍalā vibhāvarī kathaya kathaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। viṣāda-roṣa-santoṣā-dhūmādyair aśru tat-kriyāḥ । bāṣpa-bindu-parikṣepa-netra-saṃmārjanādayaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ te caraṇa-patitaṃ yāvad icchāmi kartum ।
krūras tasminn api na sahate saṅgamaṃ nau kṛtāntaḥ ।। sakhyaṃ saroja-śaśinoḥ sahasā babhūva । indīvara-dvayam avāpa tuṣāra-dhārām ।। atra sāparādha-priya-darśana-janitena roṣeṇa mugdhāyā bāṣpodgamaḥ ।
tayor aśītaṃ śiśiro bibheda । himādri-niṣyanda ivāvatīrṇaḥ ।। atra cira-proṣita-pratyāgata-rāma-lakṣmaṇa-darśanānandena kausalyā-sumitrayor bāṣpaḥ । dhūmāvilair udgata-bāṣpa-leśaiḥ ।
ayatna-karṇābharaṇair apāṅgaiḥ ।। atra vivāha-dhūmena lakṣmyā bāṣpodgamaḥ । pralayo duḥkha-dhātādyaiś ceṣṭā tatra visaṃjñatā ।। uḥkhena, yathā- nipatantī patim apy apātayan ।
saha dīpārcir upaiti medinīm ।। atrendumatī-vipatti-janitena duḥkhenājasya pralayaḥ । pratiprahārākṣamam aśvasādī । pratyāśvasantaṃ ripum ācakāṅkṣa ।।
atra pratibhaṭa-prahāreṇāśvasādino mūrcchā । sarve' pi sattva-mūlatvād bhāvā yadyapi sāttvikāḥ । tathāpy amīṣāṃ sattvaika-mūlatvāt sāttvika-prathā ।। anubhāvāś ca kathyante bhāva-saṃsūcanād amī ।
evaṃ dvairūpyam eteṣāṃ kathitaṃ bhāva-kovidaiḥ ।। anubhāvaika-nidhinā sukhānubhava-śālinā । śrī-siṃha-bhūbhujā sāṅgam anubhāvā nirūpitāḥ ।। mac-cintāmaṇi-vedibhiḥ pariṇamed dūrān nayoccair gajam ।
siṃha-kṣmābhuji kalpa-vṛkṣa-surabhī-hasty-ādi-dānodyate ।। kāruṇye rāmabhadraṃ bhuja-bala-vibhavārohaṇe rauhiṇeyam । kandarpa-rūpa-darpe tulayati nitarāṃ siṃha-bhūpāla-candraḥ ।। ।।
kalyāṇa-dāyi bhavatāṃ bhaved bhavya-guṇākaram । kamalākucakāleya-vyañjitoraḥ-sthalaṃ mahaḥ ।। cid-acit-kṣema-kāriṇyai namaḥ śrī-parṇajādibhiḥ । vandyāyai vārdhi-nandinyai karāgrastha-payoruhe ।।
vy-abhī ity upasargau dvau viśeṣābhimukhatvayoḥ । viśeṣeṇābhimukhyena caranti sthāyinaṃ prati ।। vāg-aṅga-sattva-sūcyā jñeyās te vyabhicāriṇaḥ । taṃ cārayanti bhāvasya gatiṃ sañcāriṇo' pi ।।
unmajjanto nimajjantaḥ sthāyiny amṛta-vāridhau । ūrmivad vardhayanty enaṃ yānti tad-rūpatāṃ ca te ।। nirvedo' tha viṣādo dainyaṃ glāni-śramau ca mada-garvau । śaṅkā-trāsāvegā unmādāpasmṛtī tathā vyādhiḥ ।।
moho mṛtir ālasyaṃ jāḍyaṃ vrīḍāvahitthā ca । smṛtir atha vitarka-cintā-mati-dhṛtayo harṣa utsukatvaṃ ca ।। augryam arṣāsūyāś cāpalyaṃ caiva nidrā ca । suptir bodha itīme bhāvā vyabhicāriṇaḥ samākhyātāḥ ।।
tattva-jñānāc ca daurgatyāv āpado viprayogataḥ । īrṣyāder api saṃjātaṃ nirvedaḥ svāvamānanam ।। Another reading in some manuscripts anubhāvas tu naiṣphalya-matir nirveda ucyate । atra cintāśru-niḥśvasa-vaivarṇyocchvāsa-dīnatā ।। nyastaṃ padaṃ śirasi vidviṣatāṃ tataḥ kim ।
kalpaṃ sthitaṃ tanu-bhṛtāṃ tanubhis tataḥ kim ।। kiṃ dārair abhirūpa-rūpa-caritair ātmānukūlair api । dāridryopahataṃ yad etad akhilaṃ duḥkhāya me kevalam ।। dhriyate sveda-lavodgamo' pi te ।
dhig imāṃ deha-bhṛtām asāratām ।। yat-sambandhi-kathābhir eva satataṃ dīrghābhir asthīyate । pāpaḥ pañcavaṭīṃ vilokayatu vā gacchatv asambhāvya vā ।। atra sītā-viprayuktasya rāmasya vāg-ārambha-sūcitenātmāvamānanena nirvedaḥ pratīyate ।
syāc ced brahma-gaṇo' yam ākṛti-gaṇas tatreṣyate ced bhavān । dhiṅ maurvī-kuśa-karṣaṇolbaṇa-kiṇa-granthir mamāyaṃ karaḥ ।। atra rāmacandra-śatānanda-viṣayerṣyā-janitena dhig iti vāg-ārambha-sūcitena svātmāvamānanena jāmadagnyasya nirvedaḥ । prārabdha-kāryānirvāhād iṣṭānavāpter vipattitaḥ ।
aparādha-parijñānād anutāpas tu yo bhavet ।। viṣādaḥ sa tridhā jyeṣṭha-madhyamādhama-saṃśrayāt । sahāyānveṣaṇopāya-cintādyā uttame matāḥ ।। anutsāhaś ca vaicittyam ity ādyā madhyame matāḥ ।
adhamasyānubhāvāḥ syur vaicitryam avalokanam । rodana-śvāsita-dhyāna-mukha-śoṣādayo' pi ca ।। tat-saṅkalpopahita-jaḍima stambham abhyeti gātram । pāṇir lekhāvidhiṣu nitarāṃ vartate kiṃ karomi ।।
atra prastuta-citra-nirmāṇānirvāhān mādhavasya kiṃ karomīti vāg-ārambha-sūcitayā tad-darśanopāya-cintayā viṣādo vyajyate । yaṃ yaṃ vyatīyāya patiṃvarā sā । vivarṇa-bhāvaṃ sa sa bhūmi-pālaḥ ।। atrendumatīm ākāṅkṣatāṃ bhūmipatīnāṃ tad-anavāptyā mukha-vaivarṇyena viṣādo vyajyate ।
vaidehyāḥ praśamitam adbhutair upāyaiḥ । ālarkaṃ viṣam iva sarvataḥ prasṛptam ।। atra sītāpavāda-rūpāyā vipatter hā hā dhig iti vāg-ārambheṇa rāmasya viṣādo gamyate । sadyaḥ parimlāna-mukhāravindā ।
ity āśaśaṃśe karaṇair bāhyaiḥ ।। atra durnimittānumitāyā vipatter mukha-śoṣaṇenānubhāvena vaidehyā viṣādaḥ । tasyānviṣyan vetasa-gūḍhaṃ prabhavaṃ saḥ । tāpād antaḥ-śalya ivāsīt kṣitipo' pi ।।
hṛt-tāpa-durgatatvādyair anauddhatyaṃ hi dīnatā । tatrānubhāvā mālinya-gātra-stambhādayo matāḥ ।। sauhārdād vā vidhura iti vā mayy anukrośa-buddhyā । mābhūd evaṃ kṣaṇam api ca te vidyutā viprayogaḥ ।।
krośadbhiḥ kṣudhitari nirannapiṭharā nekṣyeta ced gehinī । ko dehīti vadet sva-dagdha-jaṭharasyārthe manasvī pumān ।। ādhi-vyādhi-jarā-tṛṣṇā-vyāyāma-suratādibhiḥ । niṣprāṇatā glānir atra kṣāmāṅga-vacana-kriyāḥ ।
kampānutsāha-vaivarṇya-nayana-bhramaṇādayaḥ ।। hṛdaya-kusuma-śoṣī dāruṇo dīrgha-śokaḥ । śaradija iva gharmaḥ ketakī-patra-garbham ।। sāvalamba-gamanā mṛdu-svanā ।
kāma-yāna-samavasthayā tulām ।। avispaṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ tirayatitarāṃ bāṣpa-salilaiḥ । jarāyāḥ sāhāyyaṃ mama hi paritoṣo' dya kurute ।। atra harṣasya jarā-sahakāritva-kathanād ubhayānubhāvair api kampādibhir jarā-glāner eva prādhānyaṃ gamyate ।
yāvan mūrchāṃ kalayati kila vyākule rāmabhadre । tāvat prāpto dadhad atibhṛtāṃ vāriṇā nairjhareṇa ।। śrama-janitānatinā śarīrakeṇa । kala-bhara-karorubhir ūrubhir dadhānaiḥ ।।
kṛṣṇena talpāvaropitā sā । jyotsnā-kṛtānandam alindam āpa ।। śramo mānasa-khedaḥ syād adhva-nṛtya-ratādobhiḥ । aṅga-mardana-niḥśvāsau pāda-saṃvāhanaṃ tathā ।।
jṛmbhaṇaṃ mandayānaṃ ca mukhanetra-vighūrṇanam । sītkṛtiś ceti vijñeyā anubhāvāḥ śramodbhavāḥ ।। sītā javāt tricaturāṇi padāni gatvā । rāmāśuṇaḥ kṛtavatī prathamāvatāram ।।
ceṭī-hasta-samarpitaika-caraṇā mañjīra-sandhitsayā । raṅga-sthānam anaṅga-sātkṛtavatī tālāvadhau tasthuṣī ।। nitānta-surata-klāntāṃ celānta-kṛta-vījanām । kāntāṃ lulita-netrāntāṃ kalaye kala-bhāṣiṇīm ।।
madas tv ānanda-saṃmoha-sambhedo madirākṛtaḥ । sa tridhā taruṇo madhyo' pakṛṣṭaś ceti bhedataḥ ।। dṛṣṭiḥ smerā mukhe rāgaḥ sasmitākulitaṃ vacaḥ । lalitāviddha-gaty-ādyāś ceṣṭāḥ syus taruṇe made ।।
kauśalaṃ dṛśi vikāra-viśeṣāḥ । kāmineva taruṇena madena ।। madhyame tu made vāci skhalanaṃ ghūrṇanaṃ dṛśoḥ । gamane vaktratā bāhvor vikṣepa-srastatādayaḥ ।।
sāditobhaya-karā parirambhe । kṣībatā bahu-guṇair anujahre ।। apakṛṣṭe tu ceṣṭāḥ syur gati-bhaṅgo visaṃjñatā । niṣṭhīvanaṃ muhuḥ śvāso hikkā chardyādayo matāḥ ।।
prāyo hikkā-vikala-vikalaṃ vākyam ardhaṃ gṛṇantyaḥ । pāyaṃ pāyaṃ bahu-vidha-madhūny eka-vīthyā kumāryaḥ ।। taruṇas tūttamādīnāṃ madhyamo madhya-nīcayoḥ । apakṛṣṭas tu nīcānāṃ tat-tan-mada-vivardhane ।।
uttama-prakṛtiḥ śete madhyo hasati gāyati । adhama-prakṛtir grāmyaṃ paruṣaṃ vakti roditi ।। neṣyatoḥ śayanam iddha-rāgayoḥ । preyasaḥ suvadanā madasya ca ।।
padeṣu caskhāla same' pi mārge । ākāśam ālambanam ālalambe ।। mada-vivasā kiṃpi kiṃpi bāharai । soūṇa sarandi pihia kaṇṇāo ।।
mada-vivaśā kim api kim api vyāharati । śrutvā saranti pihita-karṇāḥ ।।) aiśvaryādi-kṛtaḥ kaiścit māno mada itīritaḥ । vakṣyamāṇasya garvasya bheda evety udāsmahe ।।
aiśvarya-rūpa-tāruṇya-kula-vidyā-balair api । iṣṭa-lābhādinānyeṣām avajñā garva īritaḥ ।। anubhāvā bhavanty atra gurv-ājñādy-ājñā-vyatikramaḥ । anuttara-praadānaṃ ca vaimukhyaṃ bhāṣaṇe' pi ca ।।
vibhramāpahnutī vākya-pāruṣyam anavekṣaṇam । avekṣaṇaṃ nijāṅgānām aṅga-bhaṅgādayo' pi ca ।। aiśvaryam ājñā-siddhiḥ । tena yathā- sarve vārimucaḥ sametya kuruta grīṣmasya darpa-cchidām ।
drāg devasya gṛhānupeta bhavatāṃ sevā-kṣaṇo vartate ।। hemantasyāntike syāḥ prathayati davathuṃ yena te grīṣma noṣmā । devo nānya-pratāpaṃ tribhuvana-vijayī mṛṣyate śrī-daśāsyaḥ ।। caran yuvā cārutayātidṛptaḥ ।
kareṇa līlā-kalitāravindaḥ ।। bhūri-śreṣṭhika-nāma dhāma paramaṃ tatrottamo naḥ pitā । prajñā-śīla-viveka-dhairya-vinayācārair ahaṃ cottamaḥ ।। karmeti krama-śikṣitānvaya-kalā ye ke' pi tebhyo namaḥ ।
ullekhaiḥ kavayanti bilhaṇa-kavis teṣv eva saṃnahyati ।। kārāveśmani puṣpakasya haraṇaṃ yasyorjitāḥ kelayaḥ । kā ślāghā guṇa-jarjareṇa dhanuṣākṛṣṭena bhagnena vā ।। dūre tiṣṭhatu matta-kokila-rutaṃ saṃvāntu mandānilāḥ ।
sākūtair urarīkaroti taruṇī seyaṃ praṇāmāñjalim ।। śaṅkā cauryāparādhādyaiḥ svāniṣṭotprekṣaṇaṃ matam । tatra ceṣṭāmuhuḥ pārśva-darśanaṃ mukha-śoṣaṇam ।। avakuṇṭhana-vaivarṇya-kaṇṭha-sādādayo' pi ca ।
śaṅkā dvidyeyam ātmotthā parotthā ceti bhedataḥ ।। svākārya-janitā svotthā prāyo vyaṅgyeyam iṅgitaiḥ । iṅgitāni tu pakṣma-bhrū-tārakā-dṛṣṭi-vikriyāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā vyākulatārayā nigadato mithyā-prasādaṃ mukhe ।
nūtnā saiva daśā svayaṃ piśunatāṃ devī-sakhīnāṃ gatā ।। āghrāyāghrāya hastaṃ sapadi paruṣayan kiṅkiṇī-mekhalāyām । mandaṃ mandaṃ jananyāḥ parisaram ayate kūṭa-gopāla-bālaḥ ।। parotthā tu nijasyaiva parasyākāryato bhavet ।
prāyeṇākāra-ceṣṭābhyāṃ tām imām anubhāvayet । ākāraḥ sāttvikaś ceṣṭā tv aṅga-pratyaṅgajāḥ kriyāḥ ।। arotthā, yathā- vavre' nyato yad abhayaṃ sa bhavān ahaṃyuḥ । hā vatsa śāntam athavā daśakandharo' si ।।
atra garvita-rāvaṇa-kṛtena martyetarābhaya-varaṇena jātā mālyavataḥ śaṅkā marmaṇi spṛśatītyādinā vāg-ārambheṇa pratīyate । trāsas tu citta-cāñcalyaṃ vidyut-kravyāda-garjitaiḥ । tathā bhūta-bhujaṅgādyair vijñeyās tatra vikriyāḥ ।। utkampa-gātra-saṅkoca-romāñca-stambha-gadgadāḥ ।
muhur nimeṣa-vibhrānti-pārśvasthālambanādayaḥ ।। trastā ramā śārṅgiṇam āliliṅga । hrīṇeva tūrṇaṃ jaladaṃ jagāhe ।। kravyādo hiṃsra-sattvam । tasmād, yathā-
priyābhir āliṅgita-kandharāṇām । vidyādharāṇām animitta-maitrī ।। sapadi vāridharārava-bhīravaḥ । vavalire bali-recita-madhyamāḥ ।।
garjitaṃ mahāravopalakṣaṇam । tena bheryādi-dhvanir api bhavati । prayāṇa-tūrya-dhvanibhir dharāpateḥ । payodhara-dvandva-nipīḍito hariḥ ।। sā patyuḥ parivāreṇa piśācair api veṣṭitā ।
utkampamāna-hṛdayā sakhībhiḥ sambodhyata ।। pāṇi-grahe bhujaga-kaṅkaṇa-bhīṣatāyāḥ । ardhokti-sasmita-nataṃ mukham ambikāyāḥ ।। cittasya sambhramo yaḥ syād āvego' yaṃ sa cāṣṭadhā । utpāta-vāta-varṣāgni-matta-kuñjara-darśanāt ।।
priyāpriya-śruteś cāpi śatrava-vyasanād api । tatrautpātas tu śailādi-kampa-ketūdayādayaḥ ।। taj-jāḥ sarvāṅga-visraṃso vaimukhyam apasarpaṇam । viṣāda-mukha-vaivarṇya-vismayādyās tu vikriyāḥ ।।
kroḍaṃ mātuḥ kumāre viśati viṣamuciprekṣamāṇe saroṣam । kruddho' py āśliṣṭa-mūrtir ghanataram umayā pātu hṛṣṭaḥ śivo vaḥ ।। atra kailāsa-kampa-janita-pramatha-gaṇa-vismaya-kārtikeyāpasarpaṇa-kātyāyanī-sādhvasādibhir anubhāvais tat-tad-gata-sambhramātiśaya-rūpa āvego vyajyate । trastāṅgās tvaritaṃ paraspara-gṛhān abhyetya cintā-parāḥ ।
nidhyāyanti viniḥśvasanti gaṇaśo rathyā-mukheṣv āsate ।। tvarayāgamanaṃ vastra-grahaṇaṃ cāvakuṇṭhanam । netrāvamārjanādyāś ca vātāvega-bhavāḥ kriyāḥ ।। jhāṅkārī śarkarālaḥ pathiṣu viṭapināṃ skandha-kāṣaiḥ sadhūmaḥ ।
caṇḍārambhaḥ samīro vahati paridiśaṃ bhīru kiṃ sambhrameṇa ।। atra vāta-kṛta-saṃrambho vāg-ārambheṇa pratipādyate । chatra-graho' ṅga-saṅkoco bāhu-svastika-dhāvane । uṣṇāśrayaṇam ity ādyā varṣāvega-bhavāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
chāyām adhaḥ sānugatāṃ niṣevya । śṛṅgāṇi yasyātapavanti siddhāḥ ।। atra siddhānām agra-śikhara-dhāvanena sūcitaḥ । agny-āvegaḥ-bhavāś ceṣṭā vījanaṃ cāṅga-dhūnanam ।
vyatyasta-pada-vikṣepa-netra-saṅkocanādayaḥ ।। prabhraśyad-vāji-varga-bhramaṇa-niyama-navyākula-bradhna-sūtaḥ । gaṅgā-sūnu-prayukta-prathita-hutavahāstrānubhāva-prasūtaḥ ।। āvege kuñjarodbhūte satvaraṃ cāpasarpaṇam ।
vilokanaṃ muhuḥ paścāt trāsa-kampādayo matāḥ ।। dūraṃ pathi prāṇa-bhṛtāṃ gaṇena । dvipair asambādhamayām babhūve ।। kīlaṃ prayatna-paramānavadurgraheṇa ।
aśveti vidrutam anudravatāśvam anyam ।। priya-śravaṇaje hy asmin abhutthānopagūhane । prīti-dānaṃ priyaṃ vākyaṃ romaharṣādayo' pi ca ।। kumāra-janmāmṛta-saṃmitākṣaram ।
śaśiprabhaṃ chatram ubhe ca cāmare ।। apriya-śrutije' py asmin vilāpah parivartanam । ākranditaṃ ca patanaṃ parito bhramaṇādayaḥ ।। ceṣṭāḥ syuḥ śātravāvege varma-śastrādi-dhāraṇam ।
ratha-vāji-gajāroha-sahasāpakramādayaḥ ।। vācā pañcavaṭī-vane nivasatas tasyāharad rāvaṇaḥ । saumitre kva dhanur dhanur dhanur iti vyagrā giraḥ pāntu vaḥ ।। ete syur uttamādīnām anubhāvā yathocitam ।।
unmādaś citta-vibhrāntir viyogād iṣṭa-nāśataḥ । viyogaje tu ceṣṭāḥ syur dhāvanaṃ paridevanam ।। asambaddha-pralapanaṃ śayaṇaṃ sahasotthitiḥ । acetanaiḥ sahālāpo nirnimitta-smitādayaḥ ।।
prauḍhauṣmābhiśvasitam asakṛn nirgato bāṣpa-pūraḥ । prāyeṇāsyāḥ prathayatitarāṃ bhrānti-dātrīm avasthām ।। iṣṭa-nāśa-kṛte tv asmin bhasmādi-parilepanam । nṛtya-gītādi-racanā tṛṇa-nirmālya-dhāraṇam ।
cīvarāvaraṇādīni prāg-uktāś cāpi vikriyāḥ ।। bhedaḥ syāt svajaneṣu kiṃ nu śatadhā sīdanti gātrāṇi me । na śraddeyam idaṃ hi vākyam ahahā muhyanti marmāṇi me ।। dhātu-vaiṣamya-doṣeṇa bhūtāveśādinā kṛtaḥ ।
citta-kṣobhas tv apasmāras tatra ceṣṭāḥ prakampanam ।। dhāvanaṃ patanaṃ stambho bhramaṇaṃ netra-vikriyāḥ । svoṣṭha-daṃśa-bhujāsphoṭa-lālā-phenādayo' pi ca ।। gāyaṃ gāyaṃ kalita-ruditaṃ pronnamantaṃ patantam ।
bhūtāviṣṭaṃ kam api puruṣaṃ tatra vīthyām apaśyam ।। doṣa-vaiṣamyajas tv eṣa vyādhir evety udāsmahe ।। doṣodreka-viyogādyair syād vyādhir atra tu । gātra-stambhaḥ ślathāṅgatvaṃ kūjanaṃ mukha-kūṇanam ।।
srastāṅgatākṣi-vikṣepa-niḥśvāsādyās tu vikriyāḥ । saśīto dāha-yuktaḥ sa dvividhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। hanu-sañcālanaṃ bāṣpaḥ sarvāṅgotkampa-kūjane । jānu-kuñcana-romāñca-mukha-śoṣādayo' pi ca ।।
sparśena sarvāṅgaka-saṅgatena । śīta-jvaraḥ kānta ivāṅganānām ।। dāha-jvare tu ceṣṭāḥ syuḥ śīta-mālyādi-kāṅkṣaṇam । pāṇi-pāda-parikṣepa-mukha-śoṣādayo' pi ca ।।
tāmyanty antikatālavṛntanalinī-patrāṇi dehoṣmaṇā । kvāthād āśu bhavanti phenila-mukhā bhūṣāmṛṇālāṅkurāḥ ।। āpad-bhīti-viyogādyair mohaś cittasya mūḍhatā । vikriyās tatra vijñeyā indriyāṇāṃ ca śūnyatā ।
niśceṣṭatāṅga-bhramaṇa-patanāghūrṇanādayaḥ ।। prabhraśyamānābharaṇa-prasūtā । lateva sītā sahasā jagāma ।। paśyann adūrān manasāpy adhṛṣyam ।
srastaṃ śaraṃ cāpam api sva-hastāt ।। sā veṇī sa bhuja-kramo' tisaralo līlālasā sā gatiḥ । nidrā no na ratir na cāpi viratiḥ śūnyaṃ mano vartate ।। vāyor dhanañjayākhyasya viprayogo ya ātmanā ।
śarīrāvacchedavatā maraṇaṃ nāma tad bhavet ।। etac ca dvividhaṃ proktaṃ vyādhijaṃ cābhighātajam । ādyaṃ tv asādhya-hṛc-chūla-viṣūcy-ādi-samudbhavam ।। amī tatrānubhāvāḥ syur avyaktākṣara-bhāṣaṇam ।
vivarṇa-gātratā manda-śvāsādi stambha-mīlane । hikkā parijanāpekṣā-niśceṣṭendriyatādayaḥ ।। jihmāyāṃ dṛśi jīvite jigamiṣau śvāse śanaiḥ śāmyati । karṇe varṇayatād bhavārṇava-bhayād uttārakaṃ tārakam ।।
dvitīyaṃ ghāta-patana-dohodbandha-viṣādijam । tatra ghātādije bhūmi-patana-krandanādayaḥ ।। ārya-śara-pāta-vivarād udbudbuda-phenilāsra-kardamitā । apatan na calati kiṃcid vikṛtākṛtir adya vajra-nihateva ।।
viṣaṃ tu vatsanābhādyam aṣṭau vegās tad-udbhavāḥ । kārṣṇyaṃ kampo dāho hikkā phenaś ca kandhara-bhaṅgaḥ । jaḍatā mṛtir iti kathitā kramaśaḥ prathamādyā vegajāś ceṣṭāḥ ।। kaṇṭho' syā uparudhyate mama giro niryānti kṛcchrād imāḥ ।
manye' syāḥ viṣa-vega eva hi paraṃ sarvaṃ tu duḥkhaṃ mayi ।। atrākṣi-nimīlana-kaṇṭha-rodhana-niḥśvāsāyāsādibhir āraṇyikāyā viṣa-vega-janitā mṛtir avagamyate । svabhāva-śrama-sauhitya-garbha-nirbharatādibhiḥ । kṛcchrāt kriyonmukhatvaṃ yat tad ālasyam iha kriyāḥ ।।
aṅga-bhaṅgaḥ kriyā-dveṣo jṛmbhaṇākṣi-vimardane । śayyāsanaika-priyatā tandrī-nidrādayo' pi ca ।। atami tadā nitarāṃ nitambinībhiḥ । ciram api tāḥ kim uta prayāsa-bhājaḥ ।।
taj-jīmūta-muhūrta-maṇḍana-dhanuḥ-pāṇḍityam ākhaṇḍalaḥ । sarvāṅgīṇa-balī-vilupta-nayana-vyūhaḥ kathaṃ vartate ।। atra mando-vṛddhyā śakrasya sauhityam । tat-kṛtam ālasyaṃ kathaṃ vartate ity anena vāg-ārambheṇa vyajyate । āsanaika-priyasyāsyāḥ sakhī-gātrāvalambinaḥ ।
garbhālasasya vapuṣo bhāro' bhūt svāṅga-dhāraṇam ।। jāḍyam apratipattiḥ syād iṣṭāniṣṭhārthayoḥ śruteḥ । dṛṣṭer vā virahādeś ca kriyās tatrānimeṣatā । aśrutiḥ pāravaśyaṃ ca tūṣṇīm-bhāvādayo' pi ca ।।
nibaddha-dṛṣṭiḥ śithilākuloccayā । na veda puṣpeṣu ca pāṇi-pallavam ।। atra priya-vākya-śravaṇa-janita-jāḍyam animeṣatvādinā vyajyate । ehai so bi pauttho ahaṃ a kuppejja so bi aṇuṇejja ।
ia ciṃteṃtī bahuā daṭṭhūṇa piaṃ ṇa kiṃ pi sammarai ।। (eṣyati so' pi proṣitaḥ ahaṃ ca kupyeyaṃ so' py anuneṣyati । iti cintayantī vadhūr dṛṣṭvā priyaṃ na kim api saṃsmarati ।।) atra priya-darśana-janitaṃ jāḍyaṃ pūrva-cintita-kriyā-vismaraṇena vyajyate ।
āpucchantasya bahū gamiduṃ daiassa suṇia addhottim । aṇumaṃṇiduṃ na jāṇai ṇa nivāreduṃ paravasā ubaha ।। (āpṛcchamānasya vadhūr gantuṃ dayitasya śrutvā ardhoktim । anumantuṃ na jānāti na nivārayituṃ para-vaśā paśyata ।।)
sasureṇa ḍajjamāṇe gharaṇiaḍabhave ṇiuṃja-puṃjaṃmi । ṇa suṇai suṇhā suṇṇā bahuso kahidaṃ bi sasurāe ।। (śvaśureṇa dahyamāne gṛha-nikaṭa-bhave nikuñja-puñje । na śṛṇoti snuṣā śūnyā bahuśaḥ kathitam api śvaśrvā ।।)
śuśrāva noktam api śūnya-manāḥ sa kiñcit । śrutvāham ity upagato' pi na saṃviveda ।। atra sītā-viraha-janitaṃ rāvaṇasya jāḍyaṃ punaḥ-praśna-śruty-ādibhir avagamyate । akārya-karaṇāvajñā-stuti-nūtana-saṅgamaiḥ ।
pratīkārākriyādyaiś ca vrīḍatvanatidhṛṣṭatā ।। tatra ceṣṭā nigūḍhoktir ādhomukhya-vicintane । anirgamo bahiḥ kvāpi dūrād evāvaguṇṭhanam । nakhānāṃ kṛntanaṃ bhūmi-lekhanaṃ caivam ādayaḥ ।।
nādharmāya strī-vadho' pi sthito' yam । lajjāsmābhir mīlitākṣair jitaiva ।। avadhūyāribhir nītā hariṇais tulya-vṛttitām । anyonyasyāpi jihrīmaḥ kiṃ punaḥ sahavāsinām ।।
tasya saṃstūyamānasya caritārthais tapasvibhiḥ । śuśubhe vikramodagraṃ vrīḍayāvanataṃ śiraḥ ।। haṭhāśleṣaṃ vāñchaty apaharati gātrāṇi nibhṛtam । hriyā tāmyaty antaḥ prathama-parihāse nava-vadhūḥ ।।
pārthasyākṛta-śātrava-pratikṛter antaḥ śucā muhyataḥ । hā vatseti giraḥ sphuranti na punar niryānti kaṇṭhād bahiḥ ।। avahitthākāra-guptir jaihmya-prābhava-nītibhiḥ । lajjā-sādhvasa-dākṣiṇya-prāgalbhyāpajayādibhiḥ ।।
anyathā-kathanaṃ mithyā-dhairyam anyatra vīkṣaṇam । kathā-bhaṅgādayo' py asyām anubhāvā bhavanty amī ।। hradāḥ prasannā iva gūḍha-nakrāḥ । pratyarpya pūjām upadācchalena ।।
anirbhinno gabhīratvād antargūḍha-ghana-vyathaḥ । puṭa-pāka-pratīkāśo rāmasya karuṇo rasaḥ ।। parābhyūha-sthānāny api tanutarāṇi sthagayati । taṭasthaḥ svān arthān ghaṭayati ca maunaṃ ca bhajate ।।
prasveda-vāryātapam ākṣipantī । jaḍābdhi-vātāhati-kaitavena ।। cintāpahnava-sāvahittha-vadana-tvag-viprakīrṇa-smitaḥ । srag-vāsojjvala-pāṇir apy avati māṃ vatso na laṅkeśvaraḥ ।।
antaḥ-sambhṛta-matsaro' pi bhagavān ākāra-guptau kṛtī । bāṣpair eva vilocanair abhinayaty ānandam ākhaṇḍalaḥ ।। tāmbūlānayana-cchalena rabhasāśleṣo' pi saṃvighnitaḥ । ālāpo' pi na miśritaḥ parijanaṃ vyāpārayanty āntike- kāntaṃ pratyupacārataś caturayā kopaḥ kṛtārthīkṛtaḥ ।।
svāsthya-cintā-dṛḍhābhyāsa-sadṛśālokanādibhiḥ । smṛtiḥ pūrvānubhūtārtha-pratītis tatra vikriyāḥ । kampanodvahane mūrdhno bhrū-vikṣepādayo' pi ca ।। paryutsuko bhavati yat sukhito' pi jantuḥ ।
bhāva-sthirāṇi jananāntara-sauhṛdāni ।। pratyupteva ca vajra-lepa-ghaṭitevāntar-nikhāteva ca । cintā-santati-tantu-jāla-niviḍa-syūteva lagnā priyā ।। sā veṇī sa bhuja-kramo' tisaralo līlālasā sā gatiḥ ।
nidrā no na ratir na cāpi viratiḥ śūnyaṃ mano vartate ।। ārakta-rājibhir iyaṃ kusumair nava-kandalī salila-garbhaiḥ । kopād antar-bāṣpe smarayati māṃ locane tasyāḥ ।। ūho vitarkaḥ sandeha-vimarṣa-pratyayādibhiḥ ।
