janito nirṇayāntaḥ syād asatyaḥ satya eva vā । tatrānubhāvāḥ syur amī bhrū-śiraḥ- ksepaṇādayaḥ ।। sāraṅgaṃ katicic ca saṃjagadire bhūmeś ca bimbaṃ pare । tan manye ravi-bhītam andha-tamasaṃ kukṣi-stham ālakṣyate ।।
vimarśo vicāraḥ । tena, yathā- śvasitam adhikaṃ kiṃ nv etat syāt kim anyad ato' tha vā । lalita-madhurās te te bhāvāḥ kṣipanti ca dhīratām ।। atra mādhava-gatāṃ cintām upalabhya kim atra kāraṇam iti vimṛśatā makarandena manmatha-nibandhana evāyaṃ bhāva iti satya-nirṇayānto vitarkaḥ ।
iṣṭa-vastv-apariprāpter aiśvarya-bhraṃśanādibhiḥ । cintā dhyānātmikā tasyām anubhāvā bhavanty amī । kārśyādhomukhya-santāpa-niḥśvāsocchrvasanādayaḥ ।। īsi-baliābaṇaā se kūṇita-pakkhaṃtatāraa tthimiā ।
diṭṭhī kapola-pālī ṇihiā kara-pallave mano suṇṇaṃ ।। [īṣad-valitāvanatā'syāḥ kūṇita-pakṣmanta-tārakā stimitā । dṛṣṭiḥ kapola-pālī nihitā kara-pallave manaḥ śūnyam ।।] yamo' pi vilikhan bhūmiṃ daṇḍenāstamita-tviṣā ।
kurute' sminn amoghe' pi nirvāṇālāta-lāghavam ।। nānā-śāstrāratha-mathanād artha-nirdhāraṇaṃ matiḥ । tatra ceṣṭās tu kartavya-karaṇaṃ saṃśaya-chidā । śiṣyopadeśa-bhrū-kṣepāv ūhāpohādayo' pi ca ।।
dinakara-kulāskandī ko' yaṃ kalaṅka-navāṅkuraḥ । yad adhikaraṇaṃ dharma-sthīyaṃ tavaiva vacāṃsi naḥ ।। jñāna-vijñāna-gurvādi-bhakti-nānārtha-siddhibhiḥ । lajjādibhiś ca cittasya naispṛhyaṃ dhṛtir ucyate ।।
atrānubhāvā vijñeyāḥ prāptārthānubhavas tathā । aprāptātīta-naṣṭārthān abhisaṅkṣobhaṇādayaḥ ।। aśnīmahi vayaṃ bhikṣām āśāvāso vasīmahi । śayīmahi mahī-pṛṣṭhe kurvīmahi kim īśvaraiḥ ।।
vartante' pi ca tatra tatra rasikā goṣṭhīṣu saktā nṛpāḥ । vāg-devī vadanāmbuje vasati cet ko nāma dīno janaḥ ।। yat saṃvāhayataḥ sukhaṃ hi caraṇau tātasya kiṃ rājyataḥ । āyāsaḥ khalu rājyam ujjhita-guros tatrāsti kaścid guṇaḥ ।।
pāñcālyā mama durnayopajanitas tīrṇo nikārārṇavaḥ । kiṃ nāmānyad ataḥ paraṃ bhagavato yāce prasannād aham ।। manorathasya lābhena siddhyā yogyasya vastunaḥ । mitra-saṅgama-devādi-prasādādeś ca kalpitaḥ ।।
manaḥ-prasādo harṣaḥ syād atra netrāsya-phullatā । priyābhāṣaṇam āśleṣaḥ pulakānāṃ prarohaṇam । svedodgamaś ca hastena hasta-sampīḍanādayaḥ ।। nṛpasya kāntaṃ pibataḥ sutānanam ।
guruḥ praharṣaḥ prababhūva nātmani ।। pulomajā-pada-tala-yāvakair iva । mukhe nirāmiṣa-kaṭhine mamārja tam ।। atra uccaiḥśravaso lābhena devendrasya harṣaḥ ।
ibha-kumbha-tuṅga-kaṭhinetaretara- stana-bhāra-dūra-vinivāritodarāḥ । pariphulla-gaṇḍa-phalakāḥ parasparaṃ parirebhire kukura-kaurava-striyaḥ ।। mitra-saṅgamaḥ pūjyādi-saṅgamādīnām apy upalakṣaṇam । jaganti yasyāṃ savikāsam āsata ।
tapadhanābhyāgama-sambhavā mudaḥ ।। gurur nṛpāṇāṃ gurave nivedya । śaśaṃsa vācā punaruktayeva ।। ādi-śabdād guru-rāja-prasādādayaḥ । guru-prasādād, yathā-
yajvāno vayam adya te bhagavatī bhūr adya rājanvatī । yenaitāvad arundhatī-patir api svenānugṛhṇāti naḥ ।। yena tat-priya-cikīrṣavo nṛpāḥ । nādhiveśma-nihitair upāyanaiḥ ।।
kālākṣamatvam autsukyam iṣṭa-vastu-viyogataḥ । tad-darśanād ramya-vastu-didṛkṣādeś ca tat-kriyāḥ ।। tvarānavasthitiḥ śayyā-sthitir uttāna-cintane । śarīra-gauravaṃ nidrā-tandrā-niḥśvasitādayaḥ ।।
sarvāvasthāsv ahar api kathaṃ manda-mandātapaṃ syāt । gāḍhoṣmābhiḥ kṛtam aśaraṇaṃ tvad-viyoga-vyathābhiḥ ।। āyāte dayite manoratha-śatair nītvā kathañcid dinaṃ gatvā vāsa-gṛhaṃ jaḍe parijane dīrghāṃ kathāṃ kurvati । daṣṭāsmīty abhidhāya satvara-padaṃ vyādhūya cīnāṃśukaṃ tanvaṅgyā rati-kātareṇa manasā nītaḥ pradīpaḥ śamam ।।
niṣkīlitenādhvani pūritena । pura-striyaḥ śiśriyire gavākṣān ।। aparādhāvamānābhyāṃ cauryāābhigrahaṇādibhiḥ । asat-pralāpanādyaiś ca kṛtaṃ caṇḍatvam ugratā ।।
kriyās tatrāsya-nayana-rāgo bandhana-tāḍane । śirasaḥ kampanaṃ kheda-vadha-nirbhartsanādayaḥ ।। lalita-śirīṣa-puṣpa-hananair api tāmyati yat । patatu śarasy akāṇḍayam adaṇḍaṃ ivaiṣa bhujaḥ ।।
atra mālatī-nikāra-rūpāparādhād mādhavasyaugryam । vijñāpayantaṃ pratiruṣṭa-cetāḥ । yajñāśi-vairī gadayā jaghāna ।। dhig apasarasi cauraṃkāram ākruśyamānaḥ ।
kuṭila-karaja-koṭi-krūra-karmā jaṭāyuḥ ।। katham api na niṣiddho duḥkhinā bhīruṇā vā drupada-tanaya-pāṇis tena pitrā mamādya । tava bhuja-bala-darpādhyāyamānasya vāmaḥ śirasi caraṇa eṣa nyasyate vārayainam ।। adhikṣepāvamānādyaiḥ krodho' marṣa itīryate ।
tatra sveda-śiraḥ-kampāv ādhomukhya-vicintane । upāyānveṣaṇotsāha-vyavasādayaḥ kriyāḥ ।। adhigatavatām iva kṣaṇāt । atho śiśupāla-pakṣa-pṛthivī-bhṛtāṃ gaṇaḥ ।।
dhvaṃsena hṛdayaṃ sadyaḥ paribhūtasya me paraiḥ । yady amarṣaḥ pratīkāraṃ bhujālambaṃ na lambhayet ।। para-saubhāgya-sampatti-vidyā-śauryādi-hetubhiḥ । guṇe' pi doṣāropaḥ syād asūyā tatra vikriyāḥ ।
mukhāpavartanaṃ garhā bhrū-bhedānādarādayaḥ ।। kānta-svahasta-likhitā mama mañjarīti । vairī na ced bhavati vepathur antarāyaḥ ।। lokopakāriṇī lakṣmīḥ satāṃ vimala-cetasām ।
tathāpi tāṃ vilokyaiva dūyante duṣṭa-cetasaḥ ।। pratyakṣādi-prabhā-siddha-viruddhārthābhidhāyinaḥ । vedāntā yadi śāstrāṇi bauddhaiḥ kim aparāddhyate ।। pratāpe cāmitrān dahati tava siṃha-kṣitipate ।
caturdhā tejo' pi vyabhajata kaṇādo munir api ।। atra prauḍha-kavi-samaya-prasiddha-mārgānusāriṇo vaktuḥ parimita-dravya-vādini kaṇāde mahaty asūyā mūḍhatama-dhīr iti vāg-ārambheṇa vyajyate । mārīco mṛga eva bhīti-bhavanaṃ vālī punar vānaraḥ । dor-darpas tu tathāpi te yadi samaṃ ko-daṇḍam āropaya ।।
rāga-dveṣādibhiś citta-lāghavaṃ cāpalaṃ bhavet । ceṣṭās tatrāvicāreṇa parirambhāvalambane । niṣkāsanokti-pāruṣye tāḍanājñāpanādayaḥ ।। kṣaṇam atha vīkṣya vipakṣam antike' nyā ।
abhavad amuñcati vallabhe' tigurvī ।। gāḍhāmodaṃ malaya-marutaḥ śṛṅkhalādāma datta । candraṃ cūrṇīkuruta ca śilāpaṭṭake piṣṭa-bimbam ।। atra sītā-viraheṇa rāvaṇasya vasantādi-viṣaya-dveṣeṇa tat-tad-adhidevatānāṃ tāḍanā-jñāpanādibhir anubhāvaiś cāpalyaṃ dyotyate ।
mada-svabhāva-vyāyāma-niścintatva-śramādibhiḥ । mano-nimīlanaṃ nidrā ceṣṭās tatrāsya-gauravam ।। āghūrṇamāna-netratvam aṅgānāṃ parimardanam । niḥśvāsocchvāsane sanna-gātratvaṃ netra-mīlanam ।
śarīrasya ca saṅkoco jāḍyaṃ cety evam ādayaḥ ।। nidrāṃ vihārārdha-pathe gatānām । ko lambayed āharaṇāya hastam ।। anyām apy alasāṃ nidhāya vipulābhoge nitamba-sthale ।
talpotpīḍana-tiryag-unnata-kucā nidrāti śātodarī ।। aśithila-parirambhair datta-saṃvāhanāni । tvam urasi mama kṛtvā yatra nidrām avāptā ।। tvad-vṛttyā śithilīkṛtas tribhuvana-trāṇāya nārāyaṇaḥ ।
prāṇottuṅga-bhujaṅga-talpam adhunā bhadreṇa nidrāyate ।। jyotiṣām avanatāsu paṅktiṣu । netra-mīlana-kutūhalaṃ kṛtam ।। udreka eva nidrāyāḥ suptiḥ syāt tatra vikriyāḥ ।
indriyoparatir netra-mīlanaṃ srasta-gātratā । utsvapnāyitanaiś calya-śvāsocchvāsādayo' pi ca ।। nisarga-niryan-nigamānta-gandhā । śayyā-bhujaṅgendra-nipīta-śeṣāḥ ।।
svapna-sparśana-nidhvāna-nidrā-sampūrṇatādibhiḥ । prabodhaś cetanāvāptiś ceṣṭās tatrākṣi-mardanam ।। śayyāyā mokṣaṇaṃ bāhu-vikṣepo' ṅguli-moṭanam । śiraḥ-kaṇḍūyanaṃ cāṅga-valanaṃ caivam ādayaḥ ।।
nimīlya netre sahasā vyabudhyata । asatya-kaṇṭhārpita-bāhu-bandhanā ।। suptaṃ tadā tvarita-keli-bhuvā śrameṇa । prābodhayan maṇi-gavākṣa-samāgato mām ।।
paṭu-paṭaha-dhvnaibhir vinīta-nidraḥ । vihaga-vikūjita-vandi-maṅgalāni ।। te ca prāpur udanvantaṃ bubudhe cādi-pūruṣaḥ । avyākṣepo bhaviṣyantyāḥ kārya-siddher hi lakṣaṇam ।।
uttamādhama-madhyeṣu sāttvikā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca varṇanīyā yathocitam ।। udvega-sneha-dambherṣyā-pramukhāś citta-vṛttayaḥ । ukteṣv antarbhavantīti na pṛthaktvena darśitāḥ ।।
Ed adds anukta-citta-vṛttīnām uktāntarbhāvaḥ । tathā hi-para-pratāraṇa-rūpa-dambhasya jihmatāvahitthāyām antar-bhāvaḥ । citta-dravatā-lakṣaṇasya snehasya harṣe' ntarbhāvaḥ । sva-viṣaya-dāna-mānādy-amarṣaṇa-rūpāyā īrṣyāyā amarṣe' ntarbhāvaḥ । para-viṣayāyās tv asūyāyām । udvegasya tu nirveda-viṣādādiṣu yathocitam antarbhāva ity ādi draṣṭavyam । tathā ca bhāva-prakāśikā-kāraḥ- anye' pi yadi bhāvāḥ syuś citta-vṛtti-viśeṣataḥ । antarbhāvas tu sarveṣāṃ draṣṭavyo vyabhicāriṣu ।। iti ।
vibhāvāś cānubhāvāś ca te bhavanti parasparam । kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvas tu jñeyaḥ prāyeṇa lokataḥ ।। tathā hi-santāpasya dainyaṃ prati vibhāvatvaṃ glāniṃ pratyanubhāvatvaṃ ca । prahārasya pralaya-mohau prati vibhāvatvam augryaṃ pratyanubhāvatvaṃ ca । viṣādasya utpātāvegaṃ pratyanubhāvatṃ stambhaṃ prati vibhāvatvam । vyādher glāni-stambha-pralayādīn prati vibhāvatvam । svātantryāt pāratantryāc ca te dvidhā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
para-poṣakatāṃ prāptāḥ paratantrā itīritāḥ । tad-abhāve svatantrāḥ syur bhāvā iti ca te smṛtāḥ ।। syāc ced brahma-gaṇo' yam ākṛti-gaṇas tatreṣyate ced bhavān । dhiṅ maurvī-kuśa-karṣaṇolbaṇa-kiṇa-granthir mamāyaṃ karaḥ ।।
ity atra nirvedasya krodhāṅgatvam । nyastaṃ padaṃ śirasi vidviṣatāṃ tataḥ kim । kalpaṃ sthitās tanubhṛtāṃ tanavas tataḥ kim ।। ityādi । atra nirvedasyānanyāṅgatvāt svatantratvam ।
nanu nirvedasya śānta-rasa-sthāyitvaṃ kaiścid uktam । tat katham asya anya-rasopakaraṇatvam iti ced, ucyate । sati khalu grāme sīmā-sambhāvanā । sthāyitvaṃ nāma saṃskāra-pāṭavena bhāvasya muhur muhur navībhāvaḥ । tena nirveda-vāsanā-vāsitaṃ bhāvaka-cetasi naiṣphalyābhimateṣu vibhāvādiṣu tat-sāmagrī-phala-bhūtasya nirvedasyotpattir eva na saṅgacchate । kiṃ punaḥ sthāyitvam । kiṃ ca asati nirveda-sthāyini śānta-rūpo bhāvakānām āsvādaś citra-gata-kadalī-phala-rasāsvāda-lampaṭānāṃ rāja-śukānāṃ viveka-sahodaro bhaved iti kṛtaṃ saṃrambheṇa । tat-saṅkalpopahita-jaḍima-stambham abhyeti gātram । pāṇir lekhā-vidhiṣu nitarāṃ vartate kiṃ karomi ।। atra viṣādasya śṛṅgārāṅgatvam । svatantratvaṃ, yathā-
yaṃ yaṃ vyatīyāya patiṃvarā sā । vivarṇa-bhāvaṃ sa sa bhūmi-pālaḥ ।। ity atra viṣādasyānanyāṅgatvam । evam anyeṣām api svatantratva-paratantratve tatra tatrohanīye । ābhāsatā bhaved eṣām anaucitya-pravartitām ।
asatyatvād ayogyatvād anaucityaṃ dvidhā bhavet । asatyatva-kṛtaṃ tat syād acetana-gataṃ tu yat ।। kas tvaṃ bhoḥ, kathayāmi daiva-hatakaṃ māṃ viddhi śākhoṭakaṃ vairāgyād iva vakṣi, sādhu viditaṃ, kasmād idaṃ, kathyate । vāmenātra vaṭas tam adhvaga-janaḥ sarvātmanā sevate na cchāyāpi paropakāra-karaṇe mārga-sthitasyāpi me ।।
atra vṛkṣa-viśeṣatvād acetane śākhoṭake citta-vikārasyāsambhavānucito nirvedo' yam ābhāsatvam āpadyate । ayogyatva-kṛtaṃ proktaṃ nīca-tiryaṅ-narāśrayam ।। velā-taṭe prasūyethā mā bhūḥ śaṅkita-mānasā । māṃ jānāti samudro' yaṃ ṭiṭṭibhaṃ sāhasa-priyam ।।
atra yadi samudra-velāyāṃ prasūye tarhi udvela-kallola-mālābhir mamāpatyāni hṛtāni bhaveyur iti śaṅkitāyāṃ nija-gṛhiṇyāṃ kaścit ṭiṭṭibhaḥ pakṣi-viśeṣo garvāyate । tad ayaṃ garvo nīca-tiryag-gatatvād ābhāso nātīva svadate । gandhūrasya taros tale ghuṭa-puṭa-dhvānānusandhāyibhiḥ । tat-pūrvaṃ kṛṣi-karmaṇi śramavatā kṣudreṇa nidrāyate ।। utpatti-sandhi-śāvalya-śāntayo vyabhicāriṇām ।
daśāś catasras tatra utpattir bhāva-sambhavaḥ ।। evaṃ vādini devarṣau pārśve pitur adhomukhī । līlā-kamala-patrāṇi gaṇayāmāsa pārvatī ।। atra lajjāyāḥ harṣasya vā samutpattiḥ ।
sarūpam asarūpaṃ vā bhinna-kāraṇa-kalpitam । bhāva-dvayaṃ milati cet sa sandhir iti gīyate ।। khaḍga-prahārair avani gatānām । bhavanti netrānta-nimīlanāni ।।
atra nāyaka-khaḍga-prahāra-priyā-janāṅga-sparśābhyāṃ kalpitayoḥ pratināyakeṣu mohayoḥ sandhir netrānta-nimīlanena vyajyate । svidyanti gātrāny ativepitāni । priyābhir ālambita-kandharāṇām ।। atra garjiteṣu nāyaka-saṃnāha-niḥsāṇa-śaṅkayāṅkuritasya pratināyakānāṃ trāsasya priyāliṅgana-taraṅgitasya ca harṣasya sveda-vepathu-sādṛśya-kalpita-saṃśleṣaḥ sandhiḥ ।
atyārūḍhasya bhāvasya vilayaḥ śāntir ucyate ।। athā- vṛddhāmātya-hitopadeśa-vacanai ruddho' pi vṛddhiṃ gataḥ । vāhinyām anapota-siṃha-nṛpater ālokitāyām api ।। atra hitopadeśānādarādhirūḍhasya pratināyaka-gatasya garvasya śāntir āmūlam unmūlyata iti vāg-ārambheṇa vyajyate ।
śavalatvaṃ tu bhāvānāṃ saṃmardaḥ syāt parasparam ।। hantāsmāsu parāṅmukho hata-vidhiḥ kiṃ durgam adhyāsmahe । kiṃ vākyair anapota-siṃha-nṛpateḥ sevaiva kṛtyaṃ param ।। atra garva-viṣādāsūyā-cintā-smṛty-amarṣa-nirveda-matīnāṃ saṃmardo bhāva-śāvalyam ity ucyate ।
dig-antarāla-sañcāra-kīrtinā siṃha-bhūbhujā । evaṃ sañcāriṇaḥ sarve sa-prapañcaṃ nirūpitāḥ ।। iti sañcāri-bhāvāḥ । sajātīyair vijātīyair bhāvair ye tv atiraskṛtāḥ ।
kṣrābdhivan nayanty anyān svātmatvaṃ sthāyino hi te ।। bharatena ca te kathitā rati-hāsotsāha-vismaya-krodhāḥ । śoko' tha jugupsā bhayam ity aṣṭau lakṣma vakṣyate teṣām ।। yūnor anyonya-viṣayā sthāyinīcchā ratir bhavet ।
nisargeṇābhiyogena saṃsargeṇābhimānataḥ ।। upamādhyātma-viṣayair eṣā syāt tatra vikriyāḥ । kaṭākṣa-pāta-bhrū-kṣepa-priya-vāg-ādayo matāḥ ।। tathāvidhas tāvad aśeṣam astu saḥ ।
na kāma-vṛttir vacanīyam īkṣate ।। atra rūpādi-dṛṣṭa-kāraṇa-nirapekṣā pārvatyāḥ ratir janmāntara-vāsanā-rūpā nisargād eva bhavati । abhiyogo' bhiniveśaḥ । tad-eka-paratvam iti yāvat । ālokya mām agaṇita-skhalad-uttarīyā । sāśliṣṭavaty amṛta-saṃvalitair ivāṅgaiḥ ।।
atrottarīya-skhalanādi-sūcitena madayantikā-premābhiyogena makarandasya tatra ratir utpadyate । utpattir deva-yajanād brahma-vādī nṛpaḥ pitā । suprasannojjvalā mūrtir asyāṃ snehaṃ karoti me ।। atra deva-yajana-janakādi-sambandha-gauraveṇa sītāyāṃ rāmasya ratiḥ ।
atha abhimāṇaḥ । idam eva mama priyaṃ nānyad ity abhiprāyo' bhimānaḥ । tena, yathā- prakṛti-madhurāḥ santy evānye mano madayanti ye । mama tu yad iyaṃ yātā loke vilocana-candrikā nayana-viṣayaṃ janmany ekaḥ sa eva mahotsavaḥ ।। atra mādhavasya vilcana-candrikā-nayana-mahotsavādy-abhimānena itara-ramaṇīya-vastu-naiḥspṛhyeṇa ca mālatyāṃ ratiḥ ।
na sa rucira-kalāpaṃ bāṇa-lakṣyīcakāra । rati-vigalita-bandhe keśa-pāśe priyāyāḥ ।। atra mṛgayāntaritāpi daśarathasya priyā-viṣayā ratis tadīya-keśa-kalāpa-sadṛśa-keki-kalāpa-darśanenotpadyate । adhyātmaṃ svātma-prāmāṇya-mātram । tena, yathā-
kāmaṃ pratyādiṣṭāṃ smarāmi na parigrahaṃ munes tanayān । balavat tu dūyamānaṃ pratyāyayatīva me hṛdayam ।। atra duṣyantasya nija-citta-santāpa-pratyayena śāpa-vismṛtāyām api śakuntalāyāṃ ratiḥ । viṣayāḥ śabdādayaḥ । tatra śabdena, yathā mamaiva-
tad-darśanam astu vā mā vā । yadi karṇa-pathe patet tad evālam ।। atra prāg-adṛṣṭe' pi kṛṣṇe veṇu-nādena kāmavallyā ratiḥ । yad ayaṃ ratha-saṅkṣobhād aṃsenāṃso rathāṅga-suśroṇyāḥ ।
spṛṣṭaḥ saroma-vikriyam aṅkuritaṃ manobhaveneva ।। ayaṃ kāmo nāyaṃ sa tu madhumadāmodita-manāḥ । nidānaṃ bhāgyānāṃ jayati khalu siṃha-kṣitipatiḥ ।। atra rāmādi-smaraṇa-hetunā nāyaka-rūpātiśayena kasyāścid ratiḥ ।
candrodayārambha ivāmburāśiḥ । vyāpārayāmāsa vilocanāni ।। atra yadyapi sambhogāt prāg-ajñātasyādhara-rasasya rasaṃ prati vibhāvatā na saṅgacchate, tathāpi prasiddehḥ sambhāvitasya rasasyaiva vibhāvatvaṃ bimba-phalādharoṣṭha iti padena vyajyate । athavā samāsvādita-dākṣāyaṇī-bimbādharasya parameśvarasya tad-rasenaiva jananāntara-saṅgatāyām api tasyāṃ ratiḥ । ālolair ali-maṇḍalaiḥ pratipadaṃ pratyāśam āsevitaḥ ।
nāmodo' yam adṛṣṭa-pūrva-mahimā badhnāti me mānasam ।। atra parāśara-muni-prasādena labdhena divyena satyavatī-śarīra-saurabheṇa śantanos tasyāṃ ratiḥ । bhojas tu samprayogeṇa ratim anyām udāharat ।। cumbati priyatame haṭha-vṛttyā ।
jalpitaṃ jayati bāla-vadhūnām ।। vākṛtaṃ ca tenaiva । atra tarjanārthamokṣaṇārtha-vāraṇārthāṇāṃ mandaṃ maṇdaṃ prayogān mānavatyāḥ samprayoge raty-utpattiḥ pratīyata iti । samprayogasya śabdādiṣv antarbhāvān na tan-matam ।। tathā hi-uktodāharaṇe mānavatī-jalpitasya śabda-rūpatvam eva । tathā ca-
āarapasārioṭṭhaṃ aghaḍiaṇāsaṃ acuṃbiaṇiḍākaṃ । baṇṇaghialippamuhie tīe paricumbaṇaṃ bharimo ।। [ādara-prasāritoṣṭham aghaṭita-nāsam acumbita-niṭilam । varṇa-ghṛta-lipta-mukhyās tasyāḥ paricumbanaṃ smarāmaḥ ।।]
ity ādiṣu cumbanādīnām api sparśeṣv antar-bhāvaḥ । aṅkura-pallava-kalikā-praspunaphalabhoga-bhāg iyaṃ kramaśaḥ । premā mānaḥ praṇayaḥ sneho rāgo' nurāgaś ca ।। sa premā bheda-rahitaṃ yūnor yad bhāva-bandhanaṃ ।।
babhūva yat prema parasparāśrayam । parasparasyopari paryacīyata ।। atra bheda-kāraṇe suta-snehe saty api sudakṣiṇā-dilīpayo rater aparihāṇena bheda-rahitatvam । navam iva jagaj jātaṃ bhūyaś cirād abhinandatoḥ ।
prasarati kathā bahvī yūnor yathā na tathā ratiḥ ।। ] yat tu premānubandhena svātantryād dhṛdayaṅgamam । bahnāti bhāva-kauṭilyaṃ so' yaṃ māna itīryate ।। apārayantaṃ kila puṣpajaṃ rajaḥ ।
priyaṃ jaghānonnata-pīvara-stanī ।। atrāparādha-sambhāvanāyām api prema-kalpita-svātantryeṇa avajñā-rūpaṃ citta-kauṭilyam । sandhyayā praṇamito' smi nānyathā । cakravāka-sama-vṛttim ātmanaḥ ।। ]
bāhyāntaropacārair yat prema-mānopakalpitaiḥ । badhnāti bhāva-viśrambhaṃ so' yaṃ praṇaya ucyate ।। vivakṣati preyasi kuñcita-bhrūḥ । mukhaṃ pidhatte svakapolakena ।।
atra bhāva-bandhanāparādha-kauṭilyayor anuvṛttau kaṇṭhālambanādinopacāreṇa visrambhaḥ । mugdhākṣī svapitīti tat-parijanaṃ svairaṃ priye pṛcchati । paryasya svapana-cchalena śayane datto' vakāśas tayā ।। ] viśrambhe paramāṃ kāṣṭhām ārūḍhe darśanādibhiḥ ।
yatra dravaty antaraṅgaṃ sa sneha iti kathyate ।। kaduṣṇa-niḥśvāsa-cariṣṇukena । rāgoṣmaṇaiva dravatām anaiṣīt ।। atra lakṣmī-nārāyaṇayor anyonya-darśanenāntaḥ-karaṇa-dravībhāvaḥ ।
sāndra-sneha-rasātireka-vigalat-śrīman-nitambāmbarā । suptā kiṃ nu mṛtā nu kiṃ manasi me līnā vilīnā nu kim ।। sa tredhā kathyate prauḍha-madhya-manda-vibhedataḥ । pravāsādibhir ajñāta-citta-vṛttau priye jane ।
itara-kleśa-kārī yaḥ sa prauḍhaḥ sneha ucyate ।। mā kaulīnād asita-nayane mayy aviśvāsinī bhūḥ । iṣṭe vastuny upacita-rasāḥ prema-rāśī bhavanti ।। atra proṣite yakṣe sneha-janitayā tad-anyāsaṅga-śaṅkayā janitaḥ priyā-kleśaḥ mayy aviśvāsinī mā bhūr iti pratyāśvāsanena vyajyate ।
itarānubhavāpekṣāṃ sahate yaḥ sa madhyamaḥ ।। kiṃ vā sāgarikāṃ kramoddhata-ruṣā santarjyamānāṃ tathā । sarvākāra-kṛta-vyathaḥ kṣaṇam api prāpnomi no nirvṛtim ।। atra sāgarikānubhavāpekṣayā rāja-sneho vāsavadattāyāṃ madhyamaḥ ।
dvayor ekasya mānādau tad anyasya karoti yaḥ । naivopekṣāṃ na cāpekṣāṃ sa sneho manda ucyate ।। manye priyāhṛtamanās tasyāḥ praṇipāta-laṅghanaṃ sevām । evaṃ hi praṇayavatī sā śakyam upekṣituṃ kupitā ।।
atra kupitāyām irāvatyām upekṣāpekṣābhāvasya kathanena rājñaḥ snehas tad-viṣayo mandaḥ । ādi-śabdād atiparicayādayaḥ । yathā- revā-rodhasi vetasī-taru-tale cetaḥ samutkaṇṭhate ।। atra kasyāścit svairiṇyā gṛhiṇītva-paricayena pati-daśāṃ prāpte' pi jāre upekṣāpekṣayor abhāva-kathanān mandaḥ snehaḥ । duḥkham apy adhikaṃ citte sukhatvenaiva rajyate ।
yena sneha-prakarṣeṇa sa rāga iti gīyate ।। kusumbha-nīlī-mañjiṣṭha-rāga-bhedena sa tridhā । kusumbha-rāgaḥ sa jñeyo yaś citte rajyati kṣaṇāt । atiprakāśamāno' pi kṣaṇād eva vinaśyati ।।
bahu-ballahassa jā hoi ballahā kahabi pañjadi ahāiṃ । sā kiṃ chaṭṭhaṃ maggaī katto miṭṭhaṃ a bahuaṃ a ।। [bahu-vallabhasya yā bhavati vallabhā katham api pañca-divasāni । sā kiṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ mṛgayate kuto mṛṣṭaṃ ca bahukaṃ ca ।।]
nīlī-rāgas tu yaḥ sakto nāpaiti na ca dīpyate ।। sā dakṣa-roṣāt sudatī sasarja । patiḥ paśūnām aparigraho' bhūt ।। atra paśupati-citta-rāgaḥ satī-saṅgamābhāva-niścayenāpi nāpaiti । viṣayābhāvān na prakāśate ca ।
acireṇaiva saṃsaktaś cirād api na naśyati । atīva śobhate yo' sau māñjiṣṭho rāga ucyate ।। viśrāmo hṛdayasya yatra jarasā yasminn ahāryo rasaḥ । bhadraṃ tasya sumānuṣasya katham apy ekaṃ hi tat prāpyate ।।
rāga eva svayaṃ vedya-daśā-prāptyā prakāśitaḥ । yāvad-āśraya-vṛttiś ced anurāga itīritaḥ ।। aśrānta-kaṇṭhakodgamam anavarata-svedam aviratotkampam । aniśa-mukulitāpāṅgaṃ mithunaṃ kalayāmi tad-avinābhūtam ।।
atra pārvatī-parameśvarayo ratiḥ śarīraikya-sambandhena yāvad-āśraya-vṛttiḥ anubhūta-sarva-rāgopaplavatayā sva-saṃvedya-daśā-prakāśita-nitya-bhoga-rūpā aśrānta-romāñcādibhir anubhāvair vyajyate । anye prītiṃ rater bhedm āmananti na tan-matam । asamprayoga-viṣayā seyaṃ harṣān na bhidyate ।। bhāṣaṇākṛti-veṣāṇaṃ kriyāyāś ca vikārataḥ ।
laulyādeś ca parasthānām eṣām anukṛter api ।। vikāraś cetaso hāsas tatra ceṣṭāḥ samīritāḥ । dṛṣṭer vikāro nāmauṣṭha-kapola-spandanādayaḥ ।। bhāṣā-vikāro bhāṣaṇāsambaddhatvādiḥ । ākṛti-vikṛtir ativāmana-danturatvādiḥ । veṣa-vikāro viruddhālaṅkāra-kalpanā । kriyā-vikāro vikaṭa-gatitvādiḥ । eṣām udāharaṇāni kaiśikyāṃ śuddha-hāsyaje narmaṇi nirūpitāni draṣṭavyāni ।
etābhir agni-śaraṇeṣu sadharmiṇībhiḥ । āghrātum icchati mṛge munayo hasanti ।। atra mṛgāṇāṃ santrāsana-yaṣṭi-samāghrāṇa-laulyena munīnāṃ hāsaḥ । ta ta tyaja du du drutaṃ bha bha bha bhājanaṃ kāñcanam ।
prage hasita-hetave sahacarībhir adhyaiyata ।। śaktir dhariya-sahāyādyaiḥ phala-ślāghyeṣu karmasu । satvarā mānasī vṛttir utsāhas tatra vikriyāḥ ।। kālādyavekṣaṇaṃ dhairyaṃ vāg-ārambhādayo' pi ca ।
sahajāhārya-bhedena sa dvidhā paribhāṣyate ।। vārāṃ nidhiṃ laṅghayituṃ hanūmān । kara-sthitāṃ rāghava-kārya-siddhim ।। nidrāṇeṣu ca vidravatsu kapiṣu prāptāvakāśe dviṣi ।
saumitrer adhiyuddha-bhūmi gaditā vācas tvayā na śrutāḥ ।। atra rāvaṇa-śakti-prahāreṇa kṣīṇa-śakter api lakṣmaṇasya dhairya-janitotsāhaḥ kapi-bhaṭāśvāsanādibhir vyajyate । sa gupta-mūla-prayatnaḥ śuddha-pārṣṇir ayānvitaḥ । ṣaḍ-vidhaṃ balam ādāya pratasthe vijigīṣayā ।।
srastaṃ bhrū-yugam unnamayya racitaṃ yajñopavītena ca । dṛṣṭaṃ bho janakasya yogina idaṃ dāntaṃ viraktaṃ manaḥ ।। sahāyam ekaṃ madhum eva labdhvā । dhairya-cyutiṃ ke mama dhanvino' nye ।।
atra svabhāva-śakti-rahitasya manmathasya indra-protsāhana-janitena dhairyeṇa vasanta-sahāyena cāhṛtotsāho dhairya-cyuti-cikīrṣā-kathanād abhivyajyate । lokottara-padārthānāṃ tat-pūrva-lokanādibhiḥ । vistāraś cetaso yas tu vismayaḥ sa nigadyate । kriyās tatrākṣi-vistāra-sādhūkti-pulakādayaḥ ।।
aho nārīcchāyām ayati vanitābhūyam ayate । sthale kṛtvā baddhvā kaca-bharam udasthād ṛṣi-vadhūḥ ।। vadhāvajñādibhiś citta-jvalanaṃ krodha īritaḥ । eṣa tridhā bhavet kordha-kopa-roṣa-prabhedataḥ ।।
vadha-cchedādi-paryantaḥ krodhaḥ krūra-janāśrayaḥ । abhyarthanāvadhiḥ prāyaḥ kopo vīra-janāśrayaḥ ।। śatru-bhṛtya-suhṛt-pūjyāś catvāro viṣayās tayoḥ । muhur daṣṭoṣṭhatā bhugna-bhrukuṭī-danta-ghaṭṭanam ।।
hasta-niṣpīḍanaṃ gātra-kampaḥ śastra-pratīkṣaṇam । sva-bhujāvekṣaṇaṃ kaṇṭha-garjādyāḥ śātrava-krudhi ।। manuja-paśubhir nirmaryādair bhavadbhir udāyudhaiḥ । ayam aham asṛṅ-medo-māṃsaiḥ karomi diśāṃ balim ।।
paśupatim avamantuṃ ceṣṭate yasya buddhiḥ । śirasi caraṇam enaṃ pātayāmi tri-vāram ।। atra parameśvarāvajñayā janito dakṣa-viṣayo dadhīci-krodhaḥ paruṣa-vāg-ārambheṇa vyajyate । bhṛtya-krodhe tu ceṣṭāḥ syus tarjanaṃ mūrdha-dhananam ।
nirbhartsanaṃ ca bahudhā muhur nirvarṇanādayaḥ ।। rūkṣekṣaṇaṃ paruṣa-huṅkṛti-garbha-kaṇṭham । saudhāt plavaṅga-pati-muṣṭi-hato daśāsyaḥ ।। atra sugrīva-sampāte palāyiteṣu bhṛtyeṣu rāvaṇasya krodho mūrdha-dhūnanādibhir anubhāvair vyajyate ।
mitra-krodhe vikārāḥ syur netrāntaḥ-patad-aśrutā । tūṣṇīṃ dhyānaṃ ca naiścalyaṃ śvasitāni muhur muhuḥ । maunaṃ vinamra-mukhatā bhugna-dṛṣṭyādayo' pi ca ।। kṛtaṃ kaunteyena kṣubhita-manasaḥ stabdha-vapuṣaḥ ।
apaśyann udbāṣpair yadu-patim apāṅgair yadu-bhaṭāḥ ।। atra subhadrā-haraṇānumatyā janitaḥ kṛṣṇa-viṣayo yadūnāṃ krodhaḥ kuṭila-vīkṣaṇādibhir vyajyate । pūjya-krodhe tu ceṣṭāḥ syuḥ sva-nindā namra-vaktratā । anuttara-pradānāṅga-sveda-gadgadikādayaḥ ।।
rūkṣaṃ vivakṣur api gadgadikāṃ dadhānaḥ । jajvāla cetasi paraṃ bharato mahātmā ।। śatru-krodhe tu ceṣṭāḥ syur bhāva-garbhita-bhāṣaṇam । bhrūbheda-niṭila-sveda-kaṭākṣaāruṇimādayaḥ ।।
kiñcit kokanada-cchadena sadṛśe netre svayaṃ rajyataḥ । candrasyodbhaṭa-lāñchanasya kamalasyodbhrānta-bhṛṅgasya ca ।। atra lavasya candraketoś ca paraspara-viṣayaḥ kopo bhrū-bhedādibhir vyajyate । bhṛtyādi-kopa-tritaye tat-tat-krodhāditāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
mithaḥ strī-puṃsayor eva roṣah strī-gocaraḥ punaḥ । pratyayāvadhir atra syur vikārāḥ kuṭilekṣaṇam । adhara-sphuraṇāpāṅga-rāga-niḥśvasitādayaḥ ।। ākampitādharam atiśvasitānubandham ।
kārā-vimuktir api kaṣṭatareti mene ।। atra rāvaṇa-kārāgāra-śaṅkayā janitaḥ sītā-viṣayo rāmasya roṣo bhrū-bhaṅgādibhir anubhāvair vyajyate । diṣṭyā no paruṣaṃ ruṣārdha-kathite kiñcin mayā vyāhṛtam । mithyā-dūṣita-yānayā virahitaṃ diṣṭyā na jātaṃ jagat ।।
atra svapna-vṛttānta-śravaṇa-bhrānti-janitasya bhānumatī-viṣayakasya suyodhana-roṣasya svapna-śeṣa-śravaṇa-janita-pratyaya-kṛtā śāntiḥ diṣṭyety-ādi-vāg-ārambheṇa vyajyate । dvedhā nigaditaḥ strīṇāṃ roṣaḥ puruṣa-gocaraḥ । sapatnī-hetur ādyaḥ syād anyaḥ syād anya-hetukaḥ ।। sapatnī-hetuko roṣo vipralambhe prapañcyate ।
anya-hetu-kṛte tv atra kriyāḥ puruṣa-roṣavat ।। vṛttaṃ rahaḥ-praṇayam apratipadyamāne । bhagnaṃ śarāsanam ivātiruṣā smarasya ।। atra prāktana-vṛttāntāpahnava-janito duṣyanta-viṣayakaḥ śakuntalā-roṣo bhrū-bhaṅgādibhir anubhāvair vyajyate ।
bandhu-vyāpatti-daurgaty-adhana-nāśādibhiḥ kṛtaḥ । citta-kleśa-bharaḥ śokas tatra ceṣṭā vivarṇatā ।। bāṣpodgamo mukhe śoṣaḥ stambha-niḥśvasitādayaḥ । uttamānam ayaṃ prauḍho vibhāvair anya-saṃśritaiḥ ।।
ātma-sthair atirūḍho' pi prāyaḥ śauryeṇa śāmyati । tatra ceṣṭā guṇākhyāna-nigūḍha-ruditādayaḥ ।। bhartur bhasmani petuṣīṃ karatala-vyāmṛṣṭa-pārśva-kṣitim । dṛṣṭvā yasya lalāṭa-locanam api vyāptāśru nirvāpitam ।।
atra rati-gata-śocya-daśā-vilokanena devasya śoko bāṣpodgamena vyajyate । giram udvamann iva mudaṃ mayi sthirām । vṛṣasena-vatsala vihāya yāsi mām ।। syād eṣa mṛti-paryantaḥ sva-parasthais tu madhyame ।
anativyakta-rudita-pramukhās tatra vikriyāḥ ।। rāgopādhir ayaṃ tyajanti viṣayān yaj jñātayo dustyajān । devaṃ cānakadundubhiṃ daśarathaṃ cekṣvāku-vaṃśyaṃ vinā ।। atra vasudevasya bandhu-vipattijaḥ śokaḥ prāṇotkramaṇena vyajyate ।
kaṇṭhe garva-niruddha-bāṣpa-vigame vācāṃ gatir gadgadā । kāṣṭhā tasya mamedṛśī yadukule kulyaḥ kathaṃ jīvati ।। karuṇā-kandalād iti bhāti । atra yadu-kula-dhvaṃsanena nāradasya śokaḥ ।
hetubhiḥ svagatair eva prāyaḥ strī-nīcayor ayam । maraṇa-vyavasāyāntas tatra bhū-pariveṣṭanam । urastāḍana-nirbheda-pātoccai rodanādayaḥ ।। nakhotkṛttair gaṇḍair upala-hati-śīrṇaiś ca niṭilaiḥ ।
manas takṣṇotyantaḥ-pura-parijanānāṃ sthitir iyam ।। vasudhāliṅgana-dhūsara-stanī । sama-duḥkhām iva kurvatī sthalīm ।। ahṛdyānāṃ padārthānāṃ darśana-śravaṇādibhiḥ ।
saṅkocanaṃ yan manasah sā jugupsātra vikriyāḥ ।। nāsāpidhānaṃ tvaritā gatir āsya-vikūṇanam । sarvāṅga-dhūnanaṃ kutsā muhur niṣṭhīvanādayaḥ ।। ākṛṣyāsakta-dhūpān api kuṇapa-bhujo bhūyasībhyaś citābhyaḥ ।
ete niścūṣya jaṅghān alakam udayinīr majja-dhārāḥ pibanti ।। atra jaṅghā-niścūṣaṇa-majja-dhārā-pānādi-janitā piśāca-viṣayā mādhavasya jugupsā garhaṇena ete kuṇapa-bhuja ity anena vyajyate । tvak-pracchanne snāyu-baddhāsthi-sandhau । badhnāty udyat-pūti-gandhe ratiṃ kaḥ ।।
atra kasyacid vastu-tattva-vicārāgama-śravaṇa-janitā dehe jugupsā-rūpā nindā vyajyate । ghṛṇā śuddhā jugupsānyā daśa-rūpe nirūpitā । sā heya-śravaṇotpanna-jugupsāyā na bhidyate ।। bhayaṃ tu mantunā ghora-darśana-śravaṇādibhiḥ ।
cittasyātīva cāñcalyaṃ tat prāyo nīca-madhyayoḥ ।। uttamasya tu jāyeta kāraṇair atilaukikaiḥ । bhaye tu ceṣṭā vaivarṇyaṃ stabdhatvaṃ gātra-kampanam ।। palāyanaṃ parāvṛtya vīkṣaṇaṃ svātma-gopanam ।
āsya-śoṣaṇam utkrośa-śaraṇānveṣaṇādayaḥ ।। mantur aparādhaḥ । tasmād, yathā- upasthitaṃ vīkṣya viśāmpatis tam । prahveṣv anirbandha-ruṣo hi santaḥ ।।
palāyamāno diśi dakṣiṇasyām । setu-cchidaṃ dāśarathiṃ nininda ।। atra yuddha-saṃrambha-bhīmasya colasya darśanāt pāṇḍyasya bhayaṃ palāyanādibhir vyajyate । prāpya pratyarthi-vīrāḥ kula-śikhari-guhāṃ gūḍha-gāḍhāndhakārām ।
sraṣṭāraṃ naṣṭa-dhairyāḥ kamala-bhuvam aho hanta nindanti mandam ।। sahasra-raśmer iva yasya darśanam । nināya bibhyad divasāni kauśikaḥ ।। atra varṇanīyatayā uttama-rāvaṇaṃ prati devendrasya madhyamatvaṃ nāśaṅkanīyam । yataḥ prakṛtir eva kāraṇaṃ puṃsām uttamatve । na tu varṇanā । varṇanāyāḥ kāraṇatve priyeṇa tasyānaparādha-bādhitāḥ ity ādibhiḥ augryādi-bhāva-kathanam uttamasya rāvaṇasya nocitaṃ syāt । tasmād uttama-prakṛter api devendrasya lokātirikta-vara-prabhāva-bhīṣaṇād rāvaṇād bhayam upapadyate ।
vaikuṇṭhe kuṇṭha-garve dravati maghavati klānta-kāntau kṛtānte । pāyād vaḥ kāla-kūṭaṃ jhaṭiti kavalayan līlayā nīla-kaṇṭhaḥ ।। ity atra vidrāva-tāralyādibhir udghoṣitasya dravya-nātha-savitrādi-gata-bhayasya apalāpaḥ katham abhidheyaḥ । tad-apalāpe ca kāla-kūṭa-bhakṣaṇasya sukaratvāt tat-kārya-nirvahaṇaika-prāṇasya nīlakaṇṭha-prabhāvotkarṣasya kathaṃ mastakonnamanaṃ syāt । hetujād itare prokte bhaye soḍhala-sūnunā ।
kṛtrimaṃ tūttama-gataṃ gurv-ādīn pratyavāstavam ।। vibhīṣikotthaṃ bālāder vitrāsitakam ity ubhe । tatrāntyam antarbhūtaṃ syād ghora-śravaṇaje bhaye ।। bhikṣu-bhallūka-corādi-sūcanā-kalpitatvataḥ ।
ādyaṃ tu yukti-kākṣyāyāṃ bhaya-kakṣyāṃ na gāhate ।। gurv-ādi-saṃnidhau yasmān nīcaiḥ sthity-ādi-sūcitam । bhāvo vinaya eva syād atha syān nāṭake yadi ।। avahitthatayā tasya bhayatvaṃ dūrato gatam ।
ato hetujam evaikaṃ bhayaṃ syād iti niścayaḥ ।। sattva-samutthaṃ tathaiva kartavyam । kṛtakaṃ mṛdu-ceṣṭitaiḥ kāryam ।। iti । nanu cātra svabhāvajaṃ kṛtakaṃ ceti dvividhaṃ bhayaṃ pratīyate । tasmāt tad-virodha iti cet, maivam । bharatādy-abhiprāyam ajānatāṃ pelavokti-mātra-tātparyeṇa na śaṅkitavyam । tathā hi-yathā loke mañjiṣṭhādi-dravyaṃ sahajo raktimā gāḍhataraṃ vyāpnoti । evaṃ madhya-nīcayor bhayaṃ svalpa-kāraṇa-mātre' pi sahajavad dṛśyata iti sahajam ity upacaryate । yathā kṛtako lākṣā-rasaḥ prayatna-sajjito' pi kāṣṭhādikam antar na vyāpnoti, evam uttama-gataṃ bhayam iti alaukika-kāraṇa-prakarṣeṇāpi kṛtakavad eva pratīyata iti kṛtakam ity upacaryate । anyathā svābhāvikasya bhayasya dāma-darśane' pi samutpatti-prasaṅgāt ।
siṃhāsanāntika-careṇa sahopasarpan । vākyād ṛte punar iva prativārito' smi ।। ity ādiṣu kathaṃ bhayotpattir iti ced ucyate । bhīṣaṇās trividhāḥ-ākṛti-bhīṣaṇāḥ kriyā-bhīṣaṇāḥ māhātmya-bhīṣaṇāś ceti । tatrākṛti-bhīṣaṇāḥ rakṣaḥ-piśācādayaḥ । kriyā-bhīṣaṇāḥ vīrabhadra-paraśurāma-śārdūla-vṛkādayaḥ । māhātmya-bhīṣaṇā deva-naradevādayaḥ । tato' tra māhātmya-bhīṣaṇa-rāja-darśanād bhayaṃ nāṭyācāryasya jāyate । na punaḥ svabhāvāt । tad etan niḥśaṃśayaṃ kṛtam aho durāsado rāja-mahimā iti pūrva-vākyaṃ grathnatā tenaiva kālidāseneti sarvaṃ kalyāṇam । bhojenoktāḥ sthāyino' nye garvaḥ sneho dhṛtir matiḥ ।
sthāsnur evoddhata-preyaḥ śāntodātta-raseṣv api । tatra sneho rater bhedas tridhā cecchātma-tat-kṛtaḥ ।। yad eva rocate mahyaṃ tad eva kurute priyā । iti vetti na jānāti tat priyaṃ yat karoti sā ।। iti ।
tenaiva vyākṛtaṃ ca-vatsala-prakṛter dhīra-lalita-nāyakasya priyālambana-vibhāvād utpannaḥ snehaḥ sthāyi-bhāvo viṣaya-saundaryādibhir uddīpana-vibhāvair uddīpyamānaḥ samupajāyamānair mati-dhṛti-smṛty-ādibhir vyabhicāri-bhāvair anubhāvaiś ca praśaṃsādibhiḥ saṃsṛjyamāno niṣpannaḥ preyo-rasa iti pratīyate । rati-prītyor api cāyam eva mūla-prakṛtir iṣyate । na tāvad asya snehasya ratiṃ prati mūla-prakṛtitvam । raty-aṅkura-daśāyām asyāsambhavāt । sambhogecchā-mātraṃ hi ratiḥ । saiva prema-māna-praṇayākhyābhis tisṛbhiḥ pūrva-daśābhir utkaṭībhūtā caturtha-daśāyāṃ citta-dravī-bhāva-lakṣaṇa-sneha-rūpatām āpnoti । tathā ca bhāva-prakāśikāyām- iyam aṅkuritā premṇā mānāt pallavitā bhavet । sakorakā praṇayataḥ snehāt kusumitā bhavet ।। iti ।
ato' sminn udāharaṇe snehasya rati-rūpeṇaivāsvādyatvaṃ na pṛthak sthāyitvena । evaṃ ca snehasya rati-bhedatva-kathanāt preyo-rasasyāpi śṛṅgārād apṛthaktvam artha-siddham । anye poṣā-sahiṣṇutvān naiva sthāyi-padocitāḥ ।। apakartāham asmīti mā te manasi bhūd bhayam । vimukheṣu na me khaḍgaḥ prahartuṃ jātu vāñchati ।।
vyākṛtaṃ ca-atra mayāpakāraḥ kṛta iti yat te cetasi bhayaṃ tan mā bhūt । mama khaḍgaḥ parāṅmukheṣu na kadācid api parahartum utsahata iti sarvathaiva rūḍho' haṅkāraḥ pratīyate । so' yaṃ garva-prakṛtir uddhato nāma raso niṣpadyate iti । na tāvad atra garvaḥ । kiṃ tu pūrvam apakartāraṃ paścād bhītaṃ dviṣantam avalokya jātayā sama-ravi-mukhaṃ na hanmi mā bhaiṣīr iti vāk-sūcitayā nīce dayayā kasyacid vīra-sārvabhaumasya śobhā nāma pauruṣa-sāttvika-bhāvaḥ pratīyate । yadi vā abhītam api śatruṃ bhīto yadi tarhi palāyasvety adhikṣipatīti garva iti ced astu vā garvaḥ । tathāpy asatyabhītikalpanā-rūpa-cittādhyavasāya-prakāśana-dvāreṇa śatru-gata-krodham eva puṣṇāti । kiṃ ca vimukhāprahāra-rūpātma-sambhāvanā-rūpa-garvasya asatya-bhīti-kalpanopabṛṃhaṇāt poṣo bhāvakānāṃ vairasyāya, na kevalaṃ svādābhāvāyeti nāsminn udāharaṇe garvasya sthāyitvam upapadyate । sarvāḥ sampattayas tasya santuṣṭaṃ yasya mānasam । upānad-gūḍha-pādasya nanu carmāstṛtaiva bhūḥ ।। iti ।
vyākṛtaṃ ca । atra kasyacid upaśānta-prakṛter dhīra-śānta-nāyakasya arthopagamana-mano' nukūla-dārādi-sampatter ālambana-vibhāva-bhūtāyāḥ samutpanno dhṛti-sthāyi-bhāvo vastu-tattvālocanādibhir uddīpana-vibhāvair uddīpyamānaḥ samupajāyamāna-smṛti-maty-ādibhir vyabhicāri-bhāvair vāg-ārambhādibhiś cānubhāvair anuṣajyamāno niṣpannaḥ śānto rasa iti gīyate । anye punar asya śamaṃ prakṛtim āmananti । sa tu dhṛter eva viśeṣo bhaviṣyatīti । atra tāvad anukūla-dāra-siddhi-janitāyāḥ dhṛtes tu rati-paratantratvam ābāla-gopāla-prasiddham । nanu, vastutattvālocanādibhir asyāḥ sthāyitvaṃ kalpyate iti cet, na । naiḥspṛhya-vāsanā-vāsite bhāvaka-citte vibhāvādiṣv api naiḥsvpṛhyonmeṣād dhṛter mūla-ccheda-prasaṅgāt । artha-sampatti-janitā dhṛtis tu agṛdhnu-lakṣaṇa-lokottaratva-prāpti-vyavasāya-rūpam utsāham anusarantī vīropakaraṇatām āpnotīti nātra dhṛteḥ sthāyitvam । dhṛti-sthāyitva-nirākaraṇa-saṃrambheṇaiva naṣṭas tad-viṣayaḥ śama-sthāyī kutra vā līno na jñāyate । mateḥ sthāyitvaṃ tenaivodāhṛtam । tathā hi- sādhāraṇyān nirātaṅkaḥ kanyām anyo' pi yācate ।
kiṃ punar jagatāṃ jetā prapautraḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। iti । vyākṛtaṃ ca-rāmasya udātta-prakṛter nisargata eva tattvābhiniveśinī matir nānya-viṣaye pravartate । na ca pravṛttā uparamati । sā ca sīteyaṃ mama svīkāra-yogyety evaṃ-rūpeṇa pravṛttā rāvaṇa-prārthanā-lakṣmaṇa-protsāhanābhyām uddīpyamānā samupajāyamāna-cintā-vitarka-vrīḍāvahittha-smṛty-ādibhiḥ kālocitottarānu-mīyamānair viveka-cāturya-dhairyaudāryādibhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānā udātta-rasa-rūpeṇa niṣpadyate iti । atra tāvat sītā-viṣayā ātma-svīkāra-yogyatva-niścaya-rūpā rāmasya matis tu rater utpatti-mātra-kāraṇam eva । tad-aniścaye rater anaucityāt । atra kanyāyāḥ sādhāraṇya-niścayo matiḥ । tasyāḥ sthāyitvam icchāma iti cet, na । sā hi rāvaṇa-viṣaya-lajjāsūyā-doṣa-nivāraṇa-dvāreṇa kārya-karaṇāparāṅmukhībhāva-lakṣaṇa-lokottara-tat-prāpti-vyavasāya-rūpā rāmotsāhaṃ bhāvakāsvāda-yogyatayā protsāhayati । tad aṣṭāv eva vijñeyāḥ sthāyino muni-saṃmatāḥ ।
sthāyino' ṣṭau trayastriṃśac cāriṇo' ṣṭau ca sāttvikāḥ ।। evam ekonapañcāśad bhāvāḥ syur militā ime । evaṃ hi sthāyino bhāvān siṃha-bhūpatir abhyadhāt ।। athaiṣāṃ rasa-rūpatvam ucyate siṃha-bhūbhujā ।
vidvan-mānasa-haṃsena rasa-bhāva-vivekinā ।। ete ca sthāyinaḥ svaiḥ svair vibhāvair vyabhicāribhiḥ । sāttvikaiś cānubhāvaiś ca naṭābhinaya-yogataḥ ।। sākṣātkāram ivānītāḥ prāpitāḥ svādu-rūpatām ।
sāmājikānāṃ manasi prayānti rasa-rūpatām ।। dadhyādi-vyañjana-dravyaiś ciñcādibhir athauṣadhaiḥ । guḍādi-madhura-dravyair yathā-yogaṃ samanvitaiḥ ।। yadvat pāka-viśeṣeṇa ṣāḍavākhyo rasaḥ paraḥ ।
niṣpadyate vibhāvādyaiḥ prayogeṇa tathā rasaḥ । so' yam ānanda-sambhedo bhāvakair anubhūyate ।। nanu nāyaka-niṣṭhasya sthāyi-prakarṣa-lakṣaṇasya rasasya sāmājikānubhava-yogyatā nopapadyate । anya-bhavasya tasyānyānubhavāyogāt iti cet satyam । ko vā nāyaka-gataṃ rasam ācaṣṭe । tathā hi-sa ca nāyako dṛṣṭaḥ śruto' nukṛto vā rasasyāśrayatām ālambate । nādyaḥ । sākṣād dṛṣṭa-nāyaka-ratyāder vrīḍā-jugupsādi-pratīpa-phalatvena svādābhāvāt । na dvitīya-tṛtīyau । tayor avidyamānatvāt । na hy asati āśraye tad-āśritasyāvasthānam upapadyate । nanu bhavatu nāmaivam । tathāpi rasasya naṭa-gatatve na sāmājikānubhavānupapattir iti cet, na । naṭe rasa-sambhavaḥ kim anubhāvādi-sad-bhāvena vibhāvādi-sambhavena vā । nādyaḥ, abhyāsa-pāṭavādināpi tat-siddheḥ । kiṃ ca sāmājikeṣu yathocitam anubhāva-sadbhāve' pi tvayā teṣāṃ rasāśrayatānaṅgīkārāt । yadi vibhāvena tatrāpi kim anukārya-mālavikādinā anukāriṇā svakāntādinā vā । nādyaḥ, anaucityāt । nāpi dvitīyaḥ, naṭe sākṣād-dṛṣṭa-nāyakavad aślīlatā-pratīteḥ ।
vibhāvādi-bhāvānām anapekṣita-bāhya-sattvānāṃ śabdopadhānād evāsādita-sad-bhāvānām anukāryāpekṣayā niḥsādhāraṇānām api kāvye nāṭye ca abhidhā-paryāyeṇa sādhāraṇīkaraṇātmanā bhāvanā-vyāpāreṇa sva-sambandhitayā vibhāvitānāṃ sākṣād bhāvaka-cetasi viparivartamānānām ālambanatvādy-avirodhād anaucityādi-viplava-rahitaḥ sthāyī nirbharānanda-viśrānti-svabhāvena bhogena bhāvakair bhujyate iti । anye tv anyathā samādhānam āhuḥ । loke pramadādi-kāraṇādibhiḥ sthāyy-anumāne abhyāsa-pāṭavavatāṃ sahṛdayānāṃ kāvye nāṭye ca vibhāvādi-pada-vyapadeśyaiḥ sva-sambandhitvena anya-sambandhitvena ca sādhāraṇyāt pratītair abhivyaktībhūto vāsanātmatayā sthitaḥ sthāyī ratyādiḥ pānaka-rasa-nyāyena carvyamāṇo lokottara-camatkāra-kārī paramānandam iva kandalayan rasa-rūpatām āpnotīti । evaṃ ca bhukti-vyakti-pakṣayor ubhayor api sāmājikānāṃ rasāśrayatvopapatter anyatara-pakṣa-parigrahāgrahād udāsmahe । prāyeṇa bhāratīya-matānusāriṇāṃ prakriyā tu -loke kāraṇa-kārya-sahakāritām upagataiḥ kāvye nāṭye vā sarasa-sūkti-sudhā-mādhurī-dhurīṇair yathoktābhinaya-sametair vā padārthatvena vibhāvānubhāva-sañcāri-vyapadeśaṃ prāpitaiḥ nāyikā-nāyaka-candra-candrikā-malayānilādi-bhrū-vikṣepa-kaṭākṣa-pāta-sveda-romāñcādi-nirveda-harṣādi-rūpair vāsanātmakair ātma-sambandhitvenābhi-matair bhāvaiḥ dharma-kīrti-ratānāṃ ṣaḍ-aṅga-nāṭya-samaya-jñānāṃ nānā-deśa-veṣa-bhāṣā-vicakṣaṇānāṃ nikhila-kalā-kalāpa-kovidānāṃ santyakta-matsarāṇāṃ sakala-siddhānta-vedināṃ rasa-bhāva-vivecakānāṃ kāvyārtha-nihita-cetasāṃ sāmājikānāṃ manasi mudrā-muditra-nyāyena viparitvartitāḥ vāsitāś cābhivardhitāḥ sthāyino bhāvāḥ kāvyārthatvenābhimatāḥ bāhyārthāvalambanātmakāḥ santo vikāsa-vistara-kṣobha-vikṣepātmakatayā vibhinnāḥ tat-tad-rūpeṇa āsvādyamānāḥ paramānanda-rūpatām āpnuvantīti sakala-sahṛdaya-saṃvedana-siddhasya rasasya pramāṇāntareṇa saṃsādhana-pariśramaḥ śrotṛ-jana-citta-kṣobhāya na kevalaṃ, pratyuta nopayogāyeti prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ ।।
aṣṭadhā sa ca śṛṅgāra-hāsya-vīrādbhutā api । raudraḥ karuṇa-bībhatsau bhayānaka itīritaḥ ।। eṣūttaras tu pūrvasmāt sambhūto viṣamāt samaḥ । bahu-vaktavyatā-hetoḥ sakalāhlādanād api ।।
raseṣu tatra śṛṅgāraḥ prathamaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca sāttvikair vyabhicāribhiḥ ।। nītā sadasya-rasyatvaṃ ratiḥ śṛṅgāra ucyate । sa vipralambhaḥ sambhoga iti dvedhā nigadyate ।।
ayuktayos taruṇayor yo' nurāgaḥ parasparam । abhīṣṭāliṅganādīnām anavāptau prakṛṣyate ।। sa vipralambho vijñeyaḥ sa caturdhā nigadyate । pūrvānurāga-mānau ca pravāsa-karuṇāv iti ।।
atrāyam arthaḥ-nāyikā-nāyakayoḥ prāg-asaṅgatayoḥ saṅgata-viyuktayor vā svocita-vibhāvair anubhāviś copajāyamānaḥ parasparānurāgo' nyatarānurāgo vā svābhilaṣitāliṅganādīnām anavāptau satyām utpadyamānair vyabhicāribhir anubhāvaiś ca prakṛṣyamāṇo vipralambha-śṛṅgāra ity ākhyāyate । sa ca pūrvānurāgādi-bhedena cāturvidhyam āpadyate । yat prema saṅgamāt pūrvaṃ darśana-śravaṇādibhiḥ । pūrvānurāgaḥ sa jñeyaḥ śravaṇaṃ tad-guṇa-śrutiḥ ।। svenānalaṃ yat kila saṃśrayiṣye ।
mṛṣā-giraṃ tvāṃ nṛpatau na kuryām ।। atra haṃsa-mukhān nala-guṇa-śravaṇena damayantyāḥ pūrvānurāgaḥ । pratyakṣa-citra-svapnādau darśanaṃ darśanaṃ matam ।। nyavartanānyopagamāt kumārī ।
vṛkṣāntaraṃ kāṅkṣati ṣaṭ-padālī ।। līlāvadhūta-kamalā kalayantī pakṣapātam adhikaṃ naḥ । mānasam upaiti keyaṃ citra-gatā rājahaṃsīva ।। atra citragata-ratnāvalī-darśanād vatsa-rājasya pūrvānurāgaḥ ।
svapne dṛṣṭākārā tam api samādāya gatavatī bhavatī । anyam upāyaṃ na labhe prasīda rambhoru dāsāya ।। atra kām api svapne dṛṣṭavataḥ kasyacin nāyakasya pūrvānurāgaḥ । yataḥ pūrvānurāgo' yaṃ saṅkalpātmā pravartate ।
so' yaṃ pūrvānurāgākhyo vipralambha itīritaḥ ।। pāratantryād ayaṃ dvedhā daiva-mānuṣa-kalpanāt । tatra sañcāriṇo glāniḥ śaṅkāsūye śramo bhayam ।। nirvedautsukya-dainyāni cintā-nidre prabodhatā ।
viṣādo jaḍatonmādo moho maraṇam eva ca ।। vyarthaṃ samarthya lalitaṃ vapur ātmanaś ca । śūnyā jagāma bhavanābhimukhī kathaṃcit ।। atra janakādy-ānukūlye' pi daiva-pāratantryeṇa pārvatyāḥ pūrvānurāgaḥ ।
ammo apaṃgo me paripphurai kiṃ bi vāmo । ṇāha maṃ parāhīṇaṃ tui parigaṇaa satiṇhaṃ ।। amho apāṅgo me parisphurati kim api vāmaḥ । nātha māṃ parādhīnāṃ tvayi parigaṇaya satṛṣṇām ।।]
atra devayānī-pāratantryeṇa śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ yayāti-viṣayaḥ pūrvānurāgaḥ । etasminn abhilāṣādi maraṇāntam anekadhā । tat-tat-sañcāri-bhāvānām utkaṭatvād daśā bhavet ।। tathāpi prāktanair asyā daśāvasthāḥ samāsataḥ ।
proktās tad-anurodhena tāsāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate ।। abhilāṣaś cintānusmṛti-guṇa-saṅkīrtanodvegāḥ । savilāpā unmāda-vyādhī jaḍatā mṛtiś ca tāḥ kramaśaḥ ।। saṅgamopāya-racita-prārabdha-vyavasāyataḥ ।
saṅkalpecchā-samudbhūtir abhilāṣo' tra vikriyāḥ ।। praveśa-nirgamau tūṣṇīṃ tad-dṛṣṭi-patha-gāminau । rāga-prakāśana-parāś ceṣṭāḥ svātma-prasādhanam । vyājoktayaś ca vijane sthitir ity evam ādayaḥ ।।
pramodād udvelaiś cakita-hariṇī-vīkṣaṇa-sakhaiḥ । apāṅgaiḥ siṃha-kṣmā-ramaṇam abalā vīkṣitavatī ।। atra rāga-prakāśana-parair dṛṣṭi-viśeṣair nāyake kasyāścid abhilāṣo vyajyate । kenopāyena saṃsiddhiḥ kadā tasya samāgamaḥ ।
dūtī-mukhena kiṃ vācyam ity ādy ūhas tu cintanam ।। atra nīvyādi-saṃsparśaḥ śayyāyāṃ parivartanam । sa-bāṣpākekarā dṛṣṭir mudrikādi-vivartanam । nirlakṣya-vīkṣaṇaṃ caivam ādyā vikṛtayo matāḥ ।।
śrī-siṃhaḥ sva-sakhī-mukhena sa kathaṃ neyaḥ sa kiṃ vakṣyati । śayyāyāṃ parivartane śvasiti ca kṣiptvā kapolaṃ kare ।। arthānām anubhūtānāṃ deśa-kālānuvartinām । sāntatyena parāmarśo mānasaḥ syād anusmṛtiḥ ।। tatrānubhāvā niḥśvāso dhyāṇaṃ kṛtya-vihastatā ।
śayyāsanādi-vidveṣa ity ādyāḥ smara-kalpitāḥ ।। vyāpārānanapota-siṃha-nṛpate rāgānusandhāyakān । nānyat kāṅkṣati karma kartum ucitaṃ nāste na śete kvacit ।। saundaryādi-guṇa-ślāghā guṇa-kīrtanam atra tu ।
romāñco gadgadā vāṇī bhāva-manthara-vīkṣaṇam । tat-saṅga-cintanaṃ sakhyā gaṇḍa-svedādayo' pi ca ।। mad-bhāgyaād anapota-siṃha-nṛpate rūpaṃ mayā vīkṣitam । svidyad-gaṇḍa-talaṃ sagadgada-padaṃ sākhyāti sakhyāḥ puraḥ ।।
manasaḥ kampa udvegaḥ kathitas tatra vikriyāḥ । cintā santāpa-niḥśvāsau dveṣaḥ śayyāsanādiṣu । stambha-cintāśru-vaivarṇya-dīnatvādaya īritāḥ ।। tat-strībhiś cirayat suteṣu vilasac-cetaḥ-samudbhrāntibhiḥ ।
kāmaṃ snigdha-sakhī-jane viracitā dīnā dṛśor vṛttayaḥ ।। iha me dṛk-pathaṃ prāpad ihātiṣṭhad ihāsta ca । ihālapad ihāvātsīd ihaiva nyavṛtat tathā ।। ity ādi-vākya-vinyāso vilāpa iti kīrtitaḥ ।
tatra ceṣṭās tu kutrāpi gamanaṃ kvacid īkṣaṇam । kvacit kvacid avasthānaṃ kvacic ca bhramaṇādayaḥ ।। kuñje sādaram īkṣitāham iha mam ānandayan sa smitaiḥ । yātaṃ yāti ca satvarā taru-talaṃ līlāta ekākinī ।।
sarvāvasthāsu sarvatra tan-manaskatayā sadā । atasmiṃs tad iti bhrāntir unmādo virahodbhavaḥ ।। tatra ceṣṭās tu vijñeyā dveṣaḥ sveṣṭe' pi vastuni । dīrghaṃ muhuś ca niḥśvāso nirnimeṣatayā sthitiḥ ।
nirnimitta-smita-dhyāna-gāna-maunādayo' pi ca ।। nirvarṇyāyam asau mama priya iti premābhiyoga-bhramāt । sāsūyaṃ sadara-smitaṃ sa-cakitaṃ sākāṅkṣam ālokate ।। abhīṣṭa-saṅgamābhāvād vyādhiḥ santāpa-lakṣaṇaḥ ।
atra santāpa-niḥśvāsau śīta-vastu-niṣevaṇam ।। jīvitopekṣaṇaṃ moho mumūrṣā dhṛti-varjanam । yatra kvacic ca patanaṃ srastākṣatvādayo' pi ca ।। kandarpānala-dīpitāni sutanor aṅgāni paryākulāḥ ।
sakhyaḥ pāṇi-talāni patra-marutā nirvāpayantyo muhuḥ ।। idam iṣṭam aniṣṭaṃ tad iti vetti na kiñcana । nottaraṃ bhāṣate praśne nekṣate na śṛṇoti ca ।। yatra dhyāyati niḥsaṃjñaṃ jaḍatā sā prakīrtitā ।
atra sparśānabhijñatvaṃ vaivarṇyaṃ śithilāṅgatā । akāṇḍa-huṅkṛtiḥ stambho niḥśvāsa-kṛśatādayaḥ ।। ākrāntā tanutāṃ gatā smara-śaraiḥ śāteva śātodarī । prāpte pakṣma-puṭāvṛtiṃ ratipates tat-ketanaṃ jṛmbhatām ।।
tais taiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārair yadi na syāt samāgamaḥ । tataḥ syān maraṇodyogah kāmāgnes tatra vikriyāḥ ।। līlā-śuka-cakorādi-nyāsaḥ snigdha-sakhī-kare । kala-kaṇṭha-kalālāpa-śrutir mandānilādaraḥ ।
jyotsnā-praveśa-mākanda-mañjarī-vīkṣaṇādayaḥ ।। nyāsīkṛtya ca śārikāṃ parijane snigdhe samaṃ vīṇayā । siktena hy anapota-siṃha-nṛpater nāmnā punar jīvitā ।। atra kecid abhilāṣāt pūrvam icchotkaṇṭhā-lakṣaṇam avasthā-dvayam aṅgīkṛtya dvādaśāvasthā iti varṇayanti । tatrecchā punar abhilāṣān na bhidyate । tat-prāpti-tvarālakṣaṇā utkaṇṭhā tu cintanān nātiricyate ity udāsitam ।
muhuḥ-kṛto meti neti pratiṣedhārtha-vīpsayā । īpsitāliṅganādīnāṃ nirodho māna ucyate ।। so' yaṃ sahetu-nirhetu-bhedād dvedhātra hetujaḥ । īrṣyayā sambhaved īrṣyā tv anyāsaṅgini vallabhe ।।
asahiṣṇutvam eva syād dṛṣṭer anumiteḥ śruteḥ । īrṣyā-māne tu nirvedāvahittha-glāni-dīnatāḥ । cintā-cāpalya-jaḍatā-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। paccakkha-maṃtu-kāraa ja{i} cumbasi maha ime hada-kapole ।
tā majjha pia-sahīe bisesao kīsa biṇṇao ।। [pratyakṣa-mantu-kāraka yadi cumbasi mamaimau hata-kapolau । tato mama priya-sakhyā viśeṣakaḥ kasmād vijñātaḥ ।।] atra nāyikā-kapola-cumbana-vyājena tat-pratibimbitāṃ sakhīṃ cumbati nāyake tad-īrṣyayā janito nāyikā-mānaḥ pratyakṣa-mantukārakety anayā sambuddhyā vyajyate ।
bhogāṅka-gotra-skhalanotsvapnair anumitis tridhā ।। dhatte bhūṣaṇam ardha-candram amalaṃ candre na kiṃ kālimā । bhāgyaṃ draṣṭum anīśayaiva bhavataḥ kāntāparāddhaṃ mayā ।। atra maṇi-mālikādi-lakṣaṇa-madana-mudrānumiti-priyāparādha-janiterṣyā-sambhūto mānaḥ tat sādhv eva kṛtam ity ādibhir viparīta-lakṣaṇoktibhir vyajyate ।
netrāñcalena mayi tāḍanam ācarantyāḥ । manye tad eva mukha-paṅkajam āyatākṣyāḥ ।। pratyabhitsur avadantya eva tam । krodha-bhinna-valayair vivartanaiḥ ।।
śrutiḥ priyāparādhasya śrutir āpta-sakhī-mukhāt ।। śruti-janiterṣyayā māno, yathā- kiṃ tūṣṇīṃ rodiṣi kopane bahutaraṃ phūtkṛtya rodiṣyasi । nirviṇṇo' nunayaṃ prati priyatamo madhyasthatām eṣyati ।। atra piśuna-sakhī-janopadeśa-janito māno bāṣpādibhir vyajyate ।
kāraṇābhāsa-sambhūto nirhetuḥ syād dvayor api । avahitthādayas tatra vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। nirāhārāḥ sakhyaḥ satata-ruditocchūṇa-nayanāḥ । tavāvasthā ceyaṃ visṛja kaṭhine mānam adhunā ।।
alia-pasuttaa viṇimīliaccha dehi suhaa majjha oāsaṃ । gaṇḍa-paricuṃbaṇāpulaiaṅga ṇa puṇo cirāissaṃ ।। (alīka-prasupta vinimīlitākṣa dehi subhaga mamāvakāśam । gaṇḍa-paricumbanā-pulakitāṅga na punaś cirayiṣyāmi ।।)
atrālīka-svāpākṣi-nimīlanādi-sūcita-puruṣa-māna-kāraṇasya prasādhana-gṛha-vyāpāra-nimittaṃ vilambanasyābhāsatvam । sandhyayā praṇamito' smi nānyathā । cakravāka-sama-vṛttim ātmanaḥ ।। atra pārvatī-māna-kāraṇasya parameśvara-kṛta-sandhyā-praṇāmasyābhāsatvam ।
nanu aliapasuttety atra gaṇḍa-paricumbanasya niṣedho nāsti । evaṃ muñca kopam ity atra ca niṣedho na śrūyate । tat katham asya nirhetukasya mānatvam iti cet । meti neti vācika-niṣedhasya upalaksaṇatvāt pūrvasminn udāharaṇe apratikriyayā cumbanānaṅgīkāra-lakṣaṇo niṣedho vidyata eva । aparatra punar anuttara-dānādinā anaṅgīkāra-lakṣaṇo niṣedho vaktavya eva । nanu nirhetukasya mānasya bhāva-kauṭilya-rūpa-mānasya ca ko bheda iti ced ucyate । nirhetuka-māne tu kopa-vyājena cumbanādi-vilambanāt prema-parīkṣaṇaṃ phalam । bhāva-kauṭilya-māne tu cumbanādy-avilambaḥ phalam iti spaṣṭa eva tayor bhedaḥ । nirhetukaḥ svayaṃ śāmyet svayaṃ grāhasmitādibhiḥ ।। mugdhe kim etad racitaṃ tvayeti ।
smitottaro' bhūt kuhanāvirodhaḥ ।। atra lakṣmī-nārāyaṇayor anyonya-mānasya paraspara-kṛta-bhoga-cihna-lakṣaṇa-kāraṇābhāsa-janitasya smitottaratayā svayaṃ śāntir avagamyate । hetujas tu śamaṃ yāti yathāyogyaṃ prakalpitaiḥ । sāmnā bhedena dānena naty-upekṣā-rasāntaraiḥ ।
tatra priyokti-kathanaṃ yat tu tat sāma gīyate ।। kim anyathā cetasi śaṅkayeti । nājñāyi māno' pi sakhī-jano' pi ।। atra priya-sāmokti-janitā kasyāścid māna-śāntiḥ sakhī-jana-mānādy-ajñāna-sūcitair āliṅganādibhir vyajyate ।
sakhyādibhir upālambha-prayogo bheda ucyate ।। vidheyas te preyān yadi vayam anullaṅghya-vacasaḥ । nivāpāmbho datte nayana-salilair māna-suhṛde ।। vyājena bhūṣaṇādīnāṃ pradānaṃ dānam ucyate ।। athā-
vitarasi naḥ kalikāṃ kim-artham enām । śaṭhaḥ kalir eva mahāṃs tvayādya dattaḥ ।। natiḥ pāda-praṇāmaḥ syāt ।। praṇamati nija-nāthe pāda-paryanta-pīṭham ।
anayata kuca-yugme nirguṇāṃ hāra-vallīm ।। tūṣṇīṃ sthitir upekṣaṇam ।। caraṇoāsaṇisaṇṇassa tassa bharimo aṇālabantassa । pāaṅguṭṭhābeṭṭhia kesa-diḍhāaḍḍhaṇa-suhaṃ ।।
[caraṇāvakāśa-niṣaṇṇasya tasya smarāmo' nālapataḥ । pādāṅguṣṭhāveṣṭhita keśa-dṛḍhākarṣaṇa-sukham ।।] atra śayyāyāṃ caraṇāvakāśa-sthiti-maunādibhir upekṣā । tayā janitā mānasya śāntiś caraṇāṅguṣṭha-veṣṭita-keśa-dṛḍhākarṣaṇena vyajyate । ākasmika-bhayādīnāṃ kalpanā syad rasāntaram ।
yādṛcchikaṃ buddhi-pūrvam iti dvedhā nigadyate । anukūlena daivena kṛtaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ bhavet ।। mānam asyā nirākartuṃ pādayor me patiṣyataḥ । upakārāya diṣṭyaitad udīṇaṃ ghana-garjitam ।।
atra māna-praṇodana-ghana-garjita-santrāsasya priya-prayatnair vinā daiva-vaśena sambhūtatvād yādṛcchikatvam । pratyutpanna-dhiyā puṃsā kalpitaṃ buddhi-pūrvakam ।। kaścit kesara-dūṣitekṣaṇa iva vyāmīlya netre sthitaḥ । bhrāntyā dhūrtatayātha sā natim ṛte tenāniśaṃ cumbitā ।।
atra mānāpanodanasya priya-trāsasya netra-vyāvṛtti-naṭana-lakṣaṇatayā nāyakasya pratyutpanna-matyā kalpitatvād buddhi-pūrvakatvam । pūrva-saṅgatayor yūnor bhaved deśāntarādibhiḥ । caraṇa-vyavadhānaṃ yat sa pravāsa itīryate ।। taj-janyo vipralambho' pi pravāsatvena saṃmataḥ ।
harṣa-garva-mada-vrīḍā varjayitvā samīritāḥ ।। śṛṅgāra-yogyāḥ sarve' pi pravāsa-vyabhicāriṇaḥ । kāryataḥ sambhramāc chāpāt sa tridhā tatra kāryajaḥ ।। buddhi-pūrvatayā yūnoḥ saṃvidhāna-vyapekṣayā ।
vṛtto vartiṣyamāṇaś ca vartamāna iti tridhā ।। dharmārtha-saṅgrahāya buddhi-pūrvo vyāpāraḥ kāryam । tena vṛtto, yathā- ajasram āhūta-sahasra-netraḥ । mandāra-śūnyān alakāṃś cakāra ।।
atra purandarasya pūrvaṃ śacīm āmantrya paścād adhvara-pradeśa-gamanena tayoḥ saṃvidhān avyapekṣayā vipralambhasya bhūta-pūrvatvam । tanur api na te doṣo' smākaṃ vidhis tu parāṅmukhaḥ । prakṛti-capale kā naḥ pīḍā gate hata-jīvite ।। yāmīti priya-puṣṭāyāḥ priyāyāḥ kaṇṭha-lagnayoḥ ।
vaco-jīvitayor āsīt puro niḥsaraṇe raṇaḥ ।। āvegaḥ sambhramaḥ so' pi naiko divyādibhedataḥ ।। svargāyotpatitā bhaven mayi punar-bhāvārdram asyā manaḥ । sā cātyantam agocaraṃ nayanayor yāteti ko' yaṃ vidhiḥ ।।
atra vipralambhasya kāraṇāntara-nirāsena ko' yaṃ vidhir iti vidheḥ kāraṇatvābhiprāyeṇa divya-sambhrama-janitatvaṃ pratīyate । śāpo vairūpyatād rūpya-pravṛtter dvividho bhavet । pravāsaḥ śāpa-vairūpyād ahalyā-gautamādiṣu ।। śāpenāstaṃgamita-mahimā varṣa-bhogyeṇa bhartuḥ ।
snigdha-cchāyā-taruṣu vasatiṃ rāma-giry-āśrameṣu ।। dvayor ekasya maraṇe punar ujjīvanāvadhau । virahaḥ karuṇo' nyasya saṅgamāśānuvartanāt ।। karuṇa-bhrama-kāritvāt so' yaṃ karuṇa ucyate ।
sañcāriṇo' nubhāvāś ca karuṇe' pi pravāsavat ।। vyasana-kṛśo pratipālayāṃ babhūva । kiraṇa-parikṣaya-dhūsarā pradoṣam ।। atrākāśa-sarasvatī-pratyayena rater vipralambhaḥ kṛśatvādy-anumitair glāny-ādibhiḥ vyabhicāri-bhāvaiḥ poṣitaḥ samaya-paripālanādibhir anubhāvair vyajyate ।
atra kecid āhuḥ-karuṇo nāma vipralambha-śṛṅgāro nāsti । ubhayālambanasya tasya ekatraivāsambhavāt । yatra tv ekasyāpāye sati tad-itara-gatāḥ pralāpādayo bhavanti sa śokān na bhidyate iti । yatra punar-ujjīvanena sambhogo nāsti, tatra satyaṃ śoka eva । yatra so' sti tatra vipralambha eva । anyathā sambhoga-śiraske anyatarāpāya-lakṣaṇe vairūpya-śāpa-pravāse' pi śoka-rūpatvāpatteḥ । nanv evaṃ pravāsa-karuṇayoḥ ko bheda iti ced ucyate-śarīreṇa deśāntara-gamane pravāsaḥ । prāṇair deśāntara-gamane karuṇa iti । atra kecid ayoga-śabdasya pūrvānurāga-vācakatvaṃ viprayoga-śabdasya mānādi-vācakatvaṃ cābhipretya ayogo viprayogaś ceti sambhogād anyasya śṛṅgārasya vibhāgam āhuḥ । vipralambha-padasyāprayoge ca kāraṇaṃ bruvate- uktvā saṅketam aprāptau tad-vyatikrame nāyikāntarānusaraṇe ca vipralambha-śabdasya prayogaḥ । vañcanārthatvāt tasya । tat-sāmānyābhidhāyitve tu vipralambha-śabdasya upacaritatvāpatter iti । tad ayuktam । caturvidhe' pi vipralambhe vañcana-rūpasyārthasya mukhyata eva siddheḥ । tathā ca śrī-bhojaḥ- vipralambhasya yadi vā vañcanāmātra-vācinaḥ ।
vinā samāse caturāś caturo' rthān niyuñjate ।। pūrvānurāge vividhaṃ vañcanaṃ vrīḍitādibhiḥ । māne viruddhaṃ tat prāhuḥ punar īrṣyāyitādibhiḥ ।। nyāviddhaṃ dīrgha-kālatvāt pravāse tat pratīyate ।
viniṣiddhaṃ tu karuṇe karuṇatvena gīyate ।। sparśanāliṅganādīnām ānukūlyān niṣevaṇam । ghaṭate yatra yūnor yat sa sambhogaś caturvidhaḥ ।। atrāyam arthaḥ-prāg-asaṅgatayoḥ saṅgata-viyuktayor vā nāyikā-nāyakayoḥ paraspara-samāgame prāg-utpannā tadānīntanī vā ratiḥ prepsitāliṅganādīnāṃ prāptau satyāṃ upajāyamānair harṣādibhiḥ saṃsṛjyamānā candrodayādibhir uddīpitā smitādibhir vyajyamānā prāpta-prakarṣā sambhoga-śṛṅgāra ity ākhyāyate । sa ca vakṣyamāṇa-krameṇa caturvidhaḥ ।
saṅkṣiptaḥ saṅkīrṇaḥ sampannataraḥ samṛddhimān iti te । pūrvānurāga-māna-pravāsa-karuṇānusambhavāḥ kramataḥ ।। yuvānau yatra saṃkṣiptān sādhvasa-vrīḍitādibhiḥ । upacārān niṣevete sa saṃkṣipta itīritaḥ ।।
līlā-hitulia-selo rakkhadu vo rāhiāi tthaṇa-paṭṭhe । hariṇo puḍhama-samāama-saddhasa-basa-bebilo hattho ।। (līlābhitulita-śailo rakṣatu vo rādhikā-stana-sparśe । hareḥ prathama-samāgama-sādhvasa-vaśa-vepana-śīlo hastaḥ ।।)
sanna-hasta-madayopagūhane । durlabha-pratikṛtaṃ vadhūratam ।। saṅkīrṇas tu parādhīna vyalīka-maraṇādibhiḥ । saṅkīryamāṇaḥ sambhogaḥ kiñcit puṣpeṣu-peśalaḥ ।।
vibhejire tair mithunai ratāni । mānāvasādād viśadīkṛtāni ।। bhaya-vyalīka-smaraṇādy-abhāvāt prāpta-vaibhavaḥ । proṣitāgatayor yūnor bhogaḥ sampanna īritaḥ ।।
daṃta-kkhaaṃ kabole kaaggahubbellio a dhammillo । parighummirāa diṭṭhī piāgamaṃ sāhai bahūe ।। (danta-kṣataṃ kapole kaca-grahodveellitaś ca dhammillaḥ । parighūrṇana-śīlā ca dṛṣṭiḥ priyāgamaṃ sādhayati vadhvāḥ ।।)
atra aprathama-sambhogatvād bhayābhāvaḥ । danta-kṣatādiṣv aṅgārpaṇānukūlyena vyalīka-smaraṇādy-abhāvaḥ । tābhyām upārūḍha-vaibhavaḥ sampadyate sambhogaḥ । punar ujjīvane bhoga-samṛddhiḥ kiyatī bhavet । śivābhyām eva vijñeyam ity ayaṃ hi samṛddhimān ।। kaṇṭha-sthānaṃ jīvitaṃ ca prapede । tenāpūrvā sā samullāsa-lakṣmīm
indu-spṛṣṭāṃ sindhu-lekheva bheje ।। ajaṇia-cumbaṇa-ḍambarāi dūraṃ । ṇamaha aṇaṃga-rahīṇa mohaṇāiṃ ।। ajanita-cumbana-ḍambarāṇi dūram ।
namatānaṅga-ratyor mohanāni ।।) atra punar-ujjīvitenaa kāmena saha ratyā rater bāhyopacārānapekṣayaiva tat-phala-rūpa-sukha-prāpti-kathanāt sambhogaḥ samṛddhyati । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ । hāsaḥ sadasya-rasyatvaṃ nīto hāsya itīryate ।।
tatrālasya-glāni-nidrā-vyādhy-ādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । eṣa dvedhā bhaved ātma-para-sthiti-vibhāgataḥ ।। ātmasthas tu yadā svasya vikārair hasati svayam । yathā bāla-rāmāyaṇe-bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ -aho tribhuvanādhipater asya anucarasya mahārha-veṣatā ।
kaupīnācchādane valkam akṣa-sūtraṃ jaṭā-cchaṭāḥ । rudrāṅkuśas tripuṇḍraṃ ca veṣo bhṛṅgiriṭer ayam ।। atra bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ sva-veṣa-vaikṛtenaiva svayam ātmānaṃ hasati । parasthas tu para-prāptair etair hasati cet param ।।
tāvat kharaḥ prakharam ullalayāṃcakāra । visrasta-vastram avarodha-vadhūḥ papāta ।। prakṛti-vaśāt sa ca ṣoḍhā smita-hasite vihasitāvahasite ca । apahasitātihasitake jyeṣṭhādīnāṃ kramād dve dve ।।
smitaṃ cālakṣya-daśanaṃ dṛk-kapola-vikāśa-kṛt ।। utphulla-gaṇḍa-maṇḍalam ullasita-dṛg-anta-sūcitākūtam । namayantyāpi mukhāmbujam unnamitaṃ rāga-sāmrājyam ।। atra gaṇḍa-maṇḍala-vikāsa-dṛg-antollāsābhyāṃ nāyikāyāḥ smitaṃ vyajyate ।
tad eva lakṣya-daśana-śikharaṃ hasitaṃ bhavet ।। kiṃcid abhivyakta-daśana-śobhi mukham । ucchvasad iva paṅkajaṃ dṛṣṭam ।। atra kiñcid abhivyakta-daśanatvād idaṃ hasitam ।
tad eva kuñcitāpāṅga-gaṇḍaṃ madhura-niḥsvanam । kālocitaṃ sānurāgam uktaṃ vihasitaṃ bhavet ।। savidhe' pi mayy apaśyati śiśujana-ceṣṭā-vilokana-vyājāt । hasitaṃ smarāmi tasyāḥ sa-svanam ākuñcitāpāṅgam ।।
phulla-nāsā-puṭaṃ yat syān nikuñcita-śiro' ṃsakam । jihmāvaloka-nayanaṃ tac cāvahasitaṃ matam ।। saṃspṛṣṭa-mātraṃ patitaṃ vilokya । phullāgra-nāsaṃ hasitaṃ sakhībhiḥ ।।
kampitāṅgaṃ sāśru-netraṃ tac cāpahasitaṃ bhavet ।। gajāsye kṛṣṭāsye niviḍa-milad-anyonya-vadanam । hasan krīḍānṛtta-ślatha-calita-tundaḥ sa ca śiśuḥ ।। karopagūḍha-pārśvaṃ yad uddhatāyata-niḥsvanam ।
bāṣpākulākṣa-yugalaṃ tac cātihasitaṃ bhavet ।। sapadi saha veṇu-dāriṇā । sa jahāsa datta-kara-tālam uccakaiḥ ।। vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ ।
nītaḥ sadasya-rasyatvam utsāho vīra ucyate ।। eṣa tridhā samāsena dāna-yuddha-dayodbhavāḥ । dāna-vīro dhṛtir harṣo matyādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। smita-pūrvābhibhāṣitvaṃ smita-pūrvaṃ ca vīkṣitam ।
prasāde bahu-dātṛtvaṃ tadvad vācānumoditam । guṇāguṇa-vicārādyās tv anubhāvāḥ samīritāḥ ।। prabhuḥ prītaḥ prādād uparitana-pāda-dvaya-kṛte । gajendrānapy aṣṭau mada-mudita-kūjan madhulihaḥ ।।
yuddha-vīre harṣa-garvāmarṣādayā vyabhicāriṇā । asāhāyye' pi yuddhecchā samarād apalāyanam । bhītābhaya-pradānādyā vikārās tatra kīrtitāḥ ।। dṛptah sa rājanyakam eka-vīraḥ ।
kalpa-kṣayodvṛttam ivārṇavāmbhaḥ ।। dayā-vīre dhṛti-mati-pramukhā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । svārtha-prāṇa-vyayenāpi vipanna-trāṇa-śīlatā । āśvāsanoktayaḥ sthairyam ity ādyās tatra vikriyāḥ ।।
ārtaṃ kaṇṭha-gata-prāṇaṃ parityaktaṃ sva-bāndhavaiḥ । trāye nainaṃ yadi tataḥ kaḥ śarīreṇa me guṇaḥ ।। vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ । nītaḥ sadasya-rasyatvaṃ vismayo' dbhutatāṃ vrajet ।।
atra dhṛtyāvega-jāḍya-harṣādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । ceṣṭās tu netra-vistāra-svedāśru-pulakādayaḥ ।। tat tādṛk samarāṅgaṇeṣu bhujayor vikrāntam avyāhatam । smāraṃ smāram arātayaḥ pulakitā recarla-siṃha-prabhoḥ ।।
atra nāyaka-guṇātiśaya-janito virodhināṃ vismayaḥ smṛti-harṣādibhiḥ vyabhicāribhir upacitaḥ pulakādibhir anubhāvair vyajyamāno' dbhutatvam āpadyate । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ । krodhaḥ sadasya-rasyatvaṃ nīto raudra itīryate ।। āvega-garvaugryāmarṣa-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
prasveda-bhrukuṭī-netra-rāgādyās tatra vikriyāḥ ।। prāptodyogair yaugapadyād abhedyaiḥ । darpād andhair āniruddhir niruddhaḥ ।। atra vajra-viṣayo bhilla-varga-krodhaḥ svātmākṣepādibhir uddīpitā darpāndha-paruṣa-vāg-ārambhādy-anumitair garvāsūyādibhiḥ paripoṣitaḥ svoṣṭha-pīḍana-śatru-nirodhādibhir anubhāvair abhivyakto raudratayā niṣpadyate ।
vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ । nītaḥ sadasya-rasyatvaṃ śokaḥ karuṇa ucyate ।। atrāṣṭau sāttvikā jāḍya-nirveda-glāni-dīnatāḥ । ālasyāpasmṛti-vyādhi-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।
muhur bāṣpaṃ śvāsān malinam api rāgaṃ prakaṭayan । yuto dhatte glāniṃ karuṇa iva mūrto yadupatiḥ ।। atra bandhu-vyāpatti-janito vasudevasya śoko bandhu-guṇa-smaraṇādibhir uddīpito mlānatvendriya-śūnyatvādi-sūcitair dainya-moha-glānyādi-sañcāribhiḥ prapañcito muhur bāṣpa-śvāsa-malina-mukha-rāgādibhir anubhāvair abhivyaktaḥ karuṇatvam āpadyate । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ ।
jugupsā poṣam āpannā bībhatsatvena rasyate ।। atra glāni-śramonmāda-mohāpasmāra-dīnatāḥ । viṣāda-cāpalāvega-jāḍyādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । sveda-romāñca-nāmāgra-cchādanādyāś ca vikriyāḥ ।।
pūya-klinnaṃ vraṇam abhimṛśan vāsasaḥ khaṇḍakena । channa-ghrāṇaṃ racayati janaṃ dadru-rogī daridraḥ ।। atra dardu-rogi-viṣayā rathyā-jana-jugupsā makṣikā-pūyādibhir uddīpitā tvarāpasaraṇānumitair viṣādādibhiḥ poṣitā netra-saṅkocanādibhir abhivyaktā bībhatsatām āpnoti । vibhāvair anubhāvaiś ca svocitair vyabhicāribhiḥ ।
bhayaṃ sadasya-rasyatvaṃ nītaṃ proktaṃ bhayānakaḥ ।। tatra santrāsa-maraṇa-cāpalāvega-dīnatāḥ । viṣāda-mohāpasmāra-śaṅkādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । vikriyās tv āsya-śoṣādyāḥ sāttvikāś cāśru-varjitāḥ ।।
śuṣyat-tālu-puṭaṃ skhalat-pada-talaṃ vyālokayanto diśaḥ । anviṣyanti tad-antare' pi kara-saṃsparśena gartāntaram ।। atra nāyaka-pratibhūpatināṃ bhayaṃ tad-dhāṭī-śravaṇādinoddīpitaṃ vyākulatva-tālu-śoṣa-pada-skhalanādy-anumitair āvega-śaṅkātrāsādibhir vyabhicāribhir upacitaṃ palāyana-guhā-praveśa-gartāntarānveṣaṇādibhir anubhāvair anubhūyamānaṃ bhayānakatvena niṣpadyate । kecit samāna-balayo rasayoḥ saṅkaraṃ viduḥ ।
na parīkṣākṣamam idaṃ mataṃ prekṣāvatāṃ bhavet ।। tuṣyatve pūrva āsvādaḥ katarasyety aniścayāt । spardhāparatvād ubhayor anāsvāda-prasaṅgataḥ ।। tayor anyatarasyaiva prāyeṇāsvādanād api ।
yugapad rasanīyatvaṃ nobhayor upapadyate । eṣām aṅgāṅgi-bhāvena saṅkaro mama saṃmataḥ ।। bhāvo vāpi raso vāpi pravṛttir vṛttir eva vā । sarveṣāṃ samavetānāṃ rūpaṃ yasya bhaved bahu ।।
sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇo matāḥ ।। iti । tulādhṛtatvam anayor na syāt prakaraṇādinā । kavi-tātparya-viśrānter ekatraivāvalokanāt ।। ubhau śṛṅgāra-bībhatsāv ubhau vīra-bhayānakau ।
raudrādbhutāv ubhau hāsya-karuṇau prakṛti-dviṣau ।। svabhāva-vairiṇor aṅgāṅgi-bhāvenāpi miśraṇam । vivekibhyo na svadate gandha-gandhakayor iva ।। virodhino' pi sāṃnidhyād atiraskāra-lakṣaṇam ।
poṣaṇaṃ prakṛtasyeti ced aṅgatvaṃ na tāvatā ।। yat kiñcid upakāritvād aṅgasyāṅgitvam aṅgini । na tat-saṃnidhi-mātreṇa carvaṇānupakārataḥ ।। anyathā pānakādyeṣu śarkarāder ivāpatet ।
antarā patitasyāpi tṛṇāder upakāritā । tac carvaṇābhimāne syāt satṛṇābhyavahāritā ।। apy astu vā rudhira-bandhuritādharaṃ vā । saṃsāra-sāram idam eva mukhaṃ bhavatyāḥ ।।
atra śṛṅgāra-rasāṅgatām aṅgīkṛtavatā bībhatsena aṅgino' pi vicchedāya mūle kuṭhāro vyāpāritaḥ । evam anyeṣām api virodhinām aṅgāṅgi-bhāvenāsvādābhāvas tatra tatrodāharaṇe draṣṭavyaḥ । bhṛtyor nāyakasyeva nisarga-dveṣiṇor api । aṅgayor aṅgino vṛddhau bhaved ekatra saṅgatiḥ ।। nirmitsūnāṃ sva-vakṣasy atiparicayanāt tvat-praśastīr upāṃśu ।
ānavyājena lajjāṃ sapadi vidadhate svāvarodhe pragalbhāḥ ।। atra pratināyaka-gatayoḥ śṛṅgāra-bībhatsayoḥ nāyaka-gata-vīra-rasāṅgatvād ekatra samāveśo na doṣāya । nanv atra śatrūṇāṃ sva-vakṣasi nāyaka-viruda-vilekhanena jīvitānta-nirmita-sthānīyena janitā nija-jīvita-jugupsā svāvarodha-sāṃnidhyādibhir uddīpitā lajjānumitair nirveda-dainya-viṣādādibhir upacitā tad-anumitair eva mānasika-kutsādibhiḥ abhivyaktā satī nāyaka-gataṃ śaraṇāgata-rakṣā-lakṣaṇaṃ vīraṃ puṣṇātīti pratīyate । na punaḥ pratināyaka-gatasya śṛṅgārasya nāyaka-vīropakaraṇatvam, ucyate-nāyaka-kṛpā-kaṭākṣa-sthirīkṛta-rājyānāṃ pratināyakānāṃ tādṛśāḥ vinodāḥ sambhaveyuḥ । nānyatheti tasya śṛṅgārasya nāyaka-vīropakaraṇatva-viruda-dhāraṇādi-paricayena rājya-lakṣmī-sapatnī-pada-prayogeṇa cābhivyajyate । aṅgenāṅgī rasaḥ svecchā-vṛtti-vardhita-sampadā ।
amātyenāvinītena svāmīvābhāsatāṃ vrajet ।। śṛṅgāro hāsya-bhūyiṣṭhaḥ śṛṅgārābhāsa īritaḥ । hāsyo bībhatsa-bhūyiṣṭho hāsyābhāsa itīritaḥ ।। vīro bhayānaka-prāyo vīrābhāsa itīritaḥ ।
adbhutaḥ karuṇāśleṣād adbhutābhāsa ucyate ।। raudraḥ śoka-bhayāśleṣād raudrābhāsa itīritaḥ । karuṇo hāsya-bhūyiṣṭhaḥ karuṇābhāsa ucyate ।। bībhatso' dbhuta-śṛṅgārī bībhatsābhāsa ucyate ।
sa syād bhayānakābhāso raudra-vīropasaṅgamāt ।। iti । atra śṛṅgāra-rasasya arāgād aneka-rāgāt tiryag-rāgāt mleccha-rāgāc ceti caturvidham ābhāsa-bhūyastvam । tatra arāgas tv ekatra rāgābhāvaḥ । tena rasasyābhāsatvaṃ, yathā- bhavitrī rambhoru tridaśa-vadana-glānir adhunā । laghiṣṭhedaṃ ṣaṣṭhākṣara-para-vilopāt paṭha punaḥ ।।
atra sītāyāṃ rāvaṇa-viṣaya-rāgātyantābhāvād ābhāsatvam । nanv ekatra rāgābhāvād rasasyābhāsatvaṃ na yujyate । prathamam ajātānurāge vatsa-rāje jātānurāgāyāḥ ratnāvalyāḥ- dullaha-jaṇāṇurāo lajjā guruī parabbaso appā । pia-sahi visamaṃ pemmaṃ maraṇaṃ saraṇaṃ nu varam ekkaṃ ।।
[durlabha-janānurāgo lajjā gurvī para-vaśa ātmā । priya-sakhi viṣamaṃ prema maraṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ nu varam ekam ।।] ity atra pūrvānurāgasyābhāsatva-prasaṅga iti ced ucyate । abhāvo hi trividhaḥ prāg-abhāvo' tyantābhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsābhāvaś ceti । tatra prāg-abhāve darśanādi-kāraṇeṣu sambhāviteṣu rāgotpatti-sambhāvanayā nābhāsatvam । itarayos tu kāraṇa-sad-bhāve' pi rāgānutpatter ābhāsatvam eva । anye tu striyā eva rāgābhāve rasasyābhāsatvaṃ pratijānate । puruṣe' pi rāgābhāve rasasyānāsvādanīyatvāt । yathā- nivṛtte sad-bhāve jana iva jane gacchati puraḥ ।
na jāne ko hetur dalati śatadhā yan na hṛdayam ।। atra hṛdaya-dalanābhāva-pūrva-gata-divasotprekṣādy-anumitair nirveda-smṛty-ādibhir abhivyakto' pi striyā anurāgaḥ premāveśa-ślathanādi-kathitena puruṣa-gata-rāga-dhvaṃsanena cārutāṃ nāpnoti । paśyānaṅga-śarāturaṃ janam imaṃ trātāpi no rakṣasi । serṣyaṃ māra-vadhūbhir ity abhihito buddho jinaḥ pātu vaḥ ।।
atra jinasya rāgātyantābhāvena rasābhāsatvam । utkrāntavāyvoḥ samakālam eva । ekāpsaraḥ-prārthanayor vivādaḥ ।। atra kasyāścid divya-vanitāyā vīra-dvaye raṇānivṛtti-maraṇa-prāpta-devatābhāve anurāgasya nirupamānaśūra-guṇopādher avaiṣamyeṇa pratibhāsanādābhāsatvam ।
citraṃ vakti tilottamā paricayaṃ nānāṅga-hāra-krame । bheje śrī-yanapota-siṃha-nṛpate tvat-khaḍga-bhinnātmanā ।। atra nāyaka-khaḍga-dhārā-galitātmanaḥ kasyacit svarga-pratināyaka-vīrasya menakādi-svarloka-gaṇikāsu avaiṣamyeṇa rāgād ābhāsatvam । nanv evaṃ dakṣiṇādīnām api rāgasyābhāsatvam iti cet, na । dakṣiṇasya nāyakasya nāyikāsu anekāsu vṛtti-mātreṇaiva sādhāraṇyam । na rāgeṇa । tad ekasyām eva rāgasya prauḍhatvam । itarāsu tu madhyamatvaṃ mandatvaṃ ceti tad-anurāgasya nābhāsatā । atra tu avaiṣamyeṇa anekatra pravṛtter ābhāsatvam upapadyate ।
papau priyāṃ svām anuvartamānaḥ । mṛgīm akaṇḍūyata kṛṣṇa-sāraḥ ।। ajjaṃ mohaṇa-suhiaṃ muatti mottū palāie halie । dara-phuḍia-beṇṭa-bhāroṇaāi hasiaṃ ba phalahīe ।।
[āryāṃ mohana-sukhitāṃ mṛteti muktvā palāyite halike । dara-sphuṭita-vṛnta-bhārāvanatayā hasitam iva kārpāsyā ।।] atra surata-mohana-supti-maraṇa-daśayor vivekābhāvena hālikasya mlecchatvaṃ gamyate । nanu tiryaṅ-mleccha-gatayor ābhāsatvaṃ na yujyate । tayor vibhāvādi-sambhavāt । āsvāda-yogyatā-pratīter iti cet, na । bho mleccha-rasa-vādin ! uktalādhipateḥ śṛṅgāra-rasābhimānino narasiṃhadevasya cittam anuvartamānena vidyādhareṇa kavinā bāḍham abhyantarī-kṛto' si । evaṃ khalu samarthitam ekāvalyām anena-
apare tu rasābhāsaṃ tiryakṣu pracakṣate । tan na parīkṣā-kṣamam । teṣv api vibhāvādi-sambhavāt । vibhāvādi-jñāna-śūnyās tiryañco na bhājanaṃ bhavitum arhanti rasasyeti cet, na । manuṣyeṣv api keṣucit tathā-bhūteṣu rasa-viṣaya-bhāvābhāva-prasaṅgāt । vibhāvādi-sambhavo hi rasaṃ prati prayojakaḥ । na vibhāvādi-jñānam । tataś ca tiraścām apy asty eva rasaḥ iti । na tāvat tiraścāṃ vibhāvatam upapadyate । śṛṅgāre hi samujjvalasya śucino darśanīyasyaiva vastuno muninā vibhāvatvenāmnātam । tiraścam udvartana-majjanākalpa-racanādy-abhāvād ujjvala-śuci-darśanīyatvānām asambhāvanā prasiddhaiva । atha sva-jāti-yogyair dharmaiḥ kāriṇāṃ kariṇīṃ prati padye iva) vibhāvatvam iti cen, na । tasyāṃ kakṣyāyāṃ kariṇāṃ kariṇī-rāgaṃ prati kāraṇatvaṃ na punar vibhāvatvam । kiṃ ca, jāti-yogyair dharmair vastuno na vibhāvatvam । api tu bhāvaka-cittollāsa-hetubhiḥ rati-viśiṣṭair eva ।
kiṃ ca, vibhāvādi-jñānaṃ nāma aucitya-vivekaḥ । tena śūnyās tiryañco na vibhāvatām arhanti । tarhi vibhāvādi-jñāna-rahiteṣu manuṣyeṣu rasābhāsa-prasaṅga iti cet, naiṣa doṣaḥ । viveka-rahita-janopalakṣaṇa-mleccha-gatasya rasasyābhāsatve sveṣṭāvāpteḥ । kiṃ ca vibhāvādi-sambhavo hi rasaṃ prati prayojako na vibhāvādi-jñānam ity etan na yujyate । tathā hi-vibhāvāder viśiṣṭasya vastu-mātrasya vā sambhavo rasaṃ prati prayojakaḥ । viśiṣṭa-prayojakatvāṅgīkāre vivekādi-praveśo' ṅgīkṛta iti asmad-anusaraṇam eva śaraṇaṃ gato' si । atra vivekaṃ vinā tad-itara-viśeṣavattvaṃ vaiśiṣṭyam iti cen, na । viśeṣāṇāṃ dharmiṇi paramotkarṣānusandhāna-tat-parāṇām anyonya-sahiṣṇūnām iyattayā niyamāsambhavāt ।
atha yadi vastu-mātrasya tarhi anvāsitam arundhatyā svāhayeva havir bhujam ity ādāv api strī-puṃsa-vyakti-mātra-vibhāva-sad-bhāvād anvāsanālakṣaṇānubhāva-sambhavāc ca śṛṅgāraḥ svadanīyaḥ prasajyeta । kiṃ ca- ajjaṃ mohaṇa-suhiaṃ muatti mottū palāie halie । dara-phuḍia-beṇṭa-bhāroṇaāi hasiaṃ ba phalahīe ।। saṅkhyaka-padyaṃ draṣṭavyam ।
ity ādiṣu strī-puṃsa-vyakti-mātra-vibhāva-sadbhāvaḥ sphuṭa eva । tad-aviveka-janita-hāsya-paṅka-nirmagnaṃ śṛṅgāra-gandha-gajam uddhartuṃ tvaratām ity alaṃ rasābhāsāpalāpa-saṃrambheṇa । nanu sītādi-vibhāvair vastu-mātrair eva yoṣin-mātra-pratītau sāmājikānāṃ rasodayaḥ । na punar viśiṣṭaiḥ । tat katham iti ced, ucyate । atra janaka-tanayatva-rāma-parigrahatvādi-viruddha-dharma-parihāreṇa lalitojjvala-śuci-darśanīyatvādi-viśiṣṭa eva śabdataḥ । sītādi-vibhāvo yoṣit-sāmānyaṃ tādṛśam eva jñāpayati । na punaḥ strī-jāti-mātram iti sakalam api kalyāṇam । vilāse vāgīśo mahati niyame nīti-nigame । vrateṣu śrī-siṃha-kṣitipatir udāro viharate ।।
saundaryaṃ sundarīṇāṃ hariṇa-vijayināṃ vāgurā locanānām । vijñānaṃ sarva-vidyā-nidhi-budha-pariṣac-chemuṣī-bhāgya-rekhā ।। ।। kaṭhora-pārāvata-kaṇṭha-nīlaḥ ।
paraḥ pumān raja-mahīdhra-vāsī ।। bhavatv iti sambandhaḥ smaraṇīyaḥ । tad īdṛśa-rasādhāraṃ nāṭyaṃ rūpakam ity api । naṭasyātipravīṇasya karmatvān nāṭyam ucyate ।।
yathā mukhādau padmāder ārope rūpaka-prathā । tathaiva nāyakāropo naṭe rūpakam ucyate । tac ca nāṭyaṃ daśa-vidhaṃ vākyārthābhinayātmakam ।। nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇam aṅko vyāyoga eva ca ।
bhāṇaḥ samavakāraś ca vīthī prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ । īhāmṛgaś ca vijñeyo daśadhā nāṭya-lakṣaṇam ।। rasetivṛtta-netāras tat-tad-rūpaka-bhedakāḥ । lakṣitau rasanetārāv itivṛttaṃ tu kathyate ।।
itivṛtta-kathā-vastu-śabdāḥ paryāya-vācinaḥ । itivṛttaṃ prabandhasya śarīraṃ trividhaṃ hi tat ।। khyātaṃ kalpyaṃ ca saṅkīrṇaṃ khyātaṃ rāma-kathādikam । kavi-buddhi-kṛtaṃ kalpyaṃ mālatī-mādhavādikam ।।
saṅkīrṇam ubhayāyattaṃ lava-rāghava-ceṣṭitam । lakṣyeṣv etat tu bahudhā divya-martyādi-bhedataḥ ।। tac cetivṛttaṃ vidvadbhiḥ pañcadhā parikīrtitam । bījaṃ binduḥ patākā ca prakarī kāryam ity api ।।
yat tu svalpam upakṣiptaṃ bahudhā vistṛtiṃ gatam । kāryasya kāraṇaṃ prājñais tad bījam iti kathyate । uptaṃ bījaṃ taror yadvad aṅkurādi-prabhedataḥ ।। phalāya kalpate tadvan nāyakādi-vibhedataḥ ।
phalāyaitad bhaved yasmād bījam ity abhidhīyate ।। yathā bāla-rāmāyaṇe prathama-dvitīyāṅkayoḥ kalpite mukha-sandhau svalpo rāmotsāho bījam ity ucyate । phale pradhāne bījasya prasaṅgoktaiḥ phalāntaraiḥ । vicchinne yad aviccheda-kāraṇaṃ bindur ucyate ।।
jala-bindur yathā siñcaṃs taru-mūlaṃ phalāya hi । tathaivāyam upakṣipto bindur ity abhidhīyate ।। yathā tatraiva tṛtīya-caturthāṅkayoḥ kalpite pratimukha-sandhau nikṣipto rāvaṇa-virodha-mūlaṃ sītā-parigraho bindur ucyate । yat pradhānopakaraṇa-prasaṅgāt svārtham ṛcchati ।
sā syāt patākā sugrīva-makarandādi-vṛttavat ।। yat kevalaṃ parārthasya sādhakaṃ ca pradeśa-bhāk । prakarī sā samuddiṣṭā nava-vṛndādi-vṛttavat ।। yathā patākā kasyāpi śobhākṛc cihna-rūpataḥ ।
svasyopanāyakādīnāṃ vṛttāntas tadvad ucyate ।। śobhāyai vedikādīnāṃ yathā puṣpākṣatādayaḥ । tatha rtu-varṇanādis tu prasaṅge prakarī bhavet ।। iti । aṅgasya ca pradhānasya bhāvyavasthasya sūcakam ।
yad āgantuka-bhāvena patākā-sthānakaṃ hi tat ।। etad dvidhā tulya-saṃvidhānaṃ tulya-viśeṣaṇam । tatrādyaṃ tri-prakāraṃ syād dvitīyaṃ tv ekam eva hi । evaṃ caturvidhaṃ jñeyaṃ patākā-sthānakaṃ budhaiḥ ।।
sahasaivārtha-sampattir guṇavaty upacārataḥ । patākā-sthānakam idaṃ prathamaṃ parikīrtitam ।। iti । vidūṣakaḥ- bhoḥ ! esā kkhu abarā debī bāsabadattā । ity atra iyaṃ vāsavattety anenopacāra-prayogeṇa bhāvino vāsavadattā-kopasya sūcanāt sahasārtha-sampatti-rūpam idam ekaṃ patākā-sthānakam ।
vacaḥ sātiśayaṃ śliṣṭaṃ kāvya-bandha-samāśrayam । patākā-sthānakam idaṃ dvitīyaṃ parikīrtitam ।। iti । asāv asyāḥ sparśo vapuṣi bahalaś candana-rasaḥ । kim asyā na preyo yadi param asahyas tu virahaḥ ।।
pratīhārī-deva upasthitaḥ । rāmaḥ-aye kaḥ ? ity atra bhaviṣyataḥ sītā-virahasya sūcanād idaṃ śliṣṭaṃ nāma dvitīyaṃ patākā-sthānakam । arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yatra līnaṃ sa-vinayaṃ bhavet । śliṣṭa-pratyuttaropetaṃ tṛtīyam idam iṣyate ।।
tvad-dṛṣṭi-hāri mama locana-bāndhavasya । paryāptam eva karabhoru maoru-yugmam ।। kañcukī-deva bhagnam । deva bhagnam ! kañcukī-deva bhīmena ।
ity atra śliṣṭa-pratyuttareṇa kañcuki-vākyena bhāvino duryodhanoru-bhaṅgasya sūcanena śliṣṭottaraṃ nāma tṛtīyam idaṃ patākā-sthānakam । dvy-artho vacana-vinyāsaḥ suśliṣṭaḥ kāvya-yojitaḥ । upanyāsa-suyuktaś ca tac caturtham udāhṛtam ।। iti । āyāsaṃ śvasanodgamair aviralair ātanvatīm ātmanaḥ ।
paśyan kopa-vipāṭala-dyuti mukhaṃ devyāḥ kariṣyāmy aham ।। ity atra viśeṣaṇa-śleṣeṇa bhāvino ratnāvalī-sandarśanasya sūcanāt tulya-viśeṣaṇaṃ nāma caturthaṃ patākā-sthānakam idam । vastunas tu samastasya dharma-kāmārtha-lakṣaṇam । phalaṃ kāryam iti śuddhaṃ miśraṃ vā kalpayet sudhīḥ ।।
tat puṇyair mad-upakramaiś ca phalitaṃ kleśo' pi mac-chiṣyayoḥ । samprītau nṛpa-nandanau yad aparaṃ preyas tad apy ucyatām ।। ity atra kāvyopasaṃhāra-ślokena tṛtīya-puruṣārthasyaiva phala-kathanāt śuddhaṃ kāryam idam । setuś ca grathitaḥ prasanna-madhuro dṛṣṭaś ca vārāṃ nidhiḥ ।
prāptaṃ yānam idaṃ ca yācitavate dattaṃ kuberāya ca ।। ity anenopasaṃhāra-ślokena miśrasya trivarga-phalasya kathanān miśram idam । pradhānam aṅgam iti ca tad vastu dvividhaṃ punaḥ । pradhānaṃ netṛ-caritaṃ pradhāna-phala-bandhi ca ।।
kāvye vyāpi pradhānaṃ tad yathā rāmādi-ceṣṭitam । nāyakārtha-kṛd-aṅgaṃ syān nāyaketara-ceṣṭitam ।। nityaṃ patākā prakarī cāṅgaṃ bījādayaḥ kvacit । bījatvād bījam ādau syāt phalatvāt kāryam antataḥ ।।
tayoḥ sandhān a-hetutvān madhye binduṃ prakalpayet । yathāyogaṃ patākāyāḥ prakaryāś ca niyojanam ।। kāryasya pañcadhāvasthā nāyakādi-kriyā-vaśāt । ārambha-yatna-prāpty-āśā-niyatāpti-phalāgamāḥ ।
tatra mukhya-phalodyoga-mātram ārambha iṣyate ।। yathā bāla-rāmāyaṇe mukha-sandhau rāmasya lokottarotkarṣa-prāptaye vyavasāya-mātram ārambhaḥ । yatnas tu tat-phala-prāptyām autsukyena tu vartanam ।। yathā tatraiva pratimukha-sandhau tāṭaka-pātana-bhūta-pati-dhanur-dalanādiṣu rāmasya yatnaḥ ।
prāpty-āśā tu mahārthasya siddhi-sadbhāva-bhāvanā ।। yathā tatraiva garbha-sandhau mālavan māyā-prayoga-vana-pravāsa-sītāpaharaṇādibhir antaritāyāḥ rāmasya paramotkarṣa-prāpter dhanur-bhaṅgādi-sugrīva-sandhi-setu-bandhanādibhiḥ siddhi-sad-bhāva-bhāvanā-kathanāt prāpty-āśā । niyatāptir avighnena kārya-saṃsiddhi-niścayaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva vimarśa-sandhau nikhila-rakṣaḥ-kula-nibarhaṇād avighnena rāmasya phala-saṃsiddhi-niścayo niyatāptiḥ ।
samagreṣṭa-phalāvāptir bhaved eva phalāgamaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva nirvahaṇa-sandhau rāmasya tātājñā-nirbahaṇa-vaira-praśamana-rājyopabhogair lokottara-trivarga-phalasyāvāptiḥ phalāgamaḥ । ekaikasyās tv avasthāyāḥ prakṛtyā caikayaikayā । yogaḥ sandhir iti jñeyo nāṭya-vidyā-viśāradaiḥ ।।
patākāyās tv avasthānaṃ kvacid asti na vā kvacit । patākā-virahe bījaṃ binduṃ vā kalpayet sudhīḥ ।। mukhya-prayojana-vaśāt kathāṅgānāṃ samanvaye । avāntarārtha-sambandhaḥ sandhiḥ sandhāna-rūpataḥ ।।
mukha-pratimukhe garbha-vimarśāv upasaṃhṛtiḥ । teṣu yatra bīja-samudbhavaḥ ।। nānā-vidhānām arthānāṃ rasānām api kāraṇam । tan mukhaṃ tatra cāṅgāni bījārambhānurodhataḥ ।।
upakṣepaḥ parikaraḥ parinyāso vilobhanam । yuktiḥ prāptiḥ samādhānaṃ vidhānaṃ paribhāvanā । udbheda-bhedau karaṇam iti dvādaśa yojayet ।। upakṣepas tu bījasya sūcanā kathyate budhaiḥ ।।
śunaḥśepaḥ-prātaḥsavana eva yajamānaṃ draṣṭum icchāmiity upakramyaà rākṣasa-rakṣauṣadhaṃ rāmam ānetuṃ siddhāśramād ayodhyāṃ gatavatā tāta-viśvāmitreṇa yajñopanimantritasya parama-suhṛdaḥ śrotriya-kṣatriyasya sīradhvajasya sva-pratinidhiḥ preṣito' smi ity antena ( padyāt pūrvam] rāvaṇādi-duṣṭa-rākṣasa-śikṣā-lakṣaṇa-rāmotsāhopabṛṃhaka-viśvāmitrārambha-rūpasya bījasya sūcanād upakṣepaḥ । parikriyā tu bījasya bahulīkaraṇaṃ matam ।। jñātuṃ pravṛttiṃ kuśikātmajasya । tāṃ cāpy ayodhyāṃ raghu-rājadhānīm ।।
kula-putraketi saprasāmad āśliṣṭo' smi ity upakramyaà sa hi naktaṃ-carāṇāṃ nisargāmitro viśvāmitro vrata-caryayā, vīra-vrata-caryayā samartho daśaratho' pi tathāvidha eva eva ( padyād anantaraṃ] ity antena viśvāmitrārambhasya mālyavadādi-vitarka-gocaratvena bahulīkaraṇāt parikaraḥ । bīja-niṣpatti-kathanaṃ parinyāsa itīryate ।। yathā tatraiva rākṣasaḥ -kathaṃ tāpasaḥ । tatrāpi viśvāmitra-dharma-putraḥ śunaḥśepaḥ ity upakramyaà sampraty eva rākṣasa-bhayāt satre dīkṣiṣyamāṇaḥ sa bhagavān goptāraṃ rāmabhadraṃ varītum ayodhyāṃ gataḥ । rākṣasaḥ -hanta katham etad api niṣpannam । bhagavan mā kopīḥ ity ādinā kṛtaṃ yat kartavyam । samprati cāra-sañcārasyāyam avasaraḥ ( padyād anantaram] ity antena viśvāmitrānubhāva-kathanāt sarākṣatrāsa-kathanāc ca bīja-niṣpatteḥ parinyāsaḥ । nāyakādi-guṇānāṃ yad varṇanaṃ tad vilobhanam ।।
yasyāropaṇa-karmaṇāpi bahavo vīra-vrataṃ tyājitāḥ ।। kāntiḥ prāvaraṇaṃ tanor madhumuco yasyāś ca vācaḥ kila । tāṃ draṣṭuṃ janakātmajāṃ hṛdaya he netrāṇi mitrīkuru ।। ity antena tad-guṇa-varṇanād vilobhanam ।
samyak prayojanānāṃ hi nirṇayo yuktir iṣyate ।। bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ -aye nirūpatāpi kvacin mahate' bhuyadayāya ity upakramya, bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ-ām, nārada yathā samarthayase । tathā hi- laṅkām ekaḥ kuberād ahṛta vasataye koṅkaṇānabdhito' nyaḥ । tat kāmaṃ karma-sāmyāt kim aparam anayor madhyagā vīra-lakṣmīḥ ।।
ity antena rāghava-pratināyakayor bhārgava-rāvaṇayoḥ karma-sāmya-nirṇaya-kathanād yuktiḥ । prājñaiḥ sukhasya samprāptiḥ prāptir ity abhidhīyate ।। mokṣa-dvāram apāvṛtaṃ mama manaḥ-prahlādanā-bheṣajam । sarve paśyata rāma-rāvaṇa-raṇaṃ vakty eṣa vo nāradaḥ ।।
ity atra nāradasya yuddhāvalokana-harṣa-prāpteḥ prāptiḥ । bījasya punar ādhānaṃ samādhānam ihocyate ।। yathā tatraiva bhṛṅgiriṭiḥ-yuddha-ruce mā nirbharaṃ saṃrambhasva । ayodhyāṃ gatvā paraṃ rāma-rāvaṇīyaṃ yojayiṣyāmi ( padyād anantaram] ity antena rāghavotsāha-bījasya nāradena punar ādhānāt samādhānam । sukha-duḥkha-karaṃ yat tu tad vidhānaṃ budhā viduḥ ।।
yathā tatraiva prathamāṅke, sītā -ammo rakkhaso tti suṇia saccaṃ sajjhasa-kodahalāṇaṃ majjhe baṭṭāmi । ity upakramya sītā-tādasadānaṃdamissāṇaṃ antare ubabisissaṃ । ( padyāt pūrvam] ity antena sītāyāḥ adṛṣṭa-pūrva-rākṣasa-darśanena sukha-duḥkha-vyatikarākhyānād vidhānam । ślāghyaiś citta-camatkāro guṇādyaiḥ paribhāvanā ।। yathā tatraiva, rāvaṇaḥ -aho tribhuvanātiśāyi makaradhvaja-sañjīvanaṃ rāmaṇīyakam asyāḥ । tathā hi- pramlānāruṇimeva vidrumalatā śyāmeva hema-prabhā ।
sītāyāḥ purataś ca hanta śikhināṃ barhāḥ sagarhā iva ।। ity upakramya, śatānandaḥ -aho laṅkādhipater apūrva-garva-garimā । yan mamāpi śatānandasya na niścinute cetaḥ । kiṃ bhaviṣyati ( padyād anantaram] ity antena rāvaṇasya sītā-rāmaṇīyaka-darśanena śatānandasya rāvaṇotsāha-darśanena ca tayoś citta-camatkāra-kathanāt paribhāvanā । udghātanaṃ yad bījasya sa udbhedaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva dvitīyāṅke, rāvaṇaḥ-traiyāmbakaḥ paraśur eṣa nisarga-caṇḍa ity ādi paṭhati । jāmadagnyaḥ-apakurvatāpi bhavatā param upakṛtam । yad eṣa smārito' smīty upakramya ( padyāt pūrvam]-
puṃsāṃ kulaṃ na hi nimittam udāratāyāḥ । līlāyitaṃ punar amuṣya samudra-pānam ।। ity antena gūḍha-śaṅkara-dhanur adhikṣepodghāṭanād vā lokottara-carita-sāmānya-varṇanena tirohita-rāmacandrotsāhodghāṭanād vā udbhedaḥ । bījasyottejanaṃ bhedo yad vā saṅghāta-bhedanam ।।
yathā tatraiva rāvaṇaḥ -atha yācita-paraśunā paraśurāmeṇa kim abhihitam āsīt । māyāmayaḥ-trailokya-māṇikya rāmodantam ākarṇayatu svāmī । deyo naiṣa hara-prasāda-paraśus tenādhikaṃ tāmyati । tubhyaṃ brūhi rasātala-tridivayor nirjitya kiṃ dīyatām ।।
rāvaṇaḥ-kadā nu khalu paraśurāmo rasātala-tridivayor jetā dātā ca saṃvṛttaḥ । rāvaṇaḥ punaḥ pratigrahītā ca । tatas tvayā kim asau pratyuktaḥ । ity upakramya māyāmayaḥ-deva prakṛti-roṣaṇo reṇukāputraḥ । tat tam evāgatam aham utprekṣe । rāvaṇaḥ-priyaṃ naḥ ( padyāt pūrvam] ity antena pratināyaka-rūpa-bhārgava-rāvaṇayor uttejanād bhedaḥ । prastutārtha-samārambhaṃ karaṇaṃ paricakṣate ।।
yathā tatraiva ( padyād anantaram] ubhāv api cāpāropaṇaṃ nāṭayataḥ ity upakramya ā aṅka-parisamāpteḥ jāmadagnya-rāvaṇayoḥ prastuta-yuddhārambha-kathanāt karaṇam । bīja-prakāśanaṃ yatra dṛśyādṛśyatayā bhavet । tat syāt pratimukhaṃ bindoḥ prayatnasyānurodhataḥ ।। iha trayodaśāṅgāni prayojyāni manīṣibhiḥ ।
vilāsa-parisarpau ca vidhutaṃ śama-narmaṇī ।। narma-dyutiḥ pragamanaṃ nirodhaḥ paryupāsanam । puṣpaṃ vajram upanyāso varṇa-saṅgrahanaṃ tathā ।। vilāsaḥ saṅgamārthas tu vyāpāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
laulyāc cakṣuḥ prahitam amunā sāṅga-bhaṅgaḥ sthito' yam । straiṇaḥ puṃsāṃ nava-parigamaḥ kāmam unmāda-hetuḥ ।। ity antena rāmādīnāṃ sītālambanābhilāṣa-kathanād vilāsaḥ । pūrva-dṛṣṭasya bījasya tv aṅka-cchedādinā tathā ।
naṣṭasyānusmṛtiḥ śaśvat parisarpa iti smṛtaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva pratīhāraḥ -katham ete kṣatriya-jana-samucite' pi cāpāropaṇa-karmaṇi nikhilāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vitatha-sāmarthyāḥ vartante । tad eṣa param anākalita-sāro vikartana-kula-kumāra āste । yad vā, kim anenāpi- yasya vajra-maṇer bhede bhidyante loha-sūcayaḥ । karotu tatra kiṃ nāma nārī-nakha-viḍambanam ।।
bhavatu । tathāpi saṅkīrtayāmy enam । anākalita-sāro hi vīra-prakāṇḍa-sambhūtiḥ ity upakramya । hemaprabhā-saṃpaṇṇaṃ ca pia-sahīe pāṇi-ggahaṇam ity antena pūrvaṃ tāṭakādi-vadha-dṛṣṭasya paścān nikhila-kṣatriya-durāropa-dhūrjaṭi-cāpāropaṇa-prabhāva-varṇanād naṣṭasya rāmabhadrotsāhasya tad-dhanur-bhaṅga-kriyā-rūpeṇa smaraṇāt parisarpaḥ । nāyakāder īpsitānām arthānām anavāptitaḥ । aratir yad bhaved tad dhi vidvadbhir vidhutaṃ matam ।
athavānunayotkarṣaṃ vidhutaṃ syān nirākṛtiḥ ।। yasyāste jananī svayaṃ kṣitir ayaṃ yogīśvaras te pitā ।। ity ārabhya, rāmaḥ -rudaty api kamanīyā jānakī-ity antena -bhagavan bhārgava sadayaṃ prasīda ity ārabhya, jāmadagnyaḥ-nābhivādana-prasādyo reṇukā-sūnuḥ ( padyāt pūrvam] ity atra rāmānunayasya bhārgaveṇāsvīkārād vidhūtam । arateḥ śamanaṃ taj-jñāḥ śamam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
yathā tatraiva hemaprabhā-jujjai paphulla-kodūhala-ttaṇaṃ । parasurāma-daṃsaṇeṇa uṇa sasajjha-sattaṇaṃ bhagga-dhana-ddaṇḍa-caṇḍa-caritassa purado rāmacaṃdassa । ity atra rāmacandra-parākrama-kathanāt sītāyāḥ arati-śamanāt śamaḥ । parihāsa-pradhānaṃ yad vacanaṃ narma tad viduḥ ।। mad-dor-daṇḍa-haṭhāñcanena tad idaṃ bhagnaṃ kṛta-nyak-kṛti । nikṣeptre nata-kandharo bhagavate rudrāya kiṃ dāsyati ।।
ity atra janakādhipāpalāpena hāsa-pradhānaṃ narma । kopasyāpahnavārthaṃ yad dhāsyaṃ narma-dyutir matā ।। vāme bāhāv uta tad-itare kāryataḥ ko viśeṣaḥ । tat tvāṃ yāce virama kalahād āryakarmārabhasva ।।
jāmadagnyaḥ mātur mātula na kiṃcid antaraṃ bhavato bhavānīvallabhasya ca । rāmaḥ jāmadagnya ! ekaḥ punar ayaṃ śastra-grahaṇādhikāro yad guruṣv api tiraskāraḥ ity antena bhārgava-rāghavayoḥ pūjya-viṣaya-krodhāpahnavārthaṃ hāsya-kathanān narma-dyutiḥ । tat tu pragamanaṃ yat syād uttarottara-bhāṣaṇam ।। kiṃ punar imāḥ sarvaṅkaṣā roṣa-vācaḥ ।
