sarvatyāgī pariṇata-vayāḥ saptamaḥ padma-yoneḥ ।। jāto yatra guhaś cakāra ca bhuvaṃ yad gīta-vīra-vratām । helojjṛmbhita-jṛmbhakeṇa dhanuṣā kṣatraṃ ca nālaṃ vayam ।। jāmadagnyaḥ sādhu re kṣatriya-ḍimbha, sādhu । ity antena bhārgava-rāghavayor ukti-pratyukti-kathanāt pragamanam ।
yatra vyasanam āyāti nirodhaḥ sa nigadyate ।। pakva-karpūra-niṣpeṣam ayaṃ nirapiṣat trayam । mama vrīḍāṃ ca caṇḍīśa-cāpaṃ ca svaṃ ca jīvitam ।। prahiṇu tad iha bāṇān vārdhakaṃ māṃ dunoti ।।
daśarathaḥ-bhoḥ sambandhin kṛtaṃ kārmuka-parigraha-vyasanena-ity antena janakasya bhārgava-nimittasya jarā-nimittasya vā vyasanasya kathanād nirodhaḥ । ruṣṭasyānunayo yaḥ syāt paryupāsanam īritam ।। rāmaḥ śiṣyo bhṛgu-suta bhavān bhāgineyī-suto me ।। ity atra śloke roṣāndhasya bhārgavasyānunayo viśvāmitreṇa kṛta iti paryupāsanam ।
sa-viśeṣābhidhānaṃ yat puṣpaṃ tad iti saṃjñitam ।। karpūra iva dagdho' pi śaktimān yo jane jane ।। ity upakramya, prakaṭita-rāmāmbhojaḥ kauśikavā sapadi lakṣmaṇānandī । sura-cāpa-namana-hetor ayam avatīrṇaḥ śarat-samayaḥ ।।
ity ante rāmacandra-lakṣaṇārtha-viśeṣābhidhānāt puṣpam । vajraṃ tad iti vijñeyaṃ sākṣān niṣṭhura-bhāṣaṇam ।। prasṛta-rudhira-dhārā-carcitoccaṇḍa-ruṇḍam । paraśur amara-vandyaḥ khaṇḍayaty adya muṇḍam ।।
ity upakramya, yaḥ preta-nāthasyātithyam anubhavitu-kāma ity antena vajra-niṣṭhura-bhāṣaṇād vajram । yuktibhiḥ sahito yo' rthaḥ upanyāsaḥ sa iṣyate ।। yad vā te guravo' vicintya-caritās tebhyo' yam astv añjaliḥ ।। ity antena upapattibhiḥ pitur nideśa-karaṇād api mātṛ-vadha-karaṇasyaiva pratipādanād vā gurūṇām avicintya-caritatvopanyāsena sarvopapannatva-pratipādanād vā upanyāsaḥ ।
sarva-varṇopagamanaṃ varṇa-saṃhāra ucyate ।। yathā tatraiva jāmadagnyaḥ -kiṃ brūtha ? kena na varṇitaṃ dāśaratheḥ śaṅkara-kārmukāropaṇam ? ko na vismitas tad-bhaṅgena ? śṛṇuta bhoḥ । draṣṭā yaś ca parīkṣitā ca ya iha stotā ca vaktā ca yaḥ ।। rāmo rāma-mayaṃ svayaṃ guha-sahādhyāyī samanviṣyati ।।
ity antena hara-cāpa-dalanasya niṣiddhayā kartṛtayā anumantṛtayā stotṛtayā ca rāghava-viśvāmitra-pīrādi-parāmarśena brāhmaṇa-kṣatriyādi-varṇānāṃ saṅgrahaṇād varṇa-saṃhāraḥ । dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasya bījasya garbhas tv anveṣaṇaṃ muhuḥ । atrāpy ācāpatākānurodhād aṅgāni kalpayet ।। abhūtāharaṇaṃ mārgo rūpodāharaṇe kramaḥ ।
saṅgrahaś cānumānaṃ ca toṭakādhibale tathā । udvegaḥ sambhramāksepau dvādaśaiṣāṃ tu lakṣaṇam ।। abhūtāharaṇam tat syād vākyaṃ yat kapaṭāśrayam ।। yayā tatraiva unmatta-daśānana-nāmani pañcamāṅke mālyavān -vṛddha-buddhir hi prathamaṃ paśyati caramaṃ kāryam । yan mayā dhūrjaṭi-dhanur-adhikṣepataḥ prabhṛti mati-cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam eva yad uta daśakandharo' nusandhāsyati sītā-haraṇam ।
mālyavān tataś ca mayā mandodarī-pitur māyā-guror mayasya prathama-śiṣyo viśārada-nāmā yantra-kāraḥ sa-bahumānaṃ niyuktaḥ sītā-pratikṛti-karaṇāya । viracitā ca sā rāvaṇopacchandanārtham । abhihitaṃ ca- sūtra-dhāra-calad-dāru-gātreyaṃ yantra-jānakī । vaktrastha-śārikālāpa laṅkendraṃ vañcayiṣyati ।। ity upakramya, rāvaṇaḥ aho matimān māyāmayaḥ । chālito' si janaka-rāja-putryāḥ pratikṛti-samarpaṇena ( padyād anantaram] ity antena mālyavat kapaṭa-vākya-saṃvidhānād abhūtāharaṇam ।
mārgas tattvārtha-kathanam ।। yathā tatraiva nirdoṣa-daśaratha-nāmani ṣaṣṭhāṅke māyā-mayaḥ-ārya kim api dviṣatām apy āvarjakam udātta-jana-caritam । paśya- tatrāpi kārya-parateti mayi prakarṣaḥ । bāṣpāmbhasām aham apīha kṛto rasajñaḥ ।।
sa yakṣo rakṣo vā bhavatu bhagavān vā raghupatiḥ । samāḥ samyaṅ nītvā vana-bhuvi catasraś ca daśa ca ।। ity antena rāma-pravāsa-viṣayasya māyamaya-duḥkhasya satyasyaiva vyaktatvād vā māyāmayādeḥ kapaṭatva-jñāne' pi rāmacandreṇa satyatayāṅgīkārād vā mārgaḥ । rūpaṃ sandeha-kṛd vacaḥ ।।
yathā tatraiva ṣaṣṭhāṅke kaikeyī -paṇamāmi bhaavadiṃ saraūṃ jā pubbaṃ dīsamāṇā ṇayaṇa-pīūsa-gaṇḍūsa-kabalaṃ kareṃti asi । sā saṃpadaṃ hālāhala-kabaḍa-paḍirūbā paḍihāadi । kiṃ puṇa me aojjhā-daṃsaṇe bi akāraṇa-pajjāulaṃ hiaaṃ । ślāghā-ślokam aguñji-mañju-murajaṃ vidhvasta-gīta-dhvani । vidvadvad vāda-kathaṃ kathaṃ puram idaṃ mauna-vrate vartate ।। ity antena kaikeyī-daśarathayor ayodhyā-viṣaya-viṣāda-vitarka-vinyāsād rūpam ।
sotkarṣa-vacanaṃ yat tu tad udāharaṇaṃ matam ।। yasyābhāti kukūla-murmura-mṛduḥ kroḍe śikhī bāḍavaḥ । dattaś caṇḍa-davāgni-ambara-vidhir devasya vārāṃ-nidheḥ ।। ity upakramya, samudraḥ-tarhi bāla-nārāyaṇaṃ rāmam evopasarpāmaḥ । na hi rākāmṛgāṅkam antareṇa candra-maṇer ānanda-jala-niṣyandaḥ ( padyād pūrvam] ity antena samudra-kṣobhaka-rāmacandrotsāhotkarṣa-kathanād udāharaṇam ।
bhāva-jñānaṃ kramo yad vā cintyamānārtha-saṅgatiḥ ।। yathā tatraiva ṣaṣṭhāṅke mālyavān -na jāne kiṃ hi vṛttaṃ kaikeyī-daśarathayoḥ । māyamayaḥ-jayatv āryaḥ । śūrpaṇakhā-jedu jedu kaṇiṭṭhamādām aho ।
māyamayaḥ-yathādiṣṭam āryeṇa । mālyavān -tarhi vistarataḥ kathyatām । ity antena mālyavac cintā-samakālam eva śūrpaṇakhā-māyāmayayor upagamanād vā mālyavato vilambāsahābhiprāya-parijñānavatā māyāmayena niṣpannasya kāryasya saṅkṣepa-kathanād vā kramaḥ । saṅgrahaḥ sāmadānārtha-saṃyogaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
svar-mātaṅgaḥ sura-yuvatayo deva dhanvantariś ca । sampraty abdhiḥ śṛṇu jala-dhanas tvāṃ prapannaḥ praśādhi ।। rāmaḥ -bhagavan ratnākara ! namas te । ity upakramya, samudraḥ-yathā saptamo vaikuṇṭhāvatāraḥ ity antena samudra-rāmacandrayoḥ paraspara-priya-vacana-saṅgrahaṇāt saṅgrahaḥ ।
arthasyābhyūhanaṃ liṅgād anumānaṃ pracakṣate ।। yathā tatraiva pratīhārī -katham ayam anyādṛśa iva lakṣyate' mburāśiḥ । vandī -paśya । vilīyamāna-jala-mānuṣa-mithunam atyartha-kadarthyamāna-śaṅkhinī-yūtham ity upakramya, viśikhāḥ prajvalantaḥ patanti ।।
ity antena samudra-kṣobha-liṅgānumita-rāmotsāhārtha-kathanād anumānam । saṃrambhaṃ tu vacanaṃ saṅgirante hi toṭakam ।। yathā tatraiva hanumān-yathādiśati svāmī । - ājñāṃ mauli-niveśitāñjali-puṭāḥ sator iha vyūhane ।
ānetuṃ sakalāḥ prayāta kakubhaḥ kiṃ nāma vo duṣkaram ।। ity upakramyāṅka-parisamāpteḥ kapi-rākṣasādi-saṃrambha-kathanāt toṭakam । budhair adhibalaṃ proktaṃ kapaṭenātivañcanam ।। yathā tatraiva ṣaṣṭhāṅke māyāmayaḥ-athaikadā dayita-sneha-mayyā kaikeyyā samam asurānīka-vijayāya pūrita-suhṛn-manorathe daśarathe tgirviṣṭapa-tilaka-bhūtaṃ puruhūtaṃ prabhāvavati samupasthitavati tad-rūpa-dhāriṇau kuvalayābhirāmaṃ rāmaṃ saparicchadaṃ chalayituṃ ayodhyāṃ śūrpaṇakhā ahaṃ ca prāptavantau । ity upakramya,
mālyavān-kim asādhyaṃ vaidagdhyasya ity antena māyāmaya-śūrpaṇakhābhyāṃ kapaṭa-veṣa-dhāraṇena rāma-vāmadeva-vañcanād adhibalam । śatru-vairādi-sambhūtaṃ bhayam udvega ucyate ।। yathā tatraiva -svasti mahārāja-daśarathāya । daśarathaḥ-api kuśalaṃ vayasyasya jaṭāyoḥ ।
ratnaśikhaṇḍaḥ-priya-suhṛd-upayogena । daśarathaḥ-bhadra samupaviśya kathyatām । vyākulo' smi ity upakramya, kosalyā-hā debba tue kida-viḍaṃbaṃ samatthiaṃ baṇa-gadaṃ rāhava-kuṭuṃbaṃ । sumitrā-ṇa kebalaṃ baṇa-gadaṃ । ( padyād anantaraṃ] ity antena mātṛ-gata-bhīter upanyāsād udvegaḥ ।
śatru-vyāghrādi-sambhūtau śaṅkātrāsau ca sambhramaḥ ।। deva stambhaya cetanāṃ śravaṇayor abhyeti śuṣkāśaniḥ । rāmaḥ prāpya gataḥ kutaścana vanaṃ saumitri-sītā-sakhaḥ ।। ubhau mūrcchataḥ । vāmadevaḥ-deva samāśvasihi ।
daśarathaḥ-vatsa rāmabhadra manye mamaiva malayācala-nivāsinaḥ priya-vayasyasya jaṭāyor api śoka-śaṅkur ayaṃ sarvaṅkaṣo bhaviṣyati । ity antena kausalyā-daśarathādīnāṃ rakṣas-tarakṣu-haryakṣa-prabhṛti-sañcaraṇa-dāruṇāraṇyādiṣu rāma-pravāsa-viṣaya-śaṅkā-trāsānuvṛtti-kathanāt sambhramaḥ । garbha-bīja-samākṣepam ākṣepaṃ paricakṣate ।। yathā tatraiva pañcamāṅke śūrpaṇakhā -ajja ekka-mādua pekkha takkhaa-cūḍāmaṇī uppāḍido । baḍavāṇala-jālā-kalāpaaṃ ghuṃtalidaṃ । dasakaṇṭha-kaniṭṭha-bahiṇie accāhidaṃ । ity upakramya, śūrpaṇakhā-sāpi laṃkessarassa samucidatti abaharaṃtī tehiṃ kābālia-bbada-joggā kidaṃhi ।
ity antena aṅkānta-gata-bhāgena sakala-devatā-tejas tiraskaraṇa-rāvaṇātiśaya-varṇanā-garbhīkṛtasya rāmotsāhasya śūrpaṇakhā-karṇa-nāsā-nikṛntana-rūpeṇa samudbhedād ākṣepaḥ । yatra pralobhana-krodha-vyasanādyair vimṛśyate । bījārtho garbha-nirbhinnaḥ sa vimarśa itīryate ।। prakarī-niyatāptyānuguṇyād atrāṅga-kalpanam ।
apavādo' tha sampheṭo vidrava-drava-śaktayaḥ ।। dyuti-prasaṅgau chalana-vyavasāyau nirodhanam । prarocanā vicalanam ādānaṃ syus trayodaśa ।। tatrāpavādo doṣāṇāṃ prakhyāpanam itīryate ।।
yathā tatraiva aṣṭamāṅke vīra-vilāsa-nāmani ekaḥ-sakhe durmukha kim api mahān sattva-bhraṃśo daśakaṇṭhasya yat kumāra-siṃhanāda-vadham apy ākarṇya na śokaṃ kṛto nāpy amarṣaḥ । ity upakramya, trijaṭā-kahaṃ deveṇa diṇṇo lajjā-deīe jalāṃjalī । ity antena rāvaṇa-gata-durbuddhi-doṣa-prakhyāpanād apavādaḥ । doṣa-saṅgrathitaṃ vākyaṃ sampheṭaṃ sampracakṣate ।। prāpta-syandana-bāṇa-cāpa-kavacaḥ svaṃ manyase durjayam ।
vandhyās tāvad ayaṃ sa śakra-vijayiṃs tvāṃ lakṣmaṇo jeṣyati ।। bāli-druhaṃ ca racitāmbudhi-bandhanaṃ ca । rāmaṃ nihatya caraṇau tava vanditāhe ।। ity antena, lakṣmaṇendrajit-kumbhakarṇānāṃ roṣa-vākya-grahaṇāt sampheṭaḥ ।
virodha-vadha-dāhādir vidravaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। sumukhaḥ-ayam aparaḥ kṣate kṣārāvasekaḥ । bibhrāṇo bhairavatvaṃ bahula-kalakalārāva-raudrāṭṭa-hāsaḥ । tad-vaktrād utpatadbhiḥ samajani śikhibhir bhasmasād indrajic ca ।।
rāvaṇaḥ ity antena kapisenāvikṣobha-sugrīva-nirodha-kumbhakarṇa-vadhendrajid-bhasmīkaraṇa-rāvaṇa-mūrcchādi-saṅkathanād vidravaḥ । guru-vyatikramaṃ prāha dravaṃ tu bharato muniḥ ।। dhig vaktrāṇi nikṛtta-kaṇṭha-valaya-prītendu-maulīni ca । pratyāśā cira-vismṛtāyudha-vidhau yat kumbhakarṇe sthitā ।।
ity atra svāminor daśakaṇṭha-kumbhakarṇayor anujīvinā rākṣasena nindā-karaṇād dravaḥ । utpannasya virodhasya śamanaṃ śaktir iṣyate ।। māsāsvādana-lubdha-gṛdhra-vihaga-śreṇībhir āsevitaḥ । heṣitvā smṛta-mandurāsthiti-hṛtair laṅkāṃ ratho nīyata ।।
ity antena niravaśeṣa-pratināyaka-bhūta-rāvaṇa-kaṇṭhotsādana-kathanena virodha-śamanāt śaktiḥ । dyutir nāma samuddiṣṭā tarjanodvejane budhaiḥ ।। yathā tatraiva aṣṭamāṅke, rāvaṇaḥ -kim ayam atisatvaraḥ sura-samājaḥ ? śaṅke katipaya-yātudhāna-vadhān tāpasaṃ prati prīyate । tan me doṣṇāṃ vijita-jagatāṃ vikramaṃ vistṛtāḥ stha ।
tūrṇaṃ jetā sa ca diviṣadāṃ bodhyate meghanādaḥ ।। ity upakramya, nepathye-biraeha keli-ākaḍḍhaṇa-pāḍaṇijjaṃ goura-duvāraṃ, boḍheha bibiha-ppaharaṇa-saṇṇāha-daha-sahassāi । ity antena devatā-tarjana-laṅkā-pura-janodvejana-kathanād dyutiḥ । prastutārthasya kathanaṃ prasaṅgaḥ parikīrtitaḥ । prasaṅgaṃ kathayanty anye gurūṇāṃ parikīrtanam ।।
daśarathaḥ-bhagavan gīrvāṇa-nātha sa-prasādam ito nidhīyantāṃ dṛṣṭayaḥ । ity antena yama-purandarādi-pūjya-saṅkīrtanād vā prastuta-rākṣasa-vadha-rūpasyārthasya prapañcanād vā prasaṅgaḥ । avamānādi-karaṇaṃ kāryārthe chalanaṃ viduḥ ।। nātya-śāstre atra chādana iti saṃjñā prāpyate । yathā tatraiva cāraṇaḥ -kim āha rāmabhadraḥ । re re rākṣasa-putra-
premārdreṇa sa-vibhrameṇa ca purā yenekṣitā jānakī । śeṣa-ccheda-vidhis tu samprati paraṃ svar-vandin-mokṣāya me ।। rāmaḥ-tad ittham abhidhānam apavitraṃ te vaktram । ito nirviśatu vadha-śuddhim ity antena rāma-rāvaṇābhyāṃ parasparāvamānana-karaṇāt chalanam । vyavasāyaḥ sva-sāmarthya-prakhyāpanam itīryate ।।
ko' yaṃ te mati-vibhramaḥ smara nayaṃ nādyāpi kiṃcid gatam । patrī naiṣa sahiṣyate mama dhanur jyā-bandha-bandhūkṛtaḥ ।। ity upakramya-kim āha rāvaṇaḥ ? re re mānuṣī-putra ! ayam asau akṣatriyo rāvaṇaḥ । tad atra dṛśyatām । kataro vinetā iti । kim āha rāmabhadraḥ ? haṃho amānuṣī-putra ! kṣatriyo rāmaḥ । ayam asau akṣatriyo rāvaṇaḥ । tad atra dṛśyatāṃ kataro vineyaḥ, kataro vinetā ity antena rāma-rāvaṇābhyāṃ sva-sāmarthya-prakhyāpanād vyavasāyaḥ । virodhanaṃ nirodhoktiḥ saṃrabdhānāṃ parasparam ।।
yathā tatraiva cāraṇaḥ-katham amarṣitābhyāṃ rāma-rāvaṇābhyāṃ pratyupakrāntam iṣu-varṣādvaitam ity upakramya, cāraṇaḥ-nanv ayam oṃkāro rāvaṇa-śiro-maṇḍala-cchedana-vidyāyāḥ ity antena saṃrabdhayo rāma-rāvaṇayoḥ divyāstra-prayoga-rūpa-paraspara-saṃrodha-karaṇād virodhanam । siddhavad bhāvino' rthasya sūcanā syāt prarocanā ।। yathā tatraiva aṣṭamāṅke, karaṅkaḥ -sakhe kañkāla devaḥ kumbhakarṇaṃ prabodhayati । kiṃ ca prayatnena bodhito' py asau rāmeṇa punaḥ śāyitavya eva । kaṅkālaḥ-maṇṇe bibhīsaṇaṃ bajjia sabbassa bi esā gaī ।
karaṅkaḥ-tathaiva । ity atra bhaviṣyataḥ kumbhakarṇādi-rākṣasa-nāśasya kaṅkāla-karaṅkābhyāṃ siddhavat niścitya sūcanāt prarocanā । ātma-ślāghā vicalanam ।। cakrair alaṃ bhavatu paṭṭiśam udgarādyaiḥ । yāsyāmy ahaṃ suhitatāṃ ca ripu-kṣayaṃ ca ।।
sādhu vatsa, sādhu । satyaṃ mad-anujo' si, ity upakramya- hanūmato gātra-gatena bhasmasāt । niṣevituṃ mām upayāti pāvakaḥ ।। ity antena rāvaṇa-kumbhakarṇābhyām ātma-ślāghā kṛteti vicalanam ।
ādānaṃ kārya-saṅgrahaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva navamāṅke purandaraḥ-sakhe daśaratha katham ayam ananya-sadṛśākāro rāmabhadra-puruṣakāraḥ । ataś ca- pāṇḍityaṃ viditaṃ guhasya kim u tāv ajñāta-yuddhotsavau । vīrāṇāṃ caritādbhutasya parame rāmaḥ sthitaḥ sīmani ।।
svayam ayam avatīrṇo lakṣmaṇa-nyasta-hastaḥ । dinakara-kula-lakṣmī-vallabho rāmabhadraḥ ।। ity antena nikhila-bhuvana-bādhā-śamana-rūpa-rāvaṇa-vadha-sampādita-dharmādi-lakṣaṇa-kārya-viśeṣa-saṅgrahaṇād ādānam । mukha-sandhyādayo yatra vikīrṇā bīja-saṃyutāḥ ।
mahat-prayojanaṃ yānti tan-nirvahaṇam ucyate ।। sandhi-virodhau grathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ paribhāṣaṇe prasādaś ca । ānanda-samaya-kṛtayo bhāṣopagūhane tadvat ।। atha pūrva-bhāva-sayujāv upasaṃhāra-praśastī ca ।
iti nirvahaṇasyāṅgāny āhur amīṣāṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye ।। bījopagamanaṃ sandhiḥ ।। yathā tatraiva rāghavānanda-nāmani daśamāṅke laṅkā-hā duddhara-taba-visesa-paritosidārabindāsaṇa tihubaṇekkamalla dasa-kaṇṭha hā helā-bandīkida-mahinda mehanāda hā samara-saṃraṃbha-suppasaṇṇa kuṃbha-kaṇṇa kahiṃsi dehi me paḍibaaṇaṃ । ity upakramya, alakā-sakhi dharma-jetari vibhīṣaṇe' pi netari tatrabhavatī sa-śoka-śaṅkur iva ।
laṅkā-jaṃ tiṇetta-mittassa ṇaarī bhaṇadī । ity antena duṣṭa-rākṣasa-śikṣā-rūpa-rāmotsāha-bījopagamanāt sandhiḥ । kāryānveṣaṇaṃ virodhaḥ syāt ।। sāvitri dhātri sakalāḥ kula-devatāś ca । tat saṃnidhatta sahasā saha loka-pālaiḥ ।।
ity upakramya, laṅkā-aho devadāṇaṃ bi sīdāpakkha-bādo । adhavā sabbo guṇesu rajjadi । ṇa sarīresu । ity antena sītā-śuddhi-rūpa-kāryānveṣaṇād virodhaḥ । grathanaṃ tad-upekṣepaḥ ।। nītaṃ rakṣaḥ-kulam adhigatāḥ śuddhimantaś ca dārāḥ । diṣṭyāyodhyāṃ vrajati dayitā-prītaye puṣpakeṇa ।।
laṅkāṅganācakita-netra-nirīkṣita-śrīḥ । rājyābhiṣeka-samayocita-kārya-siddheḥ ।। ity antena rāmābhiṣeka-rūpa-parama-kāropekṣād grathanam । syād anubhūtasya nirṇayaḥ kathanam ।।
dhārāmbhasāṃ smarasi majjana-keli-kāle । atrābja-valli-dalam āvaraṇāya dattam ।। smarasi sutanu kiṃcin nau parādhīna-suptam । tad anu madana-mudrāṃ tac ca gāḍhopagūḍham ।।
ity atra rāmeṇa svānubhūtārtha-kathanān nirṇayaḥ । paribhāṣā tv anyonyaṃ jalpanam athavā parivādaḥ ।। yathā tatraiva sītā-ajja-utta dasakaṇṭha-ṇisūaṇa vārāṇasī-saṃkittaṇeṇa sumarābidamhi akkhiāṇaddaṃ jaṇaṇī-bhūdaṃ mihilāṃ mahā-ṇāarīṃ । ity upakramya, vibhīṣaṇaḥ-iha hi khalu kṣatriyāntakarasya bhaṅgo bhārgava-muner dattaḥ ।
apāṃ phenena tṛpto' sau snātaś candrikayā ca saḥ । yad aprasūta-kauśalyaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣapitavān muniḥ ।। ity antena sītā-rāma-vibhīṣaṇa-sugrīvāṇām anyonya-saṃjalpanena vā sugrīveṇa bhārgava-parīvāda-sūcanād vā paribhāṣaṇam । śuśrūṣādi-prāptaṃ prasādam āhuḥ prasannatvam ।।
chāyāṃ mā kuru ko' py ayaṃ dina-maṇāv ekāgra-dṛṣṭiḥ sthitaḥ । kiñcit tiṣṭha tapasvinas tava puro yāvat paryānty adhvanaḥ ।। niṣkaṇṭakāni vihitāni jaganti yena । bhū-kāśyapopama-suta-dvitayā vadhūḥ syāt ।।
rāmaḥ-param anugṛhītaṃ raghu-kulam ity antena agastya-dattāśīrvāda-rūpa-prasāda-kathanāt prasādaḥ । abhilaṣitārtha-samāgamam ānandaṃ prāhur ācāryāḥ ।। yathā tatraiva, rāmaḥ-haṃho vimāna-rāja vimucya vasudhā-savidha-vartinī gatiṃ kiñcid uccair bhava । kutūhalinī jānakī divya-loka-darśana-vyatikarasya । vyomnaḥ śikhāṃ puṣpakam ānatāṅgi ।
tathā tathā saṅkuciteva pṛthvī ।। sura-cāraṇa-kiṃnara-vidyādhara-kula-saṅkulaṃ gagana-garbham īkṣasva । vidyādharaḥ ataḥ parama-gamyā asmādṛśāṃ bhuvaḥ । sa ca brahma-loka iti śrūyate । ity antena sītādīnām abhilaṣita-divya-loka-darśana-rūpārtha-siddher ānandaḥ । samayo duḥkha-saṅkṣayaḥ ।।
yathā tatraiva, bharataḥ ārya ! rāvaṇa-vidrāvaṇa bharato' ham abhivādaye । ity upakramya ity antena bandhūnām anyonyāvalokana-pariṣvaṅgādibhir duḥkhāpagama-kathanāt samayaḥ । kṛtir api labdhārtha-susthirīkaraṇam ।। yathā tatraiva, hanumān-deva mattaḥ śruta-vṛttānto vasiṣṭhaḥ samaṃ bharata-śaturghnābhyām anyābhiś ca prakṛtibhir bhavad-abhiṣeka-sajjas tiṣṭhati । ity upakramya, vasiṣṭhaḥ kā dīyatāṃ tva raghūdvaha samyag āśīr ity ādi paṭhati । rāmaḥ ārṣaṃ hi vacanaṃ vibhinna-vaktṛkam api na visaṃvadati yad agastya-vācā vasiṣṭho' pi brūte ity antena agastya-labdhāśīrvādasya vasiṣṭha-vacana-saṃvādena sthirīkaraṇāt kṛtiḥ ।
mānādyāptiś ca bhāṣaṇam ।। saumitriḥ sadṛśo' stu kasya samare yenedrajin nirjitaḥ । śatrughnaḥ kathito' grajasya ca guṇair vandyaṃ kuṭumbaṃ raghoḥ ।। ity atra vasiṣṭhena raghu-kuṭumbasya rāmacandrādi-sat-puruṣotpatti-sthānatayā tallakṣaṇa-bahu-māna-prāpti-kathanād bhāṣaṇam ।
upagūhanam adbhuta-prāptiḥ ।। yatha tatraiva, alakā-aho nu khalu bhoḥ pati-vratā-mayaṃ jyotiḥ anabhibhavanīyaṃ jyotir-antaraiḥ । yataḥ, praviśantyā citācakraṃ jānakyā pariśuddhaye । na bhedaḥ ko' pi nirṇītaḥ payasaḥ pāvakasya ca ।।
yogīndraś ca narendraś ca yasyāḥ sa janakaḥ pitā । viśuddhā rāma-gṛhiṇī babhau daśaratha-snuṣā ।। ity antena sītāyāḥ niḥśaṅka-jvalana-praveśa-nirapāya-nirgamana-rūpāścarya-kathanād upagūhanam । dṛṣṭa-krama-kāryasya syād dṛṣṭiḥ pūrva-bhāvas tu ।।
yathā tatraiva -vatsa rāmabhadra praśasto muhūrto vartate । tad adhyāssva pitryaṃ siṃhāsanam ity upakramya, vasiṣṭhaḥ-rāmabhadra dhanyo' si । yasya te bhagavān kubero' rthī ity antena vasiṣṭhena rāmabhadrasyābhiṣekāṅgīkaraṇa-kubera-vimāna-pratyarpaṇa-rūpayor arthayor darśanāt pūrva-bhāvaḥ । dharmārthādy-upagamanād upasaṃhāraḥ kṛtārthatā-kathanam ।। yathā tatraiva, vasiṣṭhaḥ-vatsa rāmabhadra kiṃ te bhūyaḥ priyam upakaromi । rāmaḥ-kim ataḥ priyam asti ।
setuś ca grathitaḥ prasanna-madhuro dṛṣṭaś ca vārāṃ nidhiḥ । prāptaṃ yānam idaṃ ca yācitavate dattaṃ kuberāya ca ।। ity atra rugṇaṃ cājagavaṃ ity anena bhūta-pati-dhanur dalanena sītādhigama-rūpakām aprāpteḥ paulasytaś caramaḥ sthitaḥ ity anena śaraṇāgata-rakṣaṇena dharma-prāpteḥ prāptaṃ yānam idaṃ cety atra vimāna-ratna-lābhenārtha-prāpteś ca na cāpi kupito bhargaḥ sura-grāmiṇīr ity ādibhiḥ pādānta-vākyaiḥ rāmacandreṇa sva-kṛtārthatā-kathanād upasaṃhāraḥ । kiṃ ca, rugṇaṃ cājagavaṃ setuś ca grathita ity ādibhyāṃ yuddhotsāha-siddheḥ paulastyaś caramaḥ sthitaḥ ity atra vibhīṣaṇasya pālanena dayā-vīra-siddheḥ yācitavate dattaṃ kuberāya cety anena dānavīra-siddheś ca rāmabhadreṇa svakṛtārthatā-kathanād vā upasaṃhāraḥ ।
bharataiś carācarāṇām āśīr āśaṃsanaṃ praśastiḥ syāt ।। grathnantu grantha-bandhaṃ vacanam anupatat-sūkti-mudrāḥ kavīndrāḥ । tat tattvaṃ sāttvikaiś ca prathama-piśunitaṃ bhāvayanto' rcayantu ।। ity atra kavīndrāṇāṃ nirdoṣa-sūkti-grathanāśaṃsanena bhāvakānāṃ ca tad-grantha-bhāvanāśaṃsanena ca sakala-vyavahāra-pravartaka-vāṅmaya-rūpa-jagan-maṅgala-kathanāt praśastir iti sarvaṃ praśastam ।
rasa-bhāvānurodhena prayojanam apekṣya ca । sāphalyaṃ kāryam aṅgānām ity ācāryāḥ pracakṣate ।। keṣāṃcid eṣām aṅgānāṃ vikalpaṃ kecid ūcire । mukhādi-sandhiṣv aṅgānāṃ kramo' yaṃ na vivakṣitaḥ ।।
kramasyānādṛtatvena bharatādibhir ādimaiḥ । lakṣyeṣu vyutkrameṇāpi kathanena vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। catuḥ-ṣaṣṭhi-kalā-marma-vedinā siṃha-bhūbhujā । lakṣitā ca catuḥṣaṣṭhir bāla-rāmāyaṇe sphuṭam ।।
mukhādi-sandhiṣv aṅgānām aśaithilya-pratītaye । sandhy-antarāṇi yojyāni tatra tatraikaviṃśatiḥ ।। ācāryāntara-saṃmatyā camatkārodayād api । vakṣye lakṣaṇam eteṣām udāhṛtim api sphuṭam ।।
sāma-dāne bheda-daṇḍau pratyutpanna-matir vadhaḥ । gotra-skhalitam ojaś ca dhīḥ krodhaḥ sāhasaṃ bhayam ।। māyā ca saṃvṛtir bhrāntir dūtyaṃ hetv-avadhāraṇam । svapna-lekhau madaś citram ity etāny ekaviṃśatiḥ ।।
tatra sāma priyaṃ vākyaṃ svānuvṛtti-prakāśanam ।। yathā mālavikāgnimitre, rājā-aye na bhetavyam । mālavikā -jo ṇa bhāadi so mae bhaṭṭiṇī-daṃsaṇe diṭṭha-sāmattho bhaṭṭā । dākṣiṇyaṃ nāma bimboṣṭhi nāyakānāṃ kula-vratam ।
tan me dīrghākṣi ye prāṇās te tvad-āśā-nibandhanāḥ ।। ity atra rājño vacanaṃ nāma । dānam ātma-pratinidhir bhūṣaṇādi-samarpaṇam ।। yathā mālatī-mādhave, mālatī-pia-sahi sabbadā sumaridabbahmi । esā bi māhaba-sahatthaṇimmāṇamaṇoharā baula-mālā māladī-ṇibbisesaṃ pia-sahīe daṭṭabbā । sabbadā hiaeṇa a dhāraṇijjā iti ।
atra mālatyā martukāmāyāḥ pratinidhitayā lavaṅgikāyāṃ bakulamālā-samarpaṇaṃ dānam । bhedas tu kapaṭālāpaiḥ suhṛdāṃ bheda-kalpanam ।। dattvātmajāṃ bhavatu nirvṛtimānamātyaḥ । dhūma-graheṇa vimalā śaśinaḥ kaleva ।।
mālatī -hā tāda tumaṃ bi ṇāma mama ebbaṃ ti sabbahā jidaṃ bhoatihṇāe । ity atra kāmandakyā mālatī-taj-janakayor bheda-kalpanaṃ bhedaḥ । daṇḍas tv avinayādīnāṃ dṛṣṭyā śrutyātha tarjanam ।। lalita-śirīṣa-puṣpa-hananair api tāmyati yat । patatu śirasy akāṇḍayam adaṇḍa ivaiṣa bhujaḥ ।।
atrāghora-ghaṇṭasyāvinaya-darśanena mādhava-kṛta-tarjanaṃ daṇḍaḥ । kaḥ paurave vasumatīṃ śāsati śāsitari durvinītānām । ayam ācaraty avinayaṃ mugdhāsu taspasvi-kanyāsu ।। atrāvinaya-śrutyā duṣyantena kṛtaṃ tarjanaṃ daṇḍaḥ ।
tāt-kālikī ca pratibhā pratyutpanna-matir smṛtā ।। yathā mālavikāgnimitre, rājā-na khalu mudrām adhikṛtya bravīmi । etayor baddhayoḥ kiṃ-nimitto mokṣaḥ । kiṃ devyāḥ parijanam atikramya bhavān sandiṣṭaḥ ity evam anayā praṣṭavyam । vidūṣakaḥ-ṇaṃ pucchido hmi । puṇo mandassa bi me tasmiṃ pañcuppaṇṇā madī āsi । rājā-kathyatām ।
vidūṣakaḥ-bhaṇidaṃ mae, debbaciṃtaehiṃ viṇṇāvido rāā । sobasaggaṃ bo ṇakkhattaṃ tā avassaṃ sabba-bandha-mokkho karīadutti । vidūṣakaḥ-taṃ suṇia devīe irāvadī-cittaṃ rakkhaṃtīe rāā kila moedi tti ahaṃ saṃdiṭṭho tti tado jujjadi tti tāe ibbaṃ saṃpādido attho । rājā -sakhe ! priyo' haṃ khalu tava । ity atra vidūṣakasya samucitottara-pratibhā pratyutpanna-matiḥ ।
vadhas tu jīvita-droha-kriyā syād ātatāyinaḥ ।। yathā veṇī-saṃhāre, kṛṣṇaḥ-ahaṃ punaś cārvākeṇa rakṣasā vyākulīkṛtaṃ bhavantam upalabhyārjunena saha tvaritataram āyātaḥ । bhīmaḥ -bhagavan kvāsau dhārtarāṣṭra-sakho rākṣasaś cārvāko yenāryasya mahāṃś citta-vibhramaḥ kṛtaḥ । kṛṣṇaḥ-nigṛhītaḥ sa durātmā nakulena ।
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ-priyaṃ naḥ, priyaṃ naḥ । ity atra cārvāka-nigraho vadhaḥ । tad gotra-skhalitaṃ yat tu nāma-vyatyaya-bhāṣaṇam ।। yathā vikramorvaśīye prathamaḥ-aye sadoṣāvakāśa iva te vākya-śeṣaḥ । dvitīyaḥ-ām । tarhi ubbasīe baaṇaṃ pamāda-kkhalidaṃ āsi ।
dvitīyaḥ-lacchī-bhūmiāe baṭṭamāṇā ubbasī vāruṇī-bhūmiāe baṭṭamāṇāe meṇaāe pucchidā । sahi samāadā ede tellokka-purisā sakesavā loa-bālā । kadamassiṃ de bhāvāhiṇibesotti dvitīyaḥ-tado tāe purisottame tti bhaṇidabbe purūravasi tti ṇiggadā bāṇī । ity atra nāma-vyatikramaḥ sphuṭa eva । ojas tu vāg-upanyāso nija-śakti-prakāśakaḥ ।। āyodhanaṃ nanu kim āttha sakhe tatheti ।
kṣattrasya śastra-śikhinaḥ śamam adya yāntu ।। ity atra ojaḥ spaṣṭam eva । iṣṭārtha-siddhi-paryantā cintā dhīr iti kathyate ।। vidūṣakaḥ -atthi ettha ubāo ।
vidūṣakaḥ -ko bi adiṭṭho suṇissad । kaṇṇe de kahemi evaṃ bia । ity āvedayati । rājā saharṣaṃ-suṣṭhu prayujyatāṃ siddhaye । ity atra vidūṣakeṇa dhāriṇī-hasta-maṇi-mudrikākarṣāṇa-hetu-bhūtasya bhujaga-viṣa-vega-kapaṭasya cintanaṃ dhīḥ । krodhas tu cetaso dīptir aparādhādi-darśanāt ।। yathā ratnāvalyāṃ tṛtīyāṅke, vāsavadattā-hañje kaṃcaṇamāle edeṇa ebba ladāpāseṇa bandhia gehaṇa eṇaṃ bahmaṇaṃ । eṇaṃ duṭṭha-kaṇṇaāṃ a aggado karehi । ity atra vāsavadattāyāḥ roṣaḥ krodhaḥ ।
sva-jīvita-nirākāṅkṣo vyāpāraḥ sāhasaṃ bhavet ।। aśastra-pātam avyāja-puruṣāṅgopakalpitam । vikrīyate mahā-māṃsaṃ gṛhyatāṃ gṛhyatām idam ।। sva-śastra-pūta-nirvyāja-puruṣāṅgopakalpitam iti mudrita-mālatī-mādhava-pāṭhaḥ ।
atra mādhavasya mahā-māṃsa-vikraya-vyāpāraḥ sāhasam । bhayaṃ tv ākasmika-trāsaḥ ।। yathā abhirāma-rāghave dvitīyāṅke, baṭuḥ-ayya parittāahi parittāahi । accahide paḍido hmi । ity ādau baṭu-trāso bhayam । māyā kaitava-kalpanā ।।
eṣa brahmā saroje rajanikara-kalā-śekharaḥ śaṅkaro' yaṃ dorbhir daityāntako' sau sa-dhanur-asi-gadā-cakra-cihnaiś caturbhiḥ । eṣo' py airāvatasthas tridaśapatir amī devi devās tathānye nṛtyanti vyomni caitāś cala-caraṇa-raṇan-nūpurā divya-nāryaḥ ।। ity atra aindrajālika-kalpitaṃ kaitavaṃ māyā । saṃvṛttiḥ svayam uktasya svayam pracchādanaṃ bhavet ।।
yathā śākuntale, rājā -aticapalo' yaṃ baṭuḥ । kadācid imāṃ kathām antaḥ-purebhyaḥ kathayet । bhavatu । enam eva vakṣye- mṛgaśāvaiḥ samam edhito janaḥ । paramārthena na gṛhyatāṃ vacaḥ ।। atra duṣyantena svayam uktasya śakuntalā-prasaṅgasya svayaṃ pracchādanaṃ saṃvṛttiḥ ।
bhrāntir viparyaya-jñānaṃ prasaṅgasya hy aniścayāt ।। yathā veṇī-saṃhāre dvitīyāṅke, bhānumatī-tado ahaṃ tassa adisaidadibba-rūbiṇo ṇaulassa daṃsaṇeṇa ucchuā jādā hida-hiaā a । tado ujjhia taṃ āsanaṭṭhāṇaṃ ladā-maṇḍapaṃ pabisiduṃ āraddhā । rājā -kiṃ nāmātiśayita-divya-rūpiṇo nakulasya darcānenotsukā jātā । tat katham anayā pāpayā mādrī-sutānuraktayā vayam evaṃ vipralabdhāḥ । mūrkha duryodhana kulaṭā-vipralabhyamānam ātmānaṃ bahu manyamāno' dhunā kiṃ vakṣyasi । aho etad artham evāsyāḥ prātar eva vivikta-sthānābhilāṣaḥ sakhī-jana-saṅkathāsu ca pakṣa-pātaḥ । duryodhanas tu mohād avijñāta-bandhakī-hṛdaya-sāraḥ kvāpi paribhrāntaḥ । ity atra devī-svapnasya aniścayād duryodhanasya viparīta-jñānaṃ bhrāntiḥ । māyā kaitava-kalpanā ।।
eṣa brahmā saroje rajanikara-kalā-śekharaḥ śaṅkaro' yaṃ dorbhir daityāntako' sau sa-dhanur-asi-gadā-cakra-cihnaiś caturbhiḥ । eṣo' py airāvatasthas tridaśapatir amī devi devās tathānye nṛtyanti vyomni caitāś cala-caraṇa-raṇan-nūpurā divya-nāryaḥ ।। ity atra aindrajālika-kalpitaṃ kaitavaṃ māyā । saṃvṛttiḥ svayam uktasya svayam pracchādanaṃ bhavet ।।
yathā śākuntale, rājā -aticapalo' yaṃ baṭuḥ । kadācid imāṃ kathām antaḥ-purebhyaḥ kathayet । bhavatu । enam eva vakṣye- mṛgaśāvaiḥ samam edhito janaḥ । paramārthena na gṛhyatāṃ vacaḥ ।। atra duṣyantena svayam uktasya śakuntalā-prasaṅgasya svayaṃ pracchādanaṃ saṃvṛttiḥ ।
bhrāntir viparyaya-jñānaṃ prasaṅgasya hy aniścayāt ।। yathā veṇī-saṃhāre dvitīyāṅke, bhānumatī-tado ahaṃ tassa adisaidadibba-rūbiṇo ṇaulassa daṃsaṇeṇa ucchuā jādā hida-hiaā a । tado ujjhia taṃ āsanaṭṭhāṇaṃ ladā-maṇḍapaṃ pabisiduṃ āraddhā । rājā -kiṃ nāmātiśayita-divya-rūpiṇo nakulasya darcānenotsukā jātā । tat katham anayā pāpayā mādrī-sutānuraktayā vayam evaṃ vipralabdhāḥ । mūrkha duryodhana kulaṭā-vipralabhyamānam ātmānaṃ bahu manyamāno' dhunā kiṃ vakṣyasi । aho etad artham evāsyāḥ prātar eva vivikta-sthānābhilāṣaḥ sakhī-jana-saṅkathāsu ca pakṣa-pātaḥ । duryodhanas tu mohād avijñāta-bandhakī-hṛdaya-sāraḥ kvāpi paribhrāntaḥ । ity atra devī-svapnasya aniścayād duryodhanasya viparīta-jñānaṃ bhrāntiḥ । dūtyaṃ tu sahakāritvaṃ durghaṭe kārya-vastuni ।।
yathā mālavikāgnimitre vidūṣakaḥ-alaṃ bhavado dhīradaṃ ujjhia paridebideṇa । diṭṭhā kkhu mae tattahodīe mālabiāe piasahī baulābaliā । suṇābidāa maha jaṃ bhavadā saṃdiṭṭhaṃ । rājā-tataḥ kim uktavatī । vidūṣakaḥ-vijñāpaya bhaṭṭārakamà tathāpi ghaṭayiṣyāmi iti । atra ca bakulāvalikayā mālavikāgnimitrayor ghaṭane sahakāritvam aṅgīkṛtam iti dūtyam । niścayo hetunārthasya mataṃ hetv-avadhāraṇam ।। sandṛśyate kim uta yāḥ pratibodhavatyaḥ ।
anyair dvijaiḥ para-bhṛtāḥ khalu poṣayanti ।। atra para-bhṛtānidarśanopabṛṃhitena strītva-hetunā mṛṣā-bhāṣaṇa-lakṣaṇasyārthasya niścayo hetv-avadhāraṇam । svapno nidrāntare mantra-bheda-kṛd vacanaṃ matam ।। nipuṇikā-sudaṃ bhaṭṭiṇīe । kassa eso attaṇioa-saṃpādaṇ vissasaṇijjo hadāso । sabba-kālaṃ ido ebba sotthibāaṇa-modaehiṃ kucchiṃ pūria saṃpadaṃ mālabiaṃ ussibiṇābedi ।
vidūṣakaḥ-irāvadiṃ adikkamaṃtī hohi । ity atra vidūṣakasyotsvapnāyitaṃ svapnaḥ । vivakṣitārtha-kalitā patrikā lekha īritaḥ ।। yathā vikramorvaśīye rājā -sakhe ! bhūrja-patra-gato' yam akṣara-vinyāsaḥ । ity ārabhya,
rājā-vayasya aṅguli-svedena dūṣyerann akṣarāṇi । dhāryatām ayaṃ priyāyāḥ sva-hasta-lekhaḥ । ity atra urvaśī-prahita-patrikārtho lekhaḥ । madas tu madyajaḥ ।। yathā mālavikāgnimitre ity atrerāvatī-madaḥ । citraṃ cākārsya vilekhanam ।।
yathā śākuntale rājā akāraṇa-parityāgānuśaya-tapta-hṛdayas tāvad anukampyatām ayaṃ janaḥ punar darśanena । ity ārabhya, rājā- darśana-mukham anubhavataḥ sākṣād iva tan-mayena hṛdayena । smṛti-kāriṇā tvayā me punar api citrīkṛtā kāntā ।। ity antena citraṃ sphuṭam iti kalyāṇam ।
bhāga-kalpanayāṅgānāṃ mukha-pramukha-sandhiṣu । pratyekaṃ niyatatvena yojyā tatraiva kalpanā ।। sandhy-antarāṇāṃ vijñeyaḥ prayogas tv avibhāgataḥ । tathaiva darśanād eṣām anaiyatyena sandhiṣu ।।
tad eṣām avicāreṇa kathito daśarūpake । sandhy-antarāṇām aṅgeṣu nāntarbhāvo mato mama ।। sāmādy-upāya-dakṣeṇa sandhyādi-guṇa-śobhitā । nirvyūḍhaṃ siṃha-bhūpena sandhy-antara-nirūpaṇam ।।
evam aṅgair upāṅgaiś ca suśliṣṭaṃ rūpaka-śriyaḥ । śarīraṃ vas tv alaṅkuryāt ṣaṭ-triṃśad bhūṣaṇaiḥ sphuṭam ।। bhūṣaṇākṣara-saṅghātau hetuḥ prāptir udāhṛtiḥ । śobhā saṃśaya-dṛṣṭāntāv abhiprāyo nidarśanam ।।
siddhi-prasiddhī dākṣiṇyam arthāpattir viśeṣaṇam । padoccayas tulya-tarko vicāras tad-viparyayaḥ ।। guṇātipāto' tiśayo niruktaṃ guṇa-kīrtanam । garhaṇānunayo bhraṃśo leśa-kṣobhau manorathaḥ ।।
anukti-siddhiḥ sārūpyaṃ mālā madhura-bhāṣaṇam । pṛcchopadiṣṭa-dṛṣṭāni ṣaṭ-triṃśad-bhūṣaṇāni hi ।। guṇālaṅkāra-bahulaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ matam ।। carcāṃ pārayatīva dardura-kulaṃ kolāhalair unmadam ।
durlakṣo' pi vibhāvyate kamalinī-hāsena bhāsāṃ patiḥ ।। atra śleṣa-prasāda-samādhi-samatādīnāṃ guṇānāṃ upamā-rūpakotprekṣa-hetūnām alaṅkārāṇāṃ ca sambhavād idaṃ bhūṣaṇam । vākyam akṣara-saṅghāto bhinnārthaṃ śliṣṭa-varṇakam ।। yathā śākuntale rājā iyaṃ khalu kathā mām eva lakṣyīkaroti । yadi tāvad asya śiśor mātaraṃ nāmataḥ pṛcchāmi । athavā anyāyyaḥ para-dāra-vyavahāraḥ । ity upakramya,
bālaḥ -kahiṃ vā me ajjū । ubhe-ṇāma-sārisseṇa baṃcido māubacchalo । dvitīyā-baccha, imassa mittiā-morassa raṃmattaṇaṃ dekkha tti bhaṇido' si । rājā -kiṃ vā śakuntalety asya mātur ākhyā । atra śakunta-lāvaṇyam ity atra śakuntalā-nāmākṣarāṇāṃ pratibhānād ayam akṣara-saṅghātaḥ ।
sa hetur iti nirdiṣṭo yat sādhyārtha-prasādhakaḥ ।। spaṣṭākṣaram idaṃ yatnān madhuraṃ strī-svabhāvataḥ । alpāṅgatvād anirhrādi manye vadati śārikā ।। atra śārikālāpa-sādhanāya yatna-spaṣṭākṣaratvādi-hetūnāṃ kathanād ayaṃ hetuḥ ।
eka-deśa-parijñānāt prāptiḥ śeṣābhiyojanam ।। haṃsa prayaccha me kāntāṃ gatir asyās tvayā hatā । vibhāvitaikadeśena deyaṃ yad abhiyujyate ।। atra haṃse priyā-gamana-mātra-vibhāvya-priyā-haraṇābhiyogaḥ prāptiḥ ।
vākyaṃ yad gūḍha-tulyārthaṃ tad udāharaṇaṃ matam ।। yathā śākuntale, rājā -katham ātmāpahāraṃ karomi ? bhavatu, evaṃ tāvad enāṃ vakṣye । bhavati yaḥ pauraveṇa rājñā dharmādhikāre niyuktaḥ so' ham avighna-kriyopalambhāya dharmāraṇyam idam āyātaḥ । ity ārabhya, śakuntalā-tumhe avedha । kiṃ bi hiae karia matedha । ṇa bo baaṇaṃ suṇissaṃ । atra sābhiprāya-gūḍhārthatayā tad idam udāharaṇam । śobhā svabhāva-prākaṭyaṃ yūnor anyonyam ucyate ।।
yathā ratnāvalyāṃ, sāgarikā -eṇaṃ pekkhia adisaddhaseṇa ṇa sakkaṇomi padādo padaṃ bi gantuṃ । tā kiṃ vā ettha karissaṃ ? vidūṣakaḥ -aho accariaṃ । īrisaṃ kaṇṇāraaṇaṃ māṇusaloe ṇa dīsadi । bho baassa taha takkemi paāvaiṇobi edaṃ ṇimmābia puṇo puṇo bihmao saṃbutto tti । rājā-sakhe mamāpy etad eva manasi vartate ity ādinā sāgarikā-vatsarājayor anyonya-nirvarṇanena rūpātiśaya-prakaṭanaṃ śobhā । aniścayāntaṃ yad vākyaṃ saṃśayaḥ sa nigadyate ।।
jīvanty athaiṣyati na vety abhiśaṅkito' smi । saudāminī-sphuraṇ-cañcalam eva saukhyam ।। ity atra mālatī kāmandhakyāḥ gṛhaṃ gatā vā jīvati vā na veti saṃśayena vākya-samāpter ayaṃ saṃśayaḥ । sva-pakṣe darśanaṃ hetor dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya-siddhaye ।।
gūḍhaṃ hi dāhātmakam asti tejaḥ । tad anya-tejo' bhibhavād vamanti ।। ity atra tapodhaneṣu gūḍha-dāhātmaka-tejaḥ-sadbhāve sādhye tat-sādhakasya anya-tejas tiraskāra-janita-tejaḥ-samudgāra-rūpasya hetoḥ sūrya-kānteṣu darśitatvād dṛṣṭāntaḥ । abhiprāyas tv abhūtārtho hṛdyaḥ sāmyena kalpitaḥ ।
abhiprāyaṃ pare prāhur mamatāṃ hṛdya-vastuni ।। vṛddhiṃ vā jhaṣaketanasya kurute nāloka-mātreṇa kim । darpaḥ syād amṛtena ced iha tad apy asty eva bimbādhare ।। ity atra candra-sāmyena mukhe amṛta-kalpanād ayam abhiprāyaḥ । athavā tatraivātihṛdya-bimbādhare rājño mamatvam abhiprāyaḥ ।
yathārthānāṃ prasiddhānāṃ kriyate parikīrtanam । paropekṣā-vyudāsārthaṃ tan nidarśanam ucyate ।। mānuṣīṣu kathaṃ vā syād asya rūpasya sambhavaḥ । na prabhā-tarala-jyotir udeti vasudhā-talāt ।।
atra prati-vastu-nyāyena sadṛśa-vastu-kīrtanaṃ nidarśanam । atarkitopapannaḥ syāt siddhir iṣṭārtha-saṅgamaḥ ।। yathā mālavikāgnimitre, vidūṣakaḥ -hī hī baassa edaṃ khu sīhupāṇu-bejjidassa macchaāḍiā ubaṇadā । vidūṣakaḥ-esā ṇādiparikkhidabesā ūsuabaaṇā eāiṇī mālabiā adūre baṭṭadi ।
rājā -kathaṃ mālavikā । vidūṣakaḥ-aha iṃ । rājā-śakyam idānīṃ jīvitam avalambitam ity atra irāvatī-saṅketaṃ gacchato rājñaḥ mālavikā-darśana-siddhir acintitā siddhiḥ । prasiddhir loka-vikhyātair vākyair artha-prasādhanam ।।
malinam api himāṃśor lakṣma lakṣmīṃ tanoti । kim iva hi madhurāṇāṃ maṇḍanaṃ nākṛtīnām ।। atra śavalādy-anuvedhe' pi ramaṇīyatayā prasiddhānāṃ sarasijādīnāṃ kathanena śakuntalā-manojñatā-sādhanaṃ prasiddhiḥ । cittānuvartanaṃ yatra tad dākṣiṇyam itīritam ।।
yathā śākuntale, senāpatiḥ-jayatu svāmī । rājā-bhadra senāpate mandotsāhaḥ kṛto' smi mṛgayāpavādinā māḍhavyena । senāpatiḥ -sakhe sthira-pratibandho bhava । ahaṃ tāvat svāminaś citta-vṛttim anuvartiṣye । pralapatv eṣa vaidheyaḥ । nanu prabhur eva nidarśanam । sattvānām api lakṣyate vikṛtimac cittaṃ bhaya-krodhayoḥ ।
mithyaiva vyasanaṃ vadanti mṛgayāmīdṛg vinodaḥ kutaḥ ।। ity atra senāpateḥ rāja-cittānuvartanaṃ dākṣiṇyam । uktārthānupapattyā'nyo yasminn arthaḥ prakalpyate । vākya-mādhurya-saṃyuktā sārthāpattir udāhṛtā ।।
yathā ratnāvalyāṃ, vidūṣakaḥ-bhoḥ esā kkhu tue apubbā sirī samāsādidā । rājā-vayasya, satyam । śrīr eṣā pāṇir apy asyāḥ pārijātasya pallavaḥ । kuto' nyathā sravaty eṣa sveda-cchadmāmṛta-dravaḥ ।।
atra sveda-cchadmāmṛta-dravotpatter anyathānupapattyā pāṇeḥ pārijātatva-kalpanād iyam arthāpattiḥ । siddhān bahūn pradhānārthān uktvā yatra prayujyate । viśeṣa-yuktaṃ vacanaṃ vijñeyaṃ tad viśeṣaṇam ।। makarandaḥ -katham acireṇaiva nirmāya likhitaḥ ślokaḥ ।
prakṛti-madhurāḥ santy evānye mano madayanti ye । nayana-viṣayaṃ janmany ekaḥ sa eva mahotsavaḥ ।। ity atra indukalādīn mano-mada-hetutayā prasiddhān uktvā tat-samāna-mādhuryāyām api mālatyāṃ viśeṣa-kathanād idaṃ viśeṣaṇam । bahūnāṃ tu prayuktānāṃ padānāṃ bahubhiḥ padaiḥ ।
uccayaḥ sadṛśārtho yaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ padoccayaḥ ।। saha maṇi-balaehiṃ bāha-dhārā galaṃti । sahaa taṇu-ladāe dubbalā jīvidāsā ।। saha maṇi-valayair bāṣpa-dhārā galanti ।
saha ca tanu-latayā durbalā jīvitāśā ।।] ity atra śvāsa-daṇḍādīnāṃ dīrgha-bhāvādi-kriyāsu divasa-niśādibhiḥ saha samāveśād ayaṃ padoccayaḥ । rūpakair upamābhir vā tulyārthābhiḥ prayojitaḥ । apratyakṣārtha-saṃsparśas tulya-tarka itīritaḥ ।। āścaryam utpala-dṛśo vadanāmalendu- sāṃnidhyato mama muhur jadimānam etya ।
jātyena candramaṇineva mahī-dharasya sandhāryate drava-mayo manasā vikāraḥ ।। ity atra indu-candrakāntādy-upamayā paratyakṣasya sneha-rūpa-vikārasya kathanāt tulya-tarkaḥ ।। vicāras tv eka-sādhyasya bahu-sādhana-varṇanam ।। tasyā bhavān api manoratha-labdha-bandhuḥ ।
yasmin vidhiś ca madanaś ca kṛtābhiyogaḥ ।। atra saṅgama-rūpa-sādhyārtha-siddhaye parasparānurāga-siddhi-madana-rūpāṇām upāyānāṃ sad-bhāva-kathanād vicāraḥ । vicārasyānyathābhāvo vijñeyas tad-viparyayaḥ ।। prajñā jāmbavato' pi yatra na gatiḥ putrasya vāyor api ।
saumitrer api patriṇām aviṣayas tatra priyā kvāpi me ।। atra bahūpāya-sāmarthyābhāva-kathanād vicāra-viparyayaḥ spaṣṭa eva । guṇātipāto vyatyasta-guṇākhyānam udāhṛtam ।। yathā veṇī-saṃhāre, bhīmaḥ-bho bho alam alam āśaṅkayā ।
kartā dyūta-cchalānāṃ jatu-maya-śaraṇoddīpanaḥ so' timānī kṛṣṇākeśottarīya-vyapanayana-marut pāṇḍavā yasya dāsāḥ । rājā duḥśāsanāder gurur anuja-śatasyāṅga-rājasya mitraṃ kvāste duryodhano' sau kathayata na ruṣā draṣṭum abhyāgatau svaḥ ।। atra adhikṣepa-vākyatvād vyatyasta-guṇākhyānaṃ spaṣṭam eva । bahūn guṇān kīrtayitvā sāmānyena ca saṃśrayān ।
viśeṣaḥ kīrtyate yatra jñeyaḥ so' tiśayo budhaiḥ ।। yathā vikramorvaśīye, rājā -anena priyopalabdhi-śaṃsinā mandra-kaṇṭha-garjitena samāśvāsito' smi । sādharmyāc ca bhūyasī me tvayi prītiḥ । avyucchinna-pṛthu-pravṛtti bhavato dānaṃ mamāpy arthiṣu । sarvaṃ mām anu te priyā-virahajāṃ tvaṃ tu vyathāṃ mānubhūḥ ।।
ity atra samāna-dharmaṇi gajādhirāje purūravasā priyā-virahābhāva-kathanād atiśayaḥ । niruktir niravadyoktir nāmāny artha-prasiddhaye ।। yathā śākuntale, priyaṃvadā-halā sauṃdale ! ettha ebba dāva muhuttaaṃ ciṭṭha । jāba tue ubagadāe ladā-saṇāho bia aaṃ kesara-rukkhao paḍibhādi । śakuntalā-ado khu piaṃbadāsi tumaṃ । atra priyaṃvadāyāḥ priya-bhāṣaṇād idaṃ nāma-dheyam ity uktir niruktiḥ ।
loke guṇātirikānāṃ bahūnāṃ yatra nāmabhiḥ । eko' pi śabdyate tat tu vijñeyaṃ guṇa-kīrtanam ।। tvaṃ kaumudī nayanayor amṛtaṃ tvam aṅge । tām eva śāntam athavā kim ihottareṇa ।।
ity atra amṛta-kaumudī-prabhṛtināmabhiḥ sītā-śaṃsanaṃ guṇa-kīrtanam । yatra saṅkīrtayan doṣān guṇam arthena darśayet । guṇān vā kīrtayan doṣān darśayed garhaṇaṃ tu tat ।। yathā mālatī-mādhave, lavaṅgikā-bhaabadi kisaṇa-cauddasī-raaṇi-mahā-masāṇa-saṃcāra-ṇibbaḍia-bisama-bbabasāo ṇiṭṭhābida-caṇḍa-pāsaṇḍ-uddaṇḍa-bhua-daṇḍa-sāhaso sāhasio kkhu eso । ado kkhu me pia-sahī ukkaṃpidā । makarandaḥ -sādhu lavaṅgike sādhu । sthāne khalv anurāgopakārayor garīyasor upanyāsaḥ ।
ity atra mahā-māṃsa-vikraya-sāhasasya doṣa-rūpeṇa kathene' pi mādhavānurāgotpādana-guṇatayā paryavasitam idaṃ pramukha-garhaṇatvād garhaṇam । guṇa-kīrtane doṣa-paryavasānam, yathā mālatī-mādhave, madayantikā -dummaṇāadi vā iaṃ vāmasīlā । lavaṅgikā-kahaṃ ṇāma ṇava-vahū-vissaṃbhaṇobāajāṇaaṃ laḍahaṃ biaḍḍha-mahura-bhāsaṇaṃ arosaṇaṃ akādaraṃ de bhādaraṃ bhattāraṃ samāsādia dummaṇāissadi me piasahī । madayantikā-pekkha buddha-rakkhide ! bippadībaṃ ubālabhīāmo ।
ity atra mukhato guṇa-kīrtanam apy antato doṣāyeti garhaṇam idam । abhyarthanā-paraṃ vākyaṃ vijñeyo' nunayo budhaiḥ ।। mama ca mṛditaṃ kṣaumaṃ bālye tvad-aṅga-vivartanaiḥ । vacana-vikṛtiṣv asya krodho mudhā kriyate tvayā ।।
ity atra aśvatthāma-prārthanam anunayaḥ । patanaṃ prakṛtād arthād anyasmin bhraṃśa īritaḥ ।। yathā prasanna-rāghave, rāvaṇaḥ -kathaya kva tāvat karṇānta-niveśanīya-guṇaṃ kanyā-ratnaṃ kārmukaṃ ca । mañjarīkaḥ-idaṃ tāvat kārmukam । kanyā tu caramaṃ locana-patham avatariṣyati ।
rāvaṇaḥ -dhiṅ mūrkha ! kathaṃ re rāśi-nakṣatra-pāṭhakānāṃ goṣṭhīṃ na dṛṣṭavān asi । te' pi kanyām eva prathamaṃ prakaṭayanti । caramaṃ dhanuḥ । mañjarīkaḥ -katham ayaṃ vācāṭatām eva prakaṭayati । ity atra rāvaṇena dhanuḥ-kanyayoḥ prakṛtam arthaṃ parityajya rāśi-lakṣaṇasyārthasya prasañjanād ayaṃ bhraṃśaḥ । leśaḥ syād iṅgita-jñāna-kṛd viśeṣaṇavad vacaḥ ।।
ihāyātaḥ sampraty avikala-śarac-candra-vadanaḥ । kaṭākṣair nārīṇāṃ kuvalayita-vātāyanam iva ।। ity atra kāmandakyā mālaty-anurāga-jñāna-nivedanasya unmāda-taralair iti viśeṣaṇasya kathanād ayaṃ leśaḥ । kṣobhas tv anya-gate hetāv anyasmin kārya-kalpanaṃ ।।
mama kaṇṭha-gatāḥ prāṇāḥ pāśe kaṇṭha-gate tava । anarthārtha-prayatno' yaṃ tyajyatāṃ sāhasaṃ priye ।। atra pāśe vāsavadattā-kaṇṭha-gate tat-kārya-bhūtasya prāṇānāṃ kaṇṭha-gatatvasya vatsa-rājena svasmin kalpanāt kṣobhaḥ । manorathas tu vyājena vivakṣita-nivedanam ।।
yathā śākuntale, śakuntalā -ladā-ballaa saṃdāba-hāraa āmaṃtemi tumaṃ bhūobi pairbhoassa । atra latā-maṇḍapa-vyājena duṣyantāmantraṇaṃ manorathaḥ । prastāvanaiva śeṣo' rtho yatrānukto' pi gṛhyate । anukta-siddhir eṣā syād ity āha bharato muniḥ ।।
Nāṭ prastāvenaiva śeṣo' rthaḥ kṛtsno yan na pratīyate । vacanena vinānukta-siddhiḥ sā parikīrtitā ।। dṛṣṭa-śrutānubhūtārtha-kathanādi-samudbhavam । sādṛśyaṃ yatra saṅkṣobhāt tat sārūpyaṃ nirūpyate ।। kṣībo balena bhujayor hata-rāja-putra ।
jīvan prayāsi na padāt padam adya pāpa ।। ity atra cārvāka-śrāvita-duryodhana-vijaya-saṅkathā-saṅkṣepeṇa yudhiṣṭhirādīnāṃ bhīme suyodhana-buddhi-kathanād idaṃ sārūpyam । īpsitārtha-prasiddhy-arthaṃ kathyante yatra sūribhiḥ । prayojanāny anekāni sā mālety abhidhīyate ।।
prītir virāṭa-nṛpater upakāriṇaś ca । sarvaṃ punar militam atra mamaiva bhāgyaiḥ ।। yat prasannena manasā pūjyaṃ pūjayitur vacaḥ । stuti-prakāśanaṃ tat tu jñeyaṃ madhura-bhāṣaṇam ।।
pratyūhena kratūnāṃ na khalu makha-bhujo bhuñjate vā havīṃṣi । yat samprāpto' si kiṃ vā raghu-kula-tapasām īdṛśo' yaṃ vivartaḥ ।। api gṛhāṅgaṇa-mātra-kuṭumbinaḥ । pratibhayonnatir astu kutas tu naḥ ।।
ity ādāv anyonyaṃ pūjā-vacanaṃ madhura-bhāṣaṇam । praśnenaivottaraṃ yatra sā pṛcchā parikīrtitā ।। sarva-kṣiti-bhṛtāṃ nātha dṛṣṭā sarvāṅga-sundarī । rāmā ramye vanānte' smin mayā virahitā tvayā ।।
ity atra parvatānāṃ nātha mayā virahitā priyā tvayā dṛṣṭeti praśne rājñāṃ nātha tvayā virahitā mayā dṛṣṭety uttarasya pratīyamānatvād iyaṃ pṛcchā । pratigṛhya tu śāstrārthaṃ yad vākyam abhidhīyate । vidvan-manoharaṃ svantam upadiṣṭaṃ tad ucyate ।। yathā śākuntale, śakuntalā -paurava rakkha abiṇaaṃ । maaṇa-saṃtattābi ṇa hu attaṇo pahabāmi ।
rājā-bhīru alaṃ guru-janād bhayena । na te vidita-dharmā hi bhagavān doṣam atra grahīṣyati kulapatiḥ । api ca- gāndharveṇa vivāhena bahvyo rājarṣi-kanyakāḥ । śrūyante pariṇītās tāḥ pitṛbhiś cānumoditāḥ ।। ity atra śāstrānurodhenaiva pravṛttatvād idam upadiṣṭam ।
yathādeśaṃ yathā-kālaṃ yathā-rūpaṃ ca varṇyate । yat pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā tad dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭavan matam ।। yathā mālavikāgnimitre, rājā-aho sarvāsv avasthāsu cārutā śobhāntaraṃ puṣyati । tathā hi- kṛtvā śyāmā-viṭapa-sadṛśaṃ srasta-muktaṃ dvitīyam ।
nṛttād asyāḥ sthitam atitarāṃ kāntam ṛjvāyatārdham ।। ity atra itara-samakṣaṃ sthitāyāḥ saṃsthāna-jāti-varṇanād idaṃ pratyakṣa-dṛṣṭam । saubhāgyam aṃsa-viralī-kṛta-keśa-pāśam । vyāmohanaṃ navam upaimi kṛpā-viśeṣam ।।
ity atra apratyakṣasyaiva gopāla-sundarasya saṃsthāna-viśeṣa-jāti-varṇanād api dṛṣṭavad ābhāsanād idam apratyakṣa-dṛṣṭam । viśrāṇitāneka-vibhūṣaṇena । sa-lakṣma-lakṣyāṇi muner matena ।। sākṣad evopadeśena prāyo dharma-samanvayāt ।
aṅgāṅgi-bhāva-sampanna-samasta-rasa-saṃśrayāt ।। prakṛty-avasthā-sandhyādi-sampatty-upanibandhanāt । āhuḥ prakaraṇādīnāṃ nāṭakaṃ prakṛtiṃ budhāḥ ।। atideśa-bala-prāpata-nāṭakāṅgopajīvanāt ।
anyāni rūpakāṇi syur vikārā nāṭakaṃ prati ।। ato hi lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ nāṭakasyābhidhīyate । divyena vā mānuṣeṇa dhīrodāttena saṃyutam ।। śṛṅgāra-vīrānyatara-pradhāna-rasa-saṃśrayam ।
khyāteti vṛtta-sambaddhaṃ sandhi-pañcaka-saṃyutam ।। prakṛty-avasthā-sandhy-aṅga-sandhy-antara-vibhūṣaṇaiḥ । patākā-sthānakair vṛtti-tad-aṅgaiś ca pravṛttibhiḥ ।। viṣkambhakādibhir yuktaṃ nāṭakaṃ tat trivargadam ।
tad etan nāṭakārambha-prakāro vakṣyate mayā ।। vidher yathaiva saṅkalpo mukhatāṃ pratipadyate । pradhānasya prabandhasya tathā prastāvanā smṛtā ।। arthasya pratipādyasya tīrthaṃ prastāvanocyate ।
prastāvanāyās tu mukhe nāndī kāryā śubhāvahā ।। āśīrnamaskriyā-vastunirdeśānyatamā smṛtā । candranāmāṅkitā prāyo maṅgalārtha-padojjvalā ।। aṣṭābhir daśabhiś ceṣṭā seyaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ padaiḥ ।
samair vā viṣamair vāpi prayojyety apare jaguḥ ।। kaṭākṣāḥ kāruṇya-praṇaya-rasa-veṇī-laharayaḥ । sudhā-sāra-smerāḥ sucarita-viśeṣaika-sulabhāḥ ।। idaṃ kavibhyaḥ pūrvebhyah namo-vākaṃ praśāsmahe ।
vandemahi ca tāṃ vāṇīm amṛtām ātmanaḥ kalām ।। svānte śānti-praṇayini samunmīlad-ānanda-sāndram । vyāja-vyaktīkṛtam iva jagad-vyāpi candrārdha-mauleḥ ।। atha svasthāya devāya nityāya hata-pāpmane ।
tyakta-krama-vibhāgāya caitanya-jyotiṣe namaḥ ।। daśa-padānvitā yathā abhirāma-rāghave kriyāsuḥ kalyāṇam ity ādi । dvādaśa-padānvitā, yathā anargha-rāghave- koka-prīti-cakora-pāraṇa-paṭū jyotiṣmatī locane । nābhī-palvala-puṇḍarīka-mukulaḥ kamboḥ sapatnī-kṛtaḥ ।।
atraiva maṅgalārtha-pada-prāyatvaṃ candranāmāṅkitatvaṃ ca draṣṭavyam । nāndy-ante tu praviṣṭena sūtradhāreṇa dhīmatā । prasādhanāya raṅgasya vṛttir yojyā hi bhāratī ।। aṅgāny asyāś ca catvāri bharatenāvabhāṣire ।
prarocanāmukhe caiva vīthī-prahasane iti ।। vīthī prahasanaṃ sva-sva-prasaṅge vakṣyate sphuṭam । prarocanā tu sā proktā prakṛtārtha-praśaṃsayā ।। sadasya-citta-vṛttīnāṃ saṃmukhīkaraṇaṃ ca yat ।
praśaṃsā tu dvidhā jñeyā cetanācetanāśrayā । acetanau deśa-kālau kālo madhu-śaran-mukhaḥ ।। ālola-stavaka-stanīr aviralādhūta-pravālādharāḥ । atyārūḍha-rasālasāla-rasikāḥ kānte vasantodaye ।।
sat-pakṣāṃ madhura-giraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ । nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kāla-vaśān medinī-pṛṣṭhe ।। deśas tu devatārāja-tīrtha-sthānādir ucyate । tad adya kāla-nāthasya yātretyādiṣu lakṣyatām ।।
cetanās tu kathā-nātha-kavi-sabhya-naṭāḥ smṛtāḥ । kathā-nāthās tu dharmārtha-rasa-mokṣopayoginaḥ ।। dharmopayoginas tatra yudhiṣṭhira-nalādayaḥ । arthopayogino rudra-narasiṃha-nṛpādayaḥ ।।
rasopayogino vidyādhara-vatseśvarādayaḥ । mokṣopayogino rāma-vāsudevādayo matāḥ ।। eke tv abhedam icchanti dharma-mokṣopayoginoḥ ।। kavayas tu prabandhāras te bhaveyuś caturvidhāḥ ।
udātta uddhataḥ prauḍho vinīta iti bhedataḥ ।। antar-gūḍhābhimānoktir udātta iti gīyate ।। na cāpi kāvyaṃ navam ity avadyam । mūḍhaḥ para-pratyayaneya-buddhiḥ ।।
atra santaḥ parīkṣety anena sva-kṛteḥ parīkṣaṇa-kṣamatva-kalpito nija-garvaḥ kāli-dāsena vivakṣita iti tasyodāttatvam । parāpavādāt svotkarṣa-vādī tūddhata ucyate ।। jānanti te kim api tān prati naiṣa yatnaḥ । kālo hy ayaṃ niravadhir vipulā ca pṛthvī ।।
atra jānanti te kim apīti parāpavādāt mama tu ko' pi samāna-dharmety ātmotkarṣa-kathanāc ca bhavabhūter uddhatatvam । yathocita-nijotkarṣa-vādī prauḍha itīritaḥ ।। rasa-śreṇī-marma-vyavaharaṇa-hevāka-rasikaḥ । amandānandātmā pariṇamati sandarbha-mahimā ।।
atra rasa-prauḍhi-sandarbha-prasādayor nāṭaka-nirmāṇocitayor eva kathanāt nijotkarṣaṃ prakaṭayann ayaṃ kaviḥ prauḍha ity ucyate । yuktyā nijotkarṣa-vādī prauḍha ity aparaiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yathā mamaiva-nedānīntana-dīpikā kim u tamaḥ-saṅghātam unmūlayed ity ādi । atra jyotsnādi-dṛṣṭānta-mukhena mādhuryaujaḥ-prasādākhyānāṃ guṇānāṃ sva-sāhityaṃ rasaucityena pratipādayann ayaṃ kaviḥ prauḍha ity ucyate ।
vinīto vinayotkarṣāt svāpakarṣa-prakāśakaḥ ।। labhyeta yatnena gaveṣito' pi । santo' nurāgeṇa samādriyante ।। atra vinayotkarṣād apakarṣam ātmany āropayann ayaṃ kavir vinīta ity ucyate ।
sabhyās tu vibudhair jñeyā ye didṛkṣānivtā janāḥ । te' pi dvidhā prārthanīyāḥ prārthak iti ca sphuṭam ।। idaṃ prayokṣye yuṣmābhir anujñā dīyatām iti । samprārthyāḥ sūtradhāreṇa prārthanīyā iti smṛtāḥ ।।
tvayā prayogaḥ kriyatām ity utkaṇṭhita-cetasaḥ । ye sūtriṇaṃ prārthayante te sabhyāḥ prārthakāḥ smṛtāh ।। raṅgopajīvinaḥ proktā naṭās te' pi tridhā smṛtāḥ । vādakā gāyakāś caiva nartakāś ceti kovidaiḥ ।।
vīṇā-veṇu-mṛdaṅgādi-vādakā vādakāḥ smṛtāḥ । ālāpana-dhruvāgīta-gāyakā gāyakā matāḥ । nānā-prakārābhinaya-kartāro nartakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vistarād uta saṅkṣepāt prayuñjīta prarocanām ।।
loke hāri ca vatsa-rāja-caritaṃ nāṭye ca dakṣā vayam । mad-bhāgyopacayād ayaṃ samuditaḥ sarvo guṇānāṃ gaṇaḥ ।। atra kathā-nāyaka-kavi-sabhya-naṭānāṃ catūrṇāṃ saṅkṣepeṇa varṇanād iyaṃ saṅkṣipta-prarocanā । vistarāt tu bāla-rāmāyaṇādiṣu draṣṭavyā । evaṃ prarocayan sabhyān sūtrī kuryād athāmukham ।
sūtra-dhāro naṭīṃ brūte sva-kāryaṃ prati yuktitaḥ ।। prastutākṣepa-citroktyā yat tad āmukham īritam । trīṇyāmukhāṅgāny ucyante kathodghātaḥ pravartakaḥ ।। prayogātiśayaś ceti teṣāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate ।
sūtriṇo vākyam arthaṃ vā svetivṛtta-samaṃ yadā । svīkṛtya praviśet pātraṃ kathodghāto dvidhā mataḥ ।। dvīpād anyasmād api madhyād api jala-nidher diśo' py antāt । ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhir abhimatam abhimukhī-bhūtaḥ ।।
iti sūtradhārasya priyā-samāśvāsana-vākyaṃ svasyānukūlatayā paṭhato yaugandharāyaṇasya praveśāt kathodghātaḥ । nandantu pāṇḍu-tanayāḥ saha mādhavena । svasthā bhavantu kuru-rāja-sutāḥ sa-bhṛtyāḥ ।। atrottarārdhe sūtradhāreṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ svarga-sthiti-nirupadrava-lakṣaṇayor arthayor vivakṣitayoḥ satoḥ bhīmena svasthā bhavantu mayi jīvati dhārtarāṣṭrā iti nirupadrava-lakṣaṇasyaivārtha-viśeṣasya grahaṇena praveśaḥ kṛta iti ayam arthena kathodghātaḥ ।
ākṣiptaṃ kāla-sāmyena pravṛttiḥ syāt pravartakam ।। prakaṭita-rāmāmbhojaḥ kauśikavān sapadi lakṣmaṇānandī । śara-cāpa-namana-hetor ayam avatīrṇaḥ śarat-samayaḥ ।। atra viśvāmitra-rāma-lakṣmaṇānāṃ śarat-samaya-varṇana-sāmyena praveśaḥ pravartakaḥ ।।
eṣo' yam ity upakṣepāt sūtradhāra-prayogataḥ । prayoga-sūcanaṃ yatra prayogātiśayo hi saḥ ।। śirasā prathama-gṛhītām ājñām icchāmi pariṣadaḥ kartum । devyā iva dhāriṇyāḥ sevā-dakṣaḥ parijano' yam ।।
atrāyam ity upakṣepeṇākṣiptaḥ parijana-praveśaḥ prayogātiśayaḥ । tavāsmi gīta-rāgeṇa hāriṇā prasabhaṃ hṛtaḥ । eṣa rājeva duṣyantaḥ sāraṅgeṇātiraṃhasā ।। ity atra eṣa ity upakṣipto duṣyanta-praveśaḥ prayogātiśayaḥ ।
prastāvanā-sthāpaneti dvidhā syād idam āmukham । vidūṣaka-naṭī-pāripārśvikaiḥ saha saṃlāpan ।। stoka-vīthy-aṅga-sahitāny āmukhāṅgāni sūtra-bhṛt । yojayed yatra nāṭya-jñair eṣā prastāvanā smṛtā ।।
sarvāmukhāṅga-vīthy-aṅga-sametair vākya-vistaraiḥ । sūtradhāro yatra naṭī-vidūṣaka-naṭādibhiḥ ।। saṃlapana prastutaṃ cārtham ākṣipet sthāpanā hi sā । śṛṅgāra-pracure nāṭye yogyaḥ syād āmukha-kramaḥ ।।
ratnāvalydike prāyo lakṣyatāṃ kovidair ayam । vīrādbhutādi prāye tu prāyaḥ prastāvanocitā ।। anargha-rāghavādyeṣu prāyaśo vīkṣyatām iyam । hāsya-bībhatsa-raudrādi-prāye tu sthāpanā matā ।।
vīra-bhadra-vijṛmbhādau sā prāyeṇa samīkṣyatām । kathitāny āmukhāṅgāni vīthy-aṅgāni pracakṣmahe ।। āmukhe' pi ca vīthyāṃ ca sādhāraṇye' pi saṃmataḥ । vīthy-aṅga-saṃprathā teṣāṃ vīthyām āvaśyakatvataḥ ।।
udghātyakāvalagita-prapañca-trigate chalam । vākkely-adhibale gaṇḍam avasyandita-nālike ।। asat-pralāpa-vyāhārau mṛdavaṃ ca trayodaśa । tatrodghātyakam anyonyālāpa-mālā dvidhā hi tat ।
gūḍhāratha-pada-paryāya-kramāt praśnottara-kramāt ।। raso nāmāyaṃ kaḥ smṛti-surabhir āsvāda-mahimā । mano' vasthā jñātaṃ nanu vadasi nidrāntaram iti ।। atra raudra-rasa-svarūpa-vivecanāya rasāsvādāvasthā-lakṣaṇair gūḍhārtha-pada-paryāyair naṭa-sūtradhārayoḥ saṃlāpād idam ādimam udghātyakam ।
śrī-siṃhaḥ sa tu kīdṛśo vada nidhir dharmasya dharmas tu kaḥ । viśveśaḥ sa tu kīdṛśo vijayate viśveṣu viśveśavat ।। atra gūḍhārtha-pada-paryāya-rahita-praśnottara-krameṇa naṭa-sūtradhārayoḥ saṃlāpāt prakṛta-kavi-varṇanopayuktam idam udghātyakam । dvidhāvalagitaṃ proktam arthāvalaganātmakam ।
anya-prasaṅgād anyasya saṃsiddhiḥ prakṛtasya va ।। hanta sārasvataṃ cakṣuḥ kavīnāṃ krānta-darśinām । atiśayya pravarteta niyatārtheṣu vastuṣu ।। atra sūtradhāreṇa kavīnāṃ sārasvataṃ cakṣur iti kavi-sāmānya-varṇanena svābhilaṣita-kavi-viśeṣotkarṣa-sādhana-rūpāt prakṛtāerthāvalaganād avalagitam idam ।
sūtradhāraḥ-māriṣa, sthāne khalu bhavataḥ kutūhalam । saurabhya-nirbhara-gabhīra-manoharāṇi । etāni bibhrati murāri-kaver vacāṃsi ।। atrāprakṛta-vālmīki-varṇana-prasaṅgena prakṛta-māriṣa-kutūhalotkarṣa-saṃsādhana-rūpāt prakṛta-nāṭyāvalaganād idaṃ dvitīyam avalagitam ।
prapañcas tu mithaḥ stotram asad-bhūtaṃ ca hāsya-kṛt ।। ko' yaṃ gīta-śrama-vidhir aho bhinna-kaṇṭho' dya jātaḥ । maivaṃ vācyaṃ tvam asi hi gurus tatra ceṣṭiḥ pramāṇam ।। atra naṭa-sūtradhārayor anyathārthasyānyonya-stotrasya hāsyāyaiva pravṛttatvāt prapañcaḥ ।
śruti-sāmyād anekārtha-yojanaṃ trigataṃ bhavet ।। vāṇī-muraja-kvaṇitaṃ śruti-subhagaṃ kiṃ sudhā-mucaḥ stanitam । jaladasya kim ā jñātaṃ tava madhura-gabhīra-vāg-vilāso' yam ।। atra sūtradhāra-vāg-vilāse muraja-jalada-dhvani-vitarka-sambhāvanāt trigatam ।
proktaṃ chalaṃ sasotprāsaiḥ priyābhāsair vilobhanam ।। vidvān asau kalāvān api rasiko bahu-vidha-prayogajñaḥ । iti ca bhavantaṃ vidmo nirvyūḍhaṃ sādhu tat tvayā sarvam ।। atra viparīta-lakṣaṇayā prahelikārtham ajānataḥ pāripārśvikasyopālambhanāt chalam ।
sākāṅkṣasyaiva vākyasya vākkeliḥ syāt samāptitaḥ ।। kuhanā-bhairava-pāraṇonmukhābhyām । upari prastutam oṃ namaḥ śivāya ।। atra vākye sākāṅkṣe viśeṣāṃśam anuktvā namaḥ śivāyeti samāpti-kathanād vāk-keliḥ ।
spardhayānyonya-sāmarthya-vyaktis tv adhibalaṃ bhavet ।। mānin jānāsi kiṃ tvaṃ kim api na viditā cāturī me tvayā kim । patnyāhaṃ vaśya-karmā sapadi naṭavidhāv eṣa sajjībhavāmi ।। atra naṭa-sūtradhārayoḥ paraspara-spardhayā sva-sva-prayoga-sāmarthya-prakāśanād adhibalam ।
gaṇḍaṃ prastuta-sambandhi bhinnārthaṃ sahasoditam ।। nandantu pāṇḍu-tanayāḥ saha mādhavena । svasthā bhavantu kuru-rāja-sutāḥ sa-bhṛtyāḥ ।। tatra sūtradhāreṇa nirupadrava-lakṣaṇe' rthe vivakṣite' pi svarga-sthiti-lakṣaṇārtha-sūcakasya rakta-prasādhitaa-bhuva ity ādi-śliṣṭa-vākyasya sahasā prastuta-sambandhitayā bhāṣitatvād gaṇḍam ।
pūrvoktasyānyathā vyākhyā yatrāvasyanditaṃ hi tat ।। sat-pakṣā madhura-giraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ । nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kāla-vaśān medinī-pṛṣṭhe ।। pāripārśvikaḥ -śāntaṃ pāpam । pratihatam amaṅgalam ।
sūtradhāraḥ-mā bhaiṣīḥ । nanu śarat-samaya-varṇanāśaṃsayā haṃsān dhārtarāṣṭrā iti vyapadiśāmi । atra pūrvoktasya suyodhanādi-nipātasya haṃsa-pātatvena vyākhyānād idam avasyanditam । prahelikā nigūḍhārthā hāsyārthaṃ nālikā smṛtā । antar-lāpā bahir-lāpety eṣā dvedhā samīritā ।।
navyollasat-kusuma-rāji-virāji-bandham । nāṭya-prabandham atimañjula-saṃvidhānam ।। atra prasanna-rāghava-nāmety uttarasya saptākṣarāṣṭa-paṅkti-krameṇa likhite' sminn eva śloke mṛgyatvād antar-lāpo nāmeyam । kama-baḍḍhanta-vilāsaṃ rasāsale kaṃ karei kandappo ।
sūtradhāraḥ-aye praśnottaram । seyam asmat-prītir iti devādeśaḥ । tat svayam eva vācayāmi- nirbhaya-gurur vyadhatta ca vālmīki-kathāṃ kim anusṛtya ।। ity atra bāla-rāmāyaṇam ity uttarasya bahir eva mṛgyatvād bahir-lāpā nāma nālikeyam । asambaddha-kathālāpo' sat-pralāpa itīritaḥ ।।
patnī parilambi-kucā tanayā mama danturāpi taruṇa-vayāḥ । krīḍā-kapir asti gṛhe tad ahaṃ nāṭya-prayoga-marmajñaḥ ।। atra naṭena svakīya-nāṭya-prayoga-marmajñatve hetutayā kathitānāṃ krīḍā-kapi-sad-bhāvādīnām asambaddhatvād ayam asat-pralāpaḥ । anyārthaṃ vacanaṃ hāsya-karaṃ vyāhāra ucyate ।।
sūtradhāraḥ-ārye gargarike nūnam ānanda-kośa-nābhilāṣiṇī pariṣad iyam । naṭī-tā daṃsedu ayyo । tado kiṃ bilaṃbeṇa । sūtradhāraḥ-ayi gāyike gargarike bhavatyā mukha-vyāpāreṇa bījotthāpanānusandhāyinā bhavitavyam । naṭī -kīriso so muha-bābāro ।
sūtradhāraḥ-nanv amum eva śiśiram adhikṛtya dhruvā-gāna-rūpaḥ । ity atra ānanda-kośa-bījotthāpana-mukha-vyāpārāṇāṃ rūpaka-bījotthāpana-dhruvā-gānārthānām api anyārtha-pratītyā hāsyakaratvād ayaṃ vyāhāraḥ । doṣā guṇā guṇā doṣā yatra syur mṛdavaṃ hi tat ।। śāstrīyābhyasanāc chunām iva nṛṇām anyonya-kolāhalaḥ ।
vyākīrṇa-vyavahāra-nirṇaya-kṛte tv ekaiva kāryā smṛtiḥ ।। atra kāvyādiṣu guṇa-bhūteṣv api doṣatva-kathanād mṛdavam idam । evam āmukham āyojya sūtradhāre sahānuge । niṣkrānte' that tad-ākṣiptaiḥ pātrair vastu prapañcayet ।।
vastu sarvaṃ dvidhā sūcyam asūcyam iti bhedataḥ । rasa-hīnaṃ bhaved atra vastu tat sūcyam ucyate ।। yad vastu nīrasaṃ tat tu sūcayet sūcakās tv amī । viṣkambha-cūlikāṅkāsyāṅkāvatāra-praveśakāḥ ।।
tatra viṣkambho bhūta-bhāvi-vastv-aṃśa-sūcakaḥ । amukhya-pātra-racitaḥ saṅkṣepaika-prayojanaḥ ।। sa śuddho miśra ity ukto miśraḥ syān nīca-madhyamaiḥ । so' yaṃ ceṭī-naṭācārya-saṃlāpa-parikalpitaḥ ।।
mālavikāgnimitrasya prathamāṅke nirūpyatām । śuddhaḥ kevala-madhyo' yam ekāneka-kṛto dvidhā ।। ratnāvalyām eka-śuddhaḥ prāpta-yaugandharāyaṇaḥ । aneka-śuddho viṣkambhaḥ ṣaṣṭhāṅke' nargha-rāghave ।
nirūpyatāṃ samprayukto mālyavacchuka-sāraṇaiḥ ।। vandi-māgadha-sūtādyaiḥ pratisīrāntara-sthitaiḥ । arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yat tu kriyate sā hi cūlikā ।। sā dvidhā cūlikā khaṇḍa-cūlikā ceti bhedataḥ ।
pātrair yavanikāntaḥsthaiḥ kevalaṃ yā tu nirmitā ।। ādāv aṅkasya madhye vā cūlikā nāma sā smṛtā । praveśa-nirgamābhāvād iyam aṅkād bahir gatā ।। raghūṇāṃ gotrasya prasavitari deve savitari ।
praviṣṭo vaidehī dahanam atha śuddhā ca niragāt ।। ity ādau nepathya-gatair eva pātraiḥ sītā-jvalana-praveśa-nirgamādīnām arthānāṃ prayogānucitānāṃ sūcanād iyaṃ cūlikā । kaṇṭhe kṛttāvaśeṣaṃ kanaka-mayam adhaḥ śṛṅkhalā-dāma karṣan krāntvā dvārāṇi helācala-caraṇa-raṇat-kiṅkaṇī-cakravālaḥ । dattātaṅko' ṅganānām anusṛta-saraṇiḥ sambhramād aśva-pālaiḥ prabhraṣṭo' yaṃ plavaṅgaḥ praviśati nṛpater mandiraṃ mandurāyāḥ ।।
atra nepathya-gataiḥ pātraiḥ prayogānucitasya vānara-viplavādy-arthasya sūcanād iyaṃ madhya-cūlikā । raṅga-nepatha-saṃsthāyi-pātra-saṃlāpa-vistaraiḥ । ādau kevalam aṅkasya kalpitā khaṇḍa-cūlikā । praveśa-nirgamāprāpter iyam aṅkād bahir-gatā ।।
yathā bāla-rāmāyaṇe saptamāṅkasyādau, vaitālikaḥ-bhadra candana-caṇḍa parityaja nidrā-mudrām । vimuñca nijoṭajābhyantaram । nepathye-ayya kappura-caṃḍa esā miṭṭhā pabhāda-ṇiddā । karpūra-caṇḍaḥ-aho utsāha-śaktir bhavataḥ । amantra-śīlo mahī-patiḥ apara-prabandha-darśī kaviḥ apāṭha-ruciś ca vadnī na ciraṃ nandati । nepathye-tā ettha saṃtthara-tthido ṇimīlida-ṇaaṇo jebba suppabhādaṃ paṭhissaṃ ।
karpūra-caṇḍaḥ-etad api bhavato bhūri । tad upaślokayāvo rāmabhadram । viśvāmitra-mahāmuner nirupadhiḥ śiṣyo raghu-grāmaṇīḥ । kausalyā-nayanotsavo vijayatāṃ bhū-kāśyapasyātmajaḥ ।। pāṇiṃ deṃtassa gaṃgā-taralida-sasiṇo pabbaī-ballahassa ।
jaṃ bhaggaṃ tassa saddo ṇisuṇiti huaṇe bittharaṃto ṇamāi ।। pāṇiṃ dātur gaṅgā-taralita-śaśinaḥ parvatī-vallabhasya । yat bhagnaṃ tasya śabdo niḥśrūyate bhuvane vistaran na māti ।।] atra praviṣṭena karpūra-caṇḍena yavanikāntargatena candana-caṇḍena ca paryāya-pravṛtta-vāg-vilāsais tāṭakāvadhādi-vibhīṣaṇābhaya-pradānāntasya rāmabhadra-caritasya bāhulyāt prayogānucitasya sūcanād iyaṃ khaṇḍa-cūlikā ।
enāṃ viṣkambham evānye prāhur naitan mataṃ mama । apraviṣṭasya saṃlāpo viṣkambhe na hi yujyate । tad viṣkambha-śiraskatvān mateyaṃ khaṇḍa-cūlikā ।। pūrvāṅkānte sampraviṣṭaiḥ pātrair bhāvy-aṅka-vastunaḥ ।
sūcanaṃ tad-avicchityai yat tad aṅkāsyam īritam ।। yathā hi vīra-carite dvitīyāṅkāvasānake । praviṣṭena sumantreṇa sūcitaṃ rāma-vigrahe ।। vasiṣṭha-viśvāmitrādi-samābhāṣaṇa-lakṣaṇam ।
vastūttarāṅke pūrvārthāvicchedenaiva kalpitam ।। aṅkāvatāraḥ pātrāṇāṃ pūrva-kāryānuvartinām । avibhāgena sarveṣāṃ bhāviny aṅke praveśanam ।। dvitīyāṅke mālavikāgnimitre sa nirūpyatām ।
pātreṇāṅka-praviṣṭena kevalaṃ sūcitatvataḥ । bhaved aṅkād abāhyatvam aṅkāsyāṅkāvatārayoḥ ।। yan nīcaiḥ kevalaṃ pātrair bhāvi-bhūtārtha-sūcanam । aṅkayor ubhayor madhye sa vijñeyaḥ praveśakaḥ ।।
so' yaṃ ceṭi-dvayālāpa-saṃvidhānopakalpitaḥ । mālatī-mādhave prājñair dvitīyāṅke nirūpyatām ।। asūcyaṃ tu śubhodātta-rasa-bhāva-nirantaram । prārambhe yady asūcyaṃ syād aṅkam evātra kalpayet ।।
rasālaṅkāra-vastūnām upalālana-kāṅkṣiṇām । janany-aṅkavadādhāra-bhūtatvād aṅka ucyate ।। aṅkas tu pañcaṣair dvitrair aṅgino' ṅgasya vastunaḥ । rasasya vā samālamba-bhūtaiḥ pātrair manoharaḥ ।
saṃvidhāna-viśeṣaḥ syāt tatrāsūcyaṃ prapañcayet ।। asūcyaṃ tad dvidhā dṛśyaṃ śrāvyaṃ cādyaṃ tu darśayet । dvedhā dvitīyaṃ svagataṃ prakāśaṃ ceti bhedataḥ ।। svagataṃ svaika-vijñeyaṃ prakāśaṃ tad dvidhā bhavet ।
sarva-prakāśaṃ niyata-prakāśaṃ ceti bhedataḥ ।। sarva-prakāśaṃ sarveṣāṃ sthitānāṃ śravaṇocitam । dvitīyaṃ tu sthiteṣv apy eṣv ekasya śravaṇocitam ।। dvidhā vibhāvyate' nyac ca janāntam apavāritam ।
tripatākā-kareṇānyān apavāryāntarā kathām ।। anyenāmantraṇaṃ yat syāt taj janāntikam ucyate । rahasyaṃ kathyate' nyasya parāvṛtyāpavāritam ।। itthaṃ śrāvyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca prayujya susamāhitaiḥ ।
pātrair niṣkramaṇaṃ kāryam aṅkānte samam eva hi ।। aṅka-cchedaś ca kartavyaḥ kālāvasthānurodhataḥ । dinārdha-dinayor yogyam aṅke vastu pravartayet ।। aṅka-prasaṅgād garbhāṅka-lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyate mayā ।
rasanāyaka-vastūnāṃ mahotkarṣāya kovidaiḥ ।। aṅkasya madhye yo' ṅkaḥ syād asau garbhāṅka īritaḥ । vastu-sūcaka-nāndīko diṅ-mātra-mukha-saṅgataḥ ।। arthopakṣepakair hīnaś cūlikā-parivarjitaiḥ ।
aneṣyad-vastu-viṣayaḥ pātraiś tri-caturair yutaḥ ।। nātiprapañcetivṛttaḥ svādhārāṅkāṅga-śobhitaḥ । prastutārthānubandhī ca pātra-niṣkramaṇāvadhiḥ ।। prathamāṅke na kartavyaḥ so' yaṃ kāvya-viśāradaiḥ ।
so' yam uttara-rāme tu rasotkarṣāya kathyatām ।। netur utkarṣako jñeyo bāla-rāmāyaṇe tv ayam । amogha-rāghave so' yaṃ vastūtkarṣaika-kāraṇam ।। nāṭake' ṅkā na kartavyāḥ pañca-nyūnā daśādhikāḥ ।
tad īdṛśa-guṇopetaṃ nāṭakaṃ bhukti-muktidam ।। dharmārtha-sādhanaṃ nāṭyaṃ sarva-duḥkhāpanoda-kṛt । āsevadhvaṃ tad ṛṣayas tasyotthānaṃ tu nāṭakam ।। iti । nāṭakasya tu pūrṇādi-bhedāḥ kecana kalpitāḥ ।
teṣāṃ nātīva ramyatvād aparīkṣākṣamatvataḥ । muninānādṛtatvāc ca tān uddeṣṭum udāsmahe ।। yatretivṛttam utpādyaṃ dhīra-śāntaś ca nāyakaḥ । rasaḥ pradhānaṃ śṛṅgāraḥ śeṣaṃ nāṭakavad bhavet ।।
tad dhi prakaraṇaṃ śuddhaṃ dhūrtaṃ miśraṃ ca tat tridhā । kula-strī-nāyakaṃ śuddhaṃ mālatī-mādhavādikam ।। gaṇikā-nāyikaṃ dhūrtaṃ kāmadattāhvayādikam । kitava-dhyputakārādi-vyāpāraṃ tv atra kalpayet ।।
miśraṃ tat kulajā-veśye kalpite yatra nāyike । dhūrta-śuddha-kramopetaṃ tan mṛcchakaṭikādikam ।। nāṭikā tv anayor bhedo na pṛthag rūpakaṃ bhavet । prakhyātaṃ nṛpater vṛttaṃ nāṭakād āhṛtaṃ yataḥ ।।
buddhi-kalpita-vastutvaṃ tathā prakaraṇād api । vimarśa-sandhi-rāhityaṃ bhedakaṃ cen na tan matam ।। ratnāvalyādike lakṣye tat-sandher api darśanāt । strī-prāya-caturaṅkādi-bhedakaṃ cen na tan matam ।।
eka-dvi-try-aṅka-pātrādi-bhedenānantatā yataḥ । devī-vaśāt saṅgamena bhedaś cet tan na yujyate । mālavikāgni-mitrādau nāṭikātva-prasaṅgataḥ ।। prakaraṇikā-nāṭikayor anusaraṇīyā hi nāṭikā-saraṇiḥ ।
ata eva bharata-muninā nāṭyaṃ daśadhā nirūpitaṃ pūrvam ।। khyātena vā kalpitena vastunā prākṛtair naraiḥ । anvitaḥ kaiśikī-hīnaḥ sāttvatyārabhaṭī-mṛduḥ ।। strīṇāṃ vilāpa-vyāpārair upetaḥ karuṇāśrayaḥ ।
nānā-saṅgrāma-saṃnāha-prahāramaraṇotkaṭaḥ ।। mukha-nirvāhavān yaḥ syād eka-dvi-try-aṅka icchayā । utsṛṣṭikāṅkaḥ sa jñeyaḥ sa-viṣkambha-praveśakaḥ ।। asminn amaṅgala-prāye kuryān maṅgalam antataḥ ।
prayojyasya vadhaḥ kāryaḥ punar ujjīvanāvadhiḥ ।। ujjīvanād apy adhikaṃ manoratha-phalo' pi vā । vijñeyam asya lakṣyaṃ tu karuṇākandalādikam ।। khātetivṛtta-sampanno niḥsahāyaka-nāyakaḥ ।
yukto daśāvaraih khyātair uddhataiḥ pratināyakaiḥ ।। vimarśa-garbha-rahito bhāraty-ārabhaṭī-sphuṭaḥ । hāsya-śṛṅgāra-rahita ekāṅko raudra-saṃśrayaḥ ।। eka-vāsara-vṛttāntaḥ prāpta-viṣkambha-cūlikaḥ ।
astrī-nimitta-samaro vyāyogaḥ kathito budhaiḥ । vijñeyam asya lakṣyaṃ tu dhanañjaya-jayādikam ।। svasya vānyasya vā vṛttaṃ viṭena nipuṇoktinā । śaurya-saubhāgya-saṃstutyā vīra-śṛṅgāra-sūcakam ।।
buddhi-kalpitam ekāṅkaṃ mukha-nirvahaṇānvitam । varṇyate bhāratī-vṛttyā yatra taṃ bhāṇam īrate ।। eka-pātra-prayojye' smin kuryād ākāśa-bhāṣitam । anyenānuktam apy anyo vacaḥ śrutveva yad vadet ।।
iti kiṃ bhaṇasīty etad bhaved ākāśa-bhāṣitam । lāsyāṅgāni daśaitasmin saṃyojyānyatra tāni tu ।। geya-padaṃ sthita-pāṭhyam āsīnaṃ puṣpa-gandhikā । pracchedakas trimūḍhaṃ ca saindhavākhyaṃ dvimūḍhakam ।
uttamottamakaṃ cānyad ukta-pratyuktam eva ca ।। vīṇādi-vādanenaiva sahitaṃ yatra bhāvyate । lalitaṃ nāyikā-gītaṃ tad geya-padam ucyate ।। cañcat-puṭādinā vākyābhinayo nāyikā-kṛtaḥ ।
bhūmi-cārī-pracāreṇa sthita-pāṭhyaṃ tad ucyate ।। bhrū-netra-pāṇi-caraṇa-vilāsābhinayānvitam । yojyam āsīnayā pāṭhyam āsīnaṃ tad udāhṛtam ।। nānā-vidhena vādyena nānā-tāla-layānvitam ।
lāsyaṃ prayujyate yatra sā jñeyā puṣpa-gandhikā ।। anyāsaṅgama-śaṅkinyā nāyakasyātiroṣayā । prema-ccheda-prakaṭanaṃ lāsyaṃ pracchedakaṃ viduḥ ।। aniṣṭhura-ślakṣṇa-padaṃ sama-vṛttair alaṅkṛtam ।
nāṭyaṃ puruṣa-bhāvāḍhyaṃ trimūḍhakam udāhṛtam ।। deśa-bhāṣā-viśeṣeṇa calad-valaya-śṛṅkhalam । lāsyaṃ prayujyate yatra tat saindhavam iti smṛtam ।। cārībhir lalitābhiś ca citrārthābhinayānvitam ।
spaṣṭa-bhāva-rasopetaṃ lāsyaṃ yat tad dvimūḍhakam ।। aparijñāta-pārśvasthaṃ geya-bhāva-vibhūṣitam । lāsyaṃ sotkaṇṭha-vākyaṃ tad uttamottamakaṃ bhavet ।। kopa-prasāda-janitaṃ sādhikṣepa-padāśrayam ।
vākyaṃ tad ukta-pratyuktaṃ yūnoḥ praśnottarātmakam ।। śṛṅgāra-mañjarī-mukhyam asyodāharaṇaṃ matam । lāsyāṅga-daśakaṃ tatra lakṣyaṃ lakṣya-vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। prakhyātenetivṛttena nāyakair api tad-vidhaiḥ ।
pṛthak-prayojanāsaktair militair deva-dānavaiḥ ।। yuktaṃ dvādaśabhir vīra-pradhānaṃ kaiśikī-mṛdu । try-aṅkaṃ vimarśa-hīnaṃ ca kapaṭa-traya-saṃyutam ।। tri-vidravaṃ tri-śṛṅgāraṃ vidyāt samavakārakam ।
mohātmako bhramaḥ proktaḥ kapaṭas trividhas tv ayam ।। sattvajaḥ śatrujo daiva-janitaś ceti sattvajaḥ । krūra-prāṇi-samutpannaḥ śatrujas tu raṇādijaḥ ।। vātyāvarṣādi-sambhūto daivajaḥ kapaṭaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
udāharaṇam eteṣām āvege lakṣyatāṃ budhaiḥ ।। jīva-grāho' pi moho vā kapaṭād vidravas tataḥ । kapaṭa-traya-sambhūter ayaṃ ca trividho mataḥ । dharmārtha-kāma-sambaddhas tridhā śṛṅgāra īritaḥ ।।
vratādi-janitaḥ kāmo dharma-śṛṅgāra īritaḥ । pārvatī-śiva-sambhogas tad udāharaṇaṃ matam ।। yatra kāmena sambaddhair arthair arthānubandhibhiḥ । bhujyamānaiḥ sukha-prāptir artha-śṛṅgāra īritaḥ ।।
sārvabhauma-phala-prāpti-hetunā vatsa-bhūpateḥ । ratnāvalyā samaṃ bhogo vijñeyā tad udāhṛtiḥ ।। durādara-surā-pāna-para-dārādi-kelijaḥ । tat-tad-āsvāda-lalitaḥ kāma-śṛṅgāra īritaḥ ।।
tad udāharaṇaṃ prāyo dṛśyaṃ prasanādiṣu । śṛṅgāra-tritayaṃ tatra nātra bindu-praveśakau ।। mukha-pratimukhe sandhī vastu dvādaśa-nāḍikam । prathame kalpayed aṅke nāḍikā ghaṭikā-dvayam ।।
mukhādi-sandhi-trayavāṃś caturnāḍika-vastukaḥ । dvitīyāṅkas tṛtīyas tu dvi-nāḍika-kathāśrayaḥ ।। nirvimarśa-catuḥ-sandhir evam aṅkās trayaḥ smṛtāḥ । vīthī-prahasanāṅgāni kuryād atra samāsataḥ ।।
prastāvanāyāḥ prastāve prokto vīthy-aṅga-vistaraḥ । daśa prahasanāṅgāni tat-prasaṅge pracakṣmahe । udāharaṇam etasya payodhi-mathanādikam ।। sūcya-pradhāna-śṛṅgārā mukha-nirvahaṇānvitā ।
eka-yojyā dviyojyā vā kaiśikī-vṛtti-nirmitā ।। vīthy-aṅga-sahitaikāṅkā vīthīti kathitā budhaiḥ । asyāṃ prāyeṇa lāsyāṅga-daśakaṃ yojayen na vā ।। sāmānyā parakīyā vā nāyikātrānurāgiṇī ।
vīthy-aṅga-prāya-vṛttitvān nocitā kula-pālikā । lakṣyam asyās tu vijñeyaṃ mādhavī-vīthikādikam ।। vastu-sandhy-aṅka-lāsyāṅga-vṛttayo yatra bhāṇavat । raso hāsyaḥ pradhānaṃ syād etat prahasanaṃ matam ।।
viśeṣeṇa daśāṅgāni kalpayed atra tāni tu । avagalitāvaskandau vyavahāro vipralambha upapattiḥ । bhayam anṛtaṃ vibhrāntir gadgada-vāk ca pralāpaś ca ।। pūrvam ātma-gṛhītasya samācārasya mohataḥ ।
dūṣaṇaṃ tyajanaṃ cātra dvidhāvagalitaṃ matam ।। yāny ūrdhvaṃ paripoṣayanti puruṣās teṣāṃ muhuḥ khaṇḍanam । śrī-gītā ca harītakī ca harato hantopabhogyaṃ vayaḥ ।। atra kenāpi yati-bhraṣṭena sva-gṛhītasya yaty-āśramasya dūṣaṇād idam avagalitam ।
ayi pīṇa-ghaṇatthaṇa-sohaṇi palitatthakulaṃga-viloaṇi । jai lamasi kāvāliṇī-bhāvehiṃ sābakā kiṃ kalissaṃdi ।। aho kāvāliṇīadaṃsaṇaṃ jebba ekkaṃ saukkhamokkha-sāhaṇam । bho kābālia hagge tuhake saṃpadaṃ dāso saṃbutto । maṃ pi mahābhairavānusāsaṇe dikkhaya । [ayi pīna-ghana-stana-śobhane paritrasta-kuraṅga-vilocane ।
yadi ramase kāpālinī-bhāvaiḥ śrāvakāḥ kiṃ kariṣyanti । aho kāpālinī-darśanam eva ekaṃ saukhya-mokṣa-sādhanam । bho kāpālika ahaṃ tava samprataṃ dāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ । mām api mahā-bhairavānuśāsane dikṣaya ।] ity ādau kṣapaṇakasya sva-mārga-paribhraṃśa avagalitam । avaskandas tv anekeṣām ayogyasyaika-vastunaḥ ।
sambandhābhāsa-kathanāt sva-sva-yogyatva-yojanā ।। bauddhaḥ-dṛṣṭyor bhedaḥ kṣaṇika-mahimā saugate datta-pādaḥ । sarve-nābher mūlaṃ prathayati phalaṃ sarva-siddhānta-sāram ।। atra yati-bauddha-jainānāṃ gaṇikāyāṃ sva-sva-siddhānta-dharma-sambandha-kathanena sva-sva-pakṣa-parigraha-yogyatva-yojanād avaskandaḥ ।
vyavahāras tu saṃvādo dvitrāṇāṃ hāsya-kāraṇam ।। yathā tatraiva prahasane bauddhaḥ -kuto maṇḍa eka-daṇḍī । mithyā-tīrthaḥ -kṣaṇikavādī na sambhāṣaṇīya eva । tathāpi daṇḍam antardhāya niruttaraṃ karomi । aye śūnya-vādin ! adaṇḍaḥ amuṇḍo' ham āgalād asmi । jainaḥ -nūnam asau māyāvādī । aham api kim apy antardhāya prastutaṃ pṛcchāmi । aye mahā-pariṇāma-vādin ! bṛhad-bīja lomnāṃ samāna-jātīyatve' pi keṣāñcit saṅkartanam anyeṣāṃ saṃrakṣaṇam iti vyavasthitau kiṃ pramāṇam ?
mithyā-tīrthaḥ-jīvad amedhyaṃ jaṅgama-narako nara-piśāco' yam antardhāyāpi na sambhāṣaṇīyaḥ । niṣkaccha-kīrtiḥ -sakhe ! ārhata-mune vāde tvayā ayam apratipattiṃ nāma nigraha-sthānam āropito māyāvādī । mithyā-tīrthaḥ -nūnam imāv api mādṛśāv eva liṅga-dhāraṇa-mātreṇa kukṣimbharaī syātām । ity atra yati-bauddha-jainānāṃ saṃvādo vyavahāraḥ ।
vipralambho vañcanā syād bhūtāveśādi-kaitavāt ।। priyām ahaṃ pūrva-bhṛtāṃ nāmnā svacchanda-bhakṣiṇī । gṛhṇāmy enāṃ yadi trātuṃ kṛpā vaḥ śrūyatām idam ।। surāghaṭānāṃ saptatyā viṃśatyā dṛpta-gaḍḍuraiḥ ।
chāgaiś ca daśabhiḥ kāryā ciraṇṭī-tarpaṇa-kriyā ।। adya kartum aśakyaṃ cet tat-paryāptatamaṃ dhanam । āsthāpyam asyāḥ sākṣiṇyāḥ jaraṭhāyāḥ paṭāñcale ।। arūpāmbaraḥ -ekena sukham upādeyam । anyena dhanaṃ pradeyam iti kiṃ yuṣmad-dharmaḥ ?
niṣkaccha-kīrtiḥ sāntarhāsaṃ sva-dhanaṃ yati-dhanaṃ ca jaraṭhāyāḥ paṭāñcale baddhvā sabalātkāraṃ jainasya kaṭakaṃ tasyāḥ pāda-mūle' rpayati ।) madhumallikā -ammo devadā vilambeṇa kuppissadi । tā ciraṃṭi-ātappaṇaṃ kāduṃ gacchemi । ity ādau bhūtāveśa-kaitavena jaina-bauddha-saṃnyāsino vilobhya dhanaṃ kayāpi gaṇikayā gṛhītam ity ayaṃ vipralambhaḥ । upapattis tu sā proktā yat prasiddhasya vastunaḥ ।
loka-prasiddhayā yuktyā sādhanaṃ hāsya-hetunā ।। yathā tatraiva prahasane mithyā-tīrthaḥ -aye upasarit-tīre pippala-nāmā vanaspatiḥ । yaś ca gītāsu bhagavatā nija-vibhūtitayā nirdiṣṭaḥ । katham asya taror iyatī mahima-sambhāvanā । upapadyata eva- tat padaṃ tanu-madhyāyā yenāśvattha-dalopamam । tad-aśvattho' smi vṛkṣāṇām ity ūce bhagavān hariḥ ।। iti ।
atra loka-prasiddhena aśvattha-daloru-mūlayoḥ sāmyena hetunā loka-prasiddhasyaiva bhagavad-aśvatthayor aikyasya sādhanaṃ hāsya-kāraṇam upapattiḥ । smṛtaṃ bhayaṃ tu nagara-śodhakādi-kṛto daraḥ ।। yathā tatraiva prahasane jainaḥ-aho arājako' yaṃ viṣayaḥ yat nagara-parisarāśrita-tapasvināṃ dhanaṃ coryate । nagara-rakṣakāḥ-aye kim apahṛtaṃ dhanam । kiyat
arūpāmbaraḥ-dhik kaṣṭam । nagara-śīghrakāḥ samāyānti । ity ādau jainādīnāṃ bhaya-kathanād bhayam । anṛtaṃ tu bhaved vākyam asabhya-stuti-gumphitam । tad evānṛtam ity āhur apare sva-mata-stuteḥ ।। māñjiṣṭha-celam iva mānmatham ātapatram ।
yūnāṃ mude taruṇi tat padam ārtavaṃ te ।। atra ārtavāruṇasyoru-mūlasya varṇanād idam anṛtam । majjaṃ maṃsaṃ pijjae khajjae a । kolo dhammo kassa ṇo bhādi rammo ।।
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ pīyate khādyate ca । kaulo dharmaḥ kasya no bhāti ramyaḥ ।।] vastu-sāmya-kṛto moho vibhrāntir iti gīyate ।। hema-kumbhavatī ramya-toraṇā cāru-darpaṇā ।
kāpi gandharva-nagarī dṛśyate bhūmi-cāriṇī ।। jainaḥ-aye kṣaṇa-bhaṅga-vādin etad utpāta-phalaṃ prathama-darśino bhavata eva pariṇamet । bauddhaḥ -hanta kim apade bhrānto' smi । na purīyaṃ viśālākṣī na toraṇam ime bhruvau ।
na darpaṇam imau gaṇḍau na ca kumbhāv imau stanau ।। ity atra bauddhasya moho vibhrāntiḥ । asatya-ruditonmiśraṃ vākyaṃ gadgada-vāg bhavet ।। anupātta-bāṣpa-kaṇikaṃ gadgada-niḥśvāsa-kalitam avyaktam ।
anayor asatya-ruditaṃ suratānta-daśāṃ vyanaktīva ।। atra gadgada-vāktvaṃ spaṣṭam । pralāpaḥ syād ayogyasya yogyatvenānumodanam ।। pati-hīnā ca yā nārī jāyā-hīnaś ca yaḥ pumān ।
tau dampatī yathā-kāmaṃ bhavetām iti ghuṣyatām ।। viḍālākṣaḥ-devaḥ pramāṇam । naṣṭāśva-bhagna-śakaṭa-nyāyena pratipāditam । ucitā te mahārāja seyaṃ kāruṇya-ghoṣaṇā ।।
manvādayo mahīpālāḥ śataśo gām apālayan । na kenāpi kṛto mārga evam āścarya-śaukhyadaḥ ।। atra ayogyasyāpi rājādeśasya dharmādhikāriṇā guhya-grāhiṇā nyāya-parikalpanayā yogyatvenānumodanād ayaṃ pralāpaḥ । śuddhaṃ kīrṇaṃ vaikṛtaṃ ca tac ca prahasanaṃ tridhā ।
śuddhaṃ śrotriya-śākhāder veṣa-bhāṣādi-saṃyutam ।। ceṭa-ceṭī-jana-vyāptaṃ tal lakṣyaṃ tu nirūpyatām । ānanda-kośa-pramukhaṃ tathā bhagavad-ajjukam ।। kīrṇaṃ tu sarvair vīthy-aṅgaiḥ saṅkīrṇaṃ dhūrta-saṅkulam ।
tasyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ bṛhat-saubhadrakādikam ।। yac cedaṃ kāmukādīnāṃ veṣa-bhāṣādi-saṅgataiḥ । ṣaṇḍatāpa-savṛddhādyair yutaṃ tad vaikṛtaṃ bhavet । kalikeli-prahasana-pramukhaṃ tad udāhṛtam ।।
khyātetivṛttaṃ nirhāsya-śṛṅgāraṃ raudra-mudritam । sāttvatī-vṛtti-viralaṃ bhāraty-ārabhaṭī-sphuṭam ।। nāyakair uddhatair deva-yakṣa-rākṣasa-pannagaiḥ । gandharva-bhūta-vetāla-siddha-vidyādharādibhiḥ ।।
samanvitaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir nyāya-mārgaṇa-nāyakam । caturbhir āṅkair anvītaṃ nirvimarśaka-sandhibhiḥ ।। nirghātolkoparāgādi-ghora-krūrāji-sambhramam । sa-praveśaka-viṣkambha-cūlikaṃ hi ḍimaṃ viduḥ ।
asyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ vīrabhadra-vijṛmbhitam ।। yatretivṛttaṃ miśraṃ syāt sa-viṣkambha-praveśakam । catvāro' ṅkā nirvimarśa-garbhāḥ syuḥ sandhayas trayaḥ ।। dhīroddhattaś ca prakhyāto divyo martyo' pi nāyakaḥ ।
divya-striyam anicchantīṃ kanyāṃ vāhartum udyataḥ ।। strī-nimittāji-saṃrambhaḥ pañcaṣāḥ pratināyakāḥ । rasā nirbhaya-bībhatsā vṛttayaḥ kaiśikīṃ vinā ।। svalpas tasyāḥ praveśo vā so' yam īhāmṛgo mataḥ ।
vyājān nivārayed atra saṅgrāmaṃ bhīṣaṇa-kramam ।। tasyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ prājñair māyā-kuraṅgikā । itthaṃ śrī-siṃha-bhūpena sarva-lakṣaṇa-śālinā । sarva-lakṣaṇa-sampūrṇo lakṣito rūpaka-kramaḥ ।।
atha rūpaka-nirmāṇa-parijñānopayoginī । śrī-siṃha-dharaṇīśena paribhāṣā nirūpyate ।। paribhāṣātra maryādā pūrvācāryopakalpitā । sā hi naur atigambhīraṃ vivikṣor nāṭya-sāgaram ।।
eṣā ca bhāṣā-nirdeśa-nāmabhis trividhā matā । tatra bhāṣā dvidhā bhāṣā vibhāṣā ceti bhedataḥ ।। caturdaśa vibhāṣāḥ syuḥ prācyādyā vākya-vṛttayaḥ । āsāṃ saṃskāra-rāhityād viniyogo na kathyate ।।
uttamādiṣu tad-deśa-vyavahārāt pratīyatām । bhāṣā dvidhā saṃskṛtā ca prākṛtī ceti bhedataḥ ।। kaumāra-pāṇinīyādi-saṃskṛtā saṃskṛtā matā । iyaṃ tu devatādīnāṃ munīnāṃ nāyakasya ca ।
liṅgināṃ ca viṭādīnm anīcānāṃ prayujyate ।। prakṛteḥ saṃskṛtāyās tu vikṛtiḥ prākṛtī matā । ṣaḍ-vidhā sā prākṛtaṃ ca śaurasenī ca māgadhī ।। paiśācī cūlikā paiśācy apabhraṃśa iti kramāt ।
atra tu prākṛtaṃ strīṇāṃ sarvāsāṃ niyataṃ bhavet ।। kvacic ca devī gaṇikā mantrijā ceti yoṣitām । yoginy-apsarasoḥ śilpa-kāriṇyā api saṃskṛtam ।। ye nīcāḥ karmaṇā jātyā teṣāṃ prākṛtam ucyate ।
chadma-liṅgavatāṃ tadvaj jainānām iti kecana ।। adhame madhyame cāpi śaurasenī prayujyate । dhīvarādy-atinīceṣu māgadhī ca niyujyate ।। rakṣaḥ-piśāca-nīceṣu paiśācī-dvitayaṃ bhavet ।
apabhraṃśas tu caṇḍāla-yavanādiṣu yujyate ।। nāṭakādāv apabhraṃśa-vinyāsasyāsahiṣṇavaḥ । anye caṇḍālakādīnāṃ māgadhy-ādīn prayuñjate ।। sarveṣāṃ kāraṇa-vaśāt kāryo bhāṣā-vyatikramaḥ ।
māhātmyasya paribhraṃśaṃ madasyātiśayaṃ tathā ।। pracchādanaṃ ca vibhrāntiṃ yathālikhita-vācanam । kadācid anuvādaṃ ca kāraṇāni pracakṣate ।। sākṣād anāma-grāhyāṇāṃ janānāṃ pratisaṃjñayā ।
āhvāna-bhaṅgī nāṭyajñair nirdeśa iti gīyate ।। sa tridhā pūjya-sadṛśa-kaniṣṭha-viṣayatvataḥ । pūjyās tu devo munayo liṅginas tat-samāstriyaḥ ।। bahuśrutāś ca bhagavac-chabda-vācyā bhavanti hi ।
āryeti brāhmaṇo vācyo vṛddhas tāteti bhāṣyate ।। upādhyāyeti cācāryo gaṇikā tv ajjukākhyayā । mahārājeti bhūpālo vidvān bhāva itīryate ।। chandato nāmabhir vācyā brāhmaṇais tu narādhipāḥ ।
deveti nṛpatir vācyo bhṛtyaiḥ prakṛtibhis tathā ।। sārvabhaumaḥ parijanair bhaṭṭa-bhaṭṭāraketi ca । vācyo rājeti munibhir apatya-pratyayena vā ।। vidūṣakeṇa tu prāyaḥ sakhe rājan nitīcchayā ।
brāhmaṇaiḥ sacivo vācyo hy amātya saciveti ca ।। śaiṣāir āryety athāyuṣman iti sārathinā rathī । tapasvi-sādhu-śabdābhyāṃ praśāntaḥ paribhāṣyate ।। svāmīti yuva-rājas tu kumāro bhartṛ-dārakaḥ ।
āvutteti svasur bhartā syāleti pṛtanā-patiḥ ।। bhaṭṭinī svāminī devī tathā bhaṭṭāriketi ca । paricārajanair vācyā yoṣito rāja-vallabhāḥ ।। rājñā tu mahiṣī vācyā devīty anyāḥ priyā iti ।
sarveṇa patnī tv āryeti pitur nāmnā sutasya vā ।। tāta-pādā iti pitā mātāmbeti sutena tu । jyeṣṭhās tv āryā iti bhrātrā tathā syur mātulādayaḥ ।। sadṛśaḥ sadṛśo vācyo vayasyety āhvayena vā ।
haleti sakhyā tu sakhī kathanīyā sakhīti vā ।। suta-śiṣya-kanīyāṃso vācyā guru-janena hi । vatsa-putraka-dīrghāyus-tāta-jāteti saṃjñayā ।। anyaḥ kanīyān āryeṇa janena paribhāṣyate ।
śilpādhikāra-nāmabhyāṃ bhadra bhadra-mukheti ।। vācye nīcātinīce tu haṇḍe hañje iti kramāt । bhartrā vācyāḥ sva-sva-nāmnā bhṛtyāḥ śilpocitena vā ।। evam ādi prakāreṇa yojyā nirdeśa-yojanā ।
loka-śāstrāvirodhena vijñeyā kāvya-kovidaiḥ ।। anukta-nāmnaḥ prakhyāte kañcuki-prabhṛter api । itivṛtte kalpite tu nāyakāder api sphuṭam ।। rasa-vastūpayogīni kavir nāmāni kalpayet ।
vinayandhara-bābhravya-jayandhara-jayādikam ।। kāryaṃ kañcukināṃ nāma prāyo viśvāsa-sūcakam । latālaṅkāra-puṣpādi-vastūnāṃ lalitātmanām ।। nāmabhir guṇa-siddhair ceṭīnāṃ nāma kalpayet ।
karabhaḥ kalahaṃsaś cety ādi nāmānujīvinām ।। karpūra-caṇḍa-kāmpilyety ādikaṃ nāma vandinām । subuddhi-vasubhūtyādi-mantriṇāṃ nāma kalpayet ।। devarātaḥ somarāta iti nāma purodhasaḥ ।
śrīvatso gautamaḥ kautso gārgyo maudgalya ity api ।। vasantakaḥ kāpileya ity ākhyeyo vidūṣakaḥ । pratāpa-vīra-vijaya-māna-vikrama-sāhasaiḥ ।। vasanta-bhūṣaṇottaṃsa-śekharāṅka-padottaraiḥ ।
dhīrottarāṇāṃ netṝṇāṃ nāma kurvīta kovidaḥ ।। candrāpīḍaḥ kāmapāla ity ādyaṃ lalitātmanām । ugravarmā caṇḍasena ity ādy-uddhata-cetasām ।। datta-senānta-nāmāni vaiśyānāṃ kalpayet sudhīḥ ।
karpūra-mañjarī candralekhā rāgataraṅgikā ।। padmāvatīti prāyeṇa nāmnā vācyā hi nāyikā । devyas tu dhāriṇī-lakṣmī-vasumatyādi-nāmabhiḥ ।। bhogavatī kāntimatī kamalā kāmavallarī ।
irāvatī haṃsapadīty ādi-nāmnā tu bhoginī ।। viprakṣatra-viśaḥ śarma-varma-dattānta-nāmabhiḥ । śikhaṇḍāṅgada-cūḍānta-nāmnā vidyādharādhipāḥ ।। kuṇḍalānanda-ghaṇṭānta-nāmnā kāpālikā janāḥ ।
yogasundarikā vaṃśaprabhā vikaṭamudrikā ।। śaṅkha-keyūrikety ādi-nāmnā kāpālika-striyaḥ । ānandinī siddhimatī śrīmatī sarvamaṅgalā ।। yaśovatī putravatīty ādi-nāmnā suvāsinī ।
ity ādi sarvam ālocya lakṣaṇaṃ kṛta-buddhinā ।। kavinā kalpitaṃ kāvyam ācandrārkaṃ prakāśate । lakṣya-lakṣaṇa-nirmāṇa-vijñāna-kṛta-buddhibhiḥ ।। parīkṣyatām ayaṃ grantho vimatsara-manīṣayā ।
bharatāgama-pārīṇaḥ śrīmān siṃha-mahīpatiḥ । rasikaḥ kṛtavān evaṃ rasārṇava-sudhākaram ।। niḥsāṇeṣu dhaṇaṃ dhaṇaṃ dhaṇam iti dhvānānusandhāyiṣu । bhrāntiṃ yānti tṛṇaṃ tṛṇaṃ tṛṇam iti pratyarthi-pṛthvī-bhujaḥ ।।
sṛṣṭe tatrātigurvyāṃ tad-upanidhitayā sthāpyamānaiḥ krameṇa । ūrdhvaṃ nītā laghimnā tad-ari-kula-śataiḥ pūryate' dyāpi sā dyauḥ ।। ।। jīyād dharir muni-cakora-suśāradenduḥ ।
saṃlipta-nirmala-viśāla-bhujāntarālaḥ ।। taruṇa-śiśira-raśmir yat suhṛt-puṇya-kīrtiḥ । sa jayatu rasikaughair vanditaḥ pañcabāṇaḥ ।। aśeṣāṇāṃ dvijanuṣām āśīrvāda-paramparā ।
taraṅgayatu kalyāṇaṃ kavīnāṃ cāyur āyatam ।।
